ba ni ma byung ngo / / de ltar dpal ldan sa skya pa'i rigs rus cho 'brang chos srid kyi ngang tshul 'di la dpags na/ g.yung po'i rigs can gyi dregs ldan mtha' dag pha
wang nam 'phang spyod pa'i tshul ltar nges pas/ mi shes gdol pa'i phrug gu 'phongs pa yi/ / 'khor gyis bteg la 'jig rten 'dren pa zhes/ / smig sgyu 'bab chur sgrog pa'i
grags stong sgras/ / 'jig rten yangs mor byed dang 'di mi mtshungs/ / zhes chos rje dkon cog lhun grub gsung ba yang dag pa'i gtam mo/ / smras pa/gser ldan lto ba 'khod snyoms
lus phra mchog gi bzhin ras ngos yangs par//rigs rus nags klung stug po'i 'khri shing mig sman g.yo ba'i gar bsgyur dbus//'khon rigs sA la'i ljon pa'i dbang po ma 'dres
'khyug pa'i zur mig can//chos srid 'bras bu'i khur gyis dud pa'i mdzes sdug rnam 'gyur ci yang bkra//

e ma rtsod dus gser 'khor can//sa la rgyu ba'i gnam gyi sras//gang gi lung bzhin bod 'bangs gtsug/bde 'byung ral pa'i zla tshes ltar//mdzes byed rgyan du spud pa'i dpyid//bstan
pa'i bdag po sa skya pa'i//gdung rabs ha la'i ka la sha/blo gsal bde 'byung mgrin par mdzes//de yang mon gor rgyal pos 'bri gung pa/ se chen rgyal pos tshal pa/ hu la
hus phag mo gru pa rnams so sor mchod gnas su bzung ste/ bod rnams rgyal po so sos ris su bcad de bdag po mdzad pa rnams mchod gnas so sor sbyar ba'i mon lug mgo steng
tshun chad/ gnyal stod smad/ gru shul/ lo ro dkar nag byar po/ e che ba'i nang nas e chung / thang po che/ 'phyong rgyas/ 'phyos/ mon mkhar/ mkhar ltag do bo/ sregs lte/
'on sna/ nam zhal lnga/ bsam yas shar sgo gdong man chad dang / lho brag shar nas/ mchod sde/ ba zhi bod 'brog gnyis/ mnga' ris nas ko ron mdo yan chad/ spu rig la rtsa man
chad rnams rgyal po hu la hur gtogs pa'i don gyi phag mo gru pa'i 'og tu yod pa dper mtshon te 'bri gung dang tshal pa rnams la yang de dang dod mtshungs pa yod pa'i dbang
gis/ g.ya' bzang ba khri bskor gyi kha grangs su bgrangs kyang don du phag mo gru pa'i 'og tu gnas pa ltar/ sna dkar rtse pa 'bri gung pa'i 'og dang / des mtshon khri
dpon gzhan rnams phag 'bri tshal gsum la chos srid gnyis ka'i sgo nas 'gran par mi nus pas 'di gsum khri

dpon rnams kyi nang nas mngon par mtho ba yin no//! de yang tshal pa ni zhang 'gro ba'i mgon po'i rnam par dkar ba'i 'phrin las kyi gdugs dkar po dbyig 'dzin gyi khyon kun
khyab pa las brgyud de khri dpon du gyur pa yin pas/ lha dbang brgya byin gyi sprul par grags pa nye gnas dar ma gzhon nus/ 'gro mgon rin po che'i thugs sras mdzad de/ gung
thang gi gtsug lag khang brtsig pa'i zhabs tog phun sum tshogs pa bsgrubs/ 'gro mgon gshegs khar sde gtsug lag khang gnyis kyi bdag por bskor te/ phyi'i khyams smad dang
mgon khang / nang du gdung rten bkra shis 'od 'bar dang / sku 'bum chen mo'i 'phro sogs grub par mdzad/ de'i rus dbon 'byung gnas brtson 'grus kyis dpon gyi go sa bzung
nas lugs zung gi bya ba mi dman pa 'ga' zhig byas shing / de'i dbo na ye shes 'byung gnas kyis sring mo bzhi bu brgyad du grags pa'i skyid smad kyi yul grong mang po mnga'
'og tu chugde rjes dpon sangs rgyas dngos grub ni gnam gyi mthongs nas mi yul du babs pas/ mgar tshe nam tsha 'brug de nas mgar bla ma mkhyen chen po/ mgar stong mes
khri chags/ de'i sras mgar stong btsan yul bzung gis chos rgyal srong btsan sgam po'i blon po mdzad/ lugs gnyis kyi mdzad pas rje'i zhabs tog dang bod 'bangs la bka' drin
che/ de'i sras btsan po yon tan rgyal bzung / de nas rim bzhin lha gcig snyan ldem bu/ khri zangs dum bu/ khri gnyer khri lcags/ de'i sras stong mes khris snang / khri sto
ro stag gzung / blon chen chas pa sgo drug de'i sras rmu bza' dang 'phags gzigs/ de nas rim bzhin mgar thog yang rgyal/ rgyal le/ mgar rgyal ba 'byung gnas/ 'di dang zhang
rin po che mchod yon du gyur te/ sras phun sum tshogs pa 'byung ba'i lung bstan dang mthun par dpon sangs rgyas dngos grub 'khrungs pa dpon

du bskos/ dge 'dun tshal pa'i bstan pa'i rtsa ba btsugs/ de'i sras dpon chen rin rgyal gyis dpon gyi las ka bzung ste gong du byon/ se chen rgyal pos skyid shod stod smad/
stod lung / gra dol/ 'phyong po/ rgyal sman/ e dwags gnyal gsum sogs lha khang zhig gsos byed pa'i mi sde shes su chug gi 'ja' sa gnang / gung thang du byon te gzims khang
shar dang khyams gra chen mo brtsigs/ 'di la sras gsum las che ba nyi ma shes rab kyis 'gro mgon 'phags pa'i phyag phyir gong du byon te 'ja' sa blangs/ gnyis pa dpon dga'
bde mgon po bya rog gdong can gyi sprul par grags shing / tshal pa'i dgon sde'i don du gong ma'i drung du lan bdun byon/ mi chen zam kha lha pa'i nye gnas 'dam ring gi
gzhan dbang du gyur te/ dpon dga' bde la rtsa ra mang du byas pas/ lkog tu rgyal por zhus par gong ma'i na bza' 'brug sder lnga pa zhig gnang ba de 'og tu gyon skabs/ zam
khas khrims rar khrid de stod gos bshus pas/ rgyal po'i na bza' 'dug pa mthong ste zam kha 'jigs/ mi ring bar zam kha la nag phog pas/ dga' bdes snying tshim gyi chang
drangs nas/nged rang gnyis po khyad par che//nga ni dge 'dun tshal pa yin//dga' bde dpal//blo bde dpal//skyid pa'i dpal//da lta tshal pa'i dga' bde dpal/ / zhes glu blangs
skad/de nas rgya'i bzo bo mkhas pa dang bcas te/ bar khang / rgya phibs/ gser 'phru sogs rten dang brten par bcas pa mtha' dag phul du byung ba'i

bkod pas khyad par du 'phags pa bzhengs/ chos 'khor gling btab nas mtshan nyid kyi bshad grwa dang / dbus gling du sngags grwa 'dzugs pa sogs rnam dkar gyi mdzad pa rgya chen
pos gong ma shin tu dgyes/ 'di'i gcung po rin cen dbang phyug rab tu byung / dga' bde'i sras gnyis las che ba rin cen seng ge/ chung ba smon lam rdo rje/ 'di nyid kyis
lha sa'i bar skor dang / brag lha klu sbug gi rgya phibs/ jo bo dang thugs rje chen po gnyis kyi dbu thog tu gser thog 'bum mo che'i ganydzi ra/ bka' 'gyur dang / dbus gling
'od gsal 'phrul gyi lha khang bzhengs pa sogs/ dkar phyogs kyi mdzad pa bla na ma mchis pa mang zhing / srid kyi mnga' thang lnga kun gsal gyi 'gram pa la reg pa lta
bur gyur/ 'di'i sras che ba dpon kun dga' rdo rje yab mes kyi chos dang rig pa'i gnas thams cad la mkhyen pa mchog tu yangs shing / gong nas phyir byon te/ sku gsung thugs
kyi rten dang ri bo dge 'phel 'debs pa sogs chos srid kyi mdzad pa mi dman pa mtha' yas/ slar yang khri dpon gyi las ka gcung po grags pa shes rab la gtad de rab tu byung
ba'i mtshan drung chen thams cad mkhyen pa dge ba'i blo gros su grags/ mkhas pa'i dbang po bu ston rin po che tshal du bka' 'gyur gyi rab gnas la gdan drangs skabs/ tshal
pa dpon po'i kha ya byed dgos pas rang dgar phyin na mi yongs gsungs nas/ phyag dpe mang po bsnams te lam du gzigs skad/ chos rje bsod grags pas/ chos 'khor gling drung
chen smon lam rdo rjes btab pa dang / si tu dge ba'i blo gros dang drung chen kun dga' rdo rje so sor 'dren pa sogs ni yig tshang gi zhib cha ma nges pa'i 'ol tshod kyi
gtam ste/ 'di dag la 'dris pa chung ba'i dbus su wa skyes rgyal po'i rnam thar 'dzin pa'i tshul yin mchis na'ang / deb ther la 'dris pa rnams kyis brtags tshe bzhad gad
kyi gnas so//

drung chen kun dga' rdo rje'i sras si tu dge legs bzang po/ de la sras tre hos dpal 'byor bzang po/ legs pa rgyal mtshan/ legs ldan bzang po dang gsum gyi dang po'i sras tre
hos dga' bde bzang po dang dngos grub rgyal mtshan gnyis 'khrungs/ gdung brgyud rim par byon pa de dag thams cad kyang gong ma'i lung dang las kas mngon par mtho zhing
/ chos dang srid kyi mdzad pa mi dman pa sha stag tu byon/ 'on kyang dpon kun dga' rdo rjes/ sa skya'i dpon chen rgyal ba bzang po/ dbang brtson/ g.ya' bzang pa sogs dang
bsdongs te/ sde srid phag mo gru pa la ngan bshoms mang du byas pas/ 'dab chags phal gyis mkha' lding gi rjes su snyeg pa rang nyid ngal ba'i rgyur 'gro ba bzhin du sngar
dpon dga' bde dang / drung chen smon lam pa'i dus mtha' sgyur ba'i gong ma'i 'ja' sa'i nang gi 'bangs ni phal cher shor ro//! dpal phag mo gru pa'i 'phrin las kyi rgyun
las/ sgrub brgyud kyi bstan pa rin po che'i dgon gnas slob rgyun dar rgyas su spel bar mdzad pa po ni skyu ra rin po che yin la/ gdan rabs bzhi tsam gyi bar du dam pa'i
chos kho na don du gnyer ba las/ 'jig rten gyi stobs dang gong ma'i lag rtags sogs med 'dug pas/ si tu rin po che'i bka' chems deb ther las/ de dus kyi bla ma de spyan snga
rin po che yin/ sgom pa shAka rin yin te dam kha ma theb rjes tsam yang khyed bla dpon la med/ rgyal po'i bla ma ti shri yang ma byas gsungs pa ltar yin la/ de yang bstan
pa snga dar gyi dus skyu ra'i rig sngags 'chang ba zhig la mkha' 'gro'i rigs can gyi sna nam bza' bya ba'i jo mo zhig blangs pa mi las 'das pa'i sprul sgyur sna tshogs
ston pa zhig byung ba/ deng sang 'bri gung a phyir 'bod pa 'di yin la/ de gnyis kyi sras la nam mkha' dbang phyug gi brgyud las a mes dbang rgyal gyi sras bzhi pa rdo rje
la jo mo rje btsun ma bya ba blangs

pa'i sras su 'bri gung rin po che 'khrungs te 'gro mgon rin po che'i drung du zab rgyas kyi chos bum pa gang byo'i tshul du gsan cing mtshan rin cen dpal du grags/ 'gro mgon
gshegs rjes zhang sum thog pa'i mjug tu gdan sa mdzad kyang 'phrin las bzhed pa bzhin ma byung bas byang phyogs su byon nas rtogs ldan mi nyag sgom rin gyi dgon pa nye
gnas kyis phul bar phyag phab ste dar rgyas su mdzad pas 'bri gung thel zhes gangs ri'i khrod kyi sgrub brgyud pa'i gtsug na mngon par mtho ba byung zhing /skyob pa rin po
che'i khu bo dkon cog rin cen gyi sras a mes grags rgyal/ de la sras mched gsum las che ba dbon rin po che/ 'bring dbon brgyud rdo rje seng ge/ chung ba gcung rin po che
rdo rje grags pa las/ gcung rin po che ti li pa'i sprul par grags shing / 'di'i dus su sgom pa la khri dpon gyi 'ja' sa lon te/ byar dgas tshun lung gis mnga' sgyur bas
stobs 'byor gyi longs spyod shin tu che/ de dag la bsams nas phyis su gong ma si tu rin po che la 'bri gung sgom pas/ da lta sa skya pas bdag byed pa 'di sngon nged 'bri
gung pas byed par snang zer ba'i khengs dregs kyi gtam smras skad/ 'on kyang sgom pa gsum bzhi'i ring la sa skya pa dang ma mthun pas/ 'bring po'i sras thog kha pa rin cen
seng ge dang spyan snga mtshams bcad pa'i rjes su gnubs gdan sar bzhugs thog gling log chen po de byung skabs 'du khang la me brgyab pas dge 'dun khri tsho tsam gnam g.yang
nas mkha' la 'phur zer/ zhal ngo kong por bros/ mnga' thang yang cung zad bri/de rjes rdo rje rin cen/ rdo rje rgyal po/ nyer gnyis rin po che/ don grub rgyal po rnams
rim par byon te spyan snga'i go sa dang sgrub brgyud kyi bstan pa spel ba kho na las/ 'jig rten gyi srid 'dzin pa ni sa skya'i dpon chen gyi dod

po lta bu 'bri gung gi sgom pa yin pas/ de dag gi go rim ni/ sgom pa rdo rje seng ge/ shAkya rin cen/ byang she/ byang chub/ spang ras/ chos seng / rin cen seng ge/ sgom pa
dpon po/ sgom pa shAkya dar/ rin cen grags/ ye shes dpal/ 'di grongs pa'i dus si tu rin po che 'bri gung du 'phrad mo la byon/ bkra shis ljongs su rin po che dang mjal/
si tu rin po ches kyang rin cen rdo rje sgom pa che ba la bskos/ kun rin chung ba la bskos na legs pa'i rgyu mtshan phul ba bzhin mdzad/ de nas rin rdor 'das rjes kun rin
la gong ma'i lung med na'ang / dbus gtsang swon wi si pa rnams kyis khyon bskos byas/ spyir gdan sa phan tshun gnyis zung 'brel yin pa dang / khyad par sgom pa rang la si
tu bka' drin che bar/ slob dpon kun rin gyis sde srid phag mo gru pa la ngan bshoms kyi gra sgrig 'ga' zhig byas pa la brten/ 'bri gung gi srid la phan pa che ba ma byung
/de rjes shAkya bzang pos sgom pa'i las ka bzung / de nas rdzong ji bsod rin dang sku zhang tshul rgyal sogs kyis srid 'dzin pa'i srol byung 'dug na'ang / chos rgyal rin
cen dpal bzang gi thog bla dpon sbrags te chos srid kyi lung bzang po yongs su bzung / sras gnyis 'khrungs pa'i chung ba bco lnga rin po che chos srid kyis mngon par mtho
ba'i go sar byon/ sras gsum byung ba'i che ba phag mor byon/ 'bring po chos rje kun dga' rin cen gdan sar bzhugs/ 'di'i dus zhal ngo nang mtshams ma mthun pa dang / snga
thog 'bri gung pa dang dga' ldan pa gnyis lugs gnyis kyi 'brel zab pa'i mu can du yod na'ang / 'di nyid kyi 'bri gung mnga' 'og na yod pa'i dge lugs kyi dgon pa rnams
kyi zhwa bsgyur ba dang / dgon pa gzhan la'ang dpung gyi sbyor ba bshams pa sogs sde 'khrug kho nas dus 'da' bas/ 'bri gung bka' brgyud kyi bstan pa la phan

pa cher ma byung ba'i ngang du grongs/ gcung chos kyi rgyal pos spu lung bzung ba'i sras dbon rin cen phun tshogs ni rgya bod kyi mkhas grub 'ga' zhig gi skye ba gsal bar dran
zhing gdan sar byon/ ratna'i ming can 'gro ba'i kha lo sgyur/ / zhes pa'i lung bstan dang mthun par mnga' thang gong du 'phel/ 'di'i rjes su phag mo nas dbon rin po che
gdan sar byon/ thog kha nang sos kong dmag drangs/ 'bri gtsang srid du bsgril ba dang / gong ma sde srid la 'bangs gyen log gi rnam pa mdzad pa la brten dus mi bde ba
mang du byung / de rjes zur pa'i sras rje chos rgyal phun tshogs rgyal po gtsug lag 'dzin gyi sprul par grags shing / de la sras rje bkra shis phun tshogs rje drung dkon
cog yan lag gi sprul sku/ rje dkon cog rin cen/ rje dkon cog phun tshogs bzhi las/ da lta chos rje rin po che dkon cog phun tshogs gdan sar bzhugs te chos srid kyi mnga'
thang gi rgyun gnas so//! de ltar gong du smos pa bzhin khri skor gzhan rnams kyis 'bri gung dang tshal pa'i mnga' thang dpal 'byor la 'gran par mi nus na'ang / sna dkar
rtse pas 'brog khri dpon gyi lung dang lag rtags lon zhing / 'bri gung du gling log gtong ba'i sa skya'i dpon chen ang len zhes mgon po gur gyi sprul par grags pa'i dpa'
rtags kyi grags snyan can de yang 'di'i zhal ngo yin/ sde pa bstan 'dzin pa'i dus rin po che las grub pa'i bde bar gshegs pa'i mchod rten brgyad las/ rten 'brel gyi sgo nas
myang 'das mchod rten gyi tshab tu mchod rdzas kyi rim pa bzheng ba sogs rnam dkar gyi dge las che zhing / yar 'brog stag lung gi btsan rdzong yang 'di nyid kyi dus bslangs
pas chos srid gnyis ka nas grags che/ gtso bor dpal ldan sa skya pa dang / chos rje bo dong pa'i bstan pa la phu dud ma dmad pa mdzad/ grub mtha' gzhan dag la'ang kun
slong

skyon can gyi sbyor ba mi rtsom pas mtshan jus brtan chags shing / zhal ngo rim par byon pa rnams mkhyen sgo yangs pa dang thabs mkhas kyi mdzad pas deng sang sa skyong kun
dga' dbang chen phun tshogs mched kyi bar du chab srid la 'pho 'gyur med par yod do//! byang pa bdag po ni phun sum tshogs pa'i bsod nams kyi dpal las grub pa'i dbang phyogs
rgya nag gong ma'i khri la gnam gyi lung gis dbang sgyur ba mi nyag si'u rgyal po nas gdung rabs bdun pa mi nyag rgyal rgod las rim par brgyud pa'i rigs las mi nyag
sengge dar/ de'i sras rdo rje dpal gyi rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi zhabs la gtugs nas/ dpal sa skya pa dang 'brel ba'i 'go tshugs/ de'i sras dkon cog de la sras gsum
las/ 'bum sdes chos rje sa paN la gus 'dud lhur mdzad/ 'di la sras drug las grags pa dar gyis gong ma se chen rgyal po'i lung bzhin rin po che'i dam kha dang si tu'i
las ka blangs/ byang ngam ring gi chos sde chen po btsugs/ dpon chen grags pa dar ming gzhan yon btsun zhes grags snyan can de'i sras rdo rje mgon pos yab mes kyi srol bzhin
sa skya'i dpon chen gyi las ka bzung / tshogs sde bzhi la bkur sti bla lhag tu mdzad/de la sras drug las/ nam mkha' brtan pas gong sar byon nas stag mgo nor bu gsum pa
gu'i gung gi mtshan shel gyi tho shu rnams gnang / slar ta dben gu shri ming dang shel gyi dam kha blangs/ dpal ldan sa skya dang ngam ring gis gtsos pa'i chos sde rnams
su bsnyen bkur sogs lugs gnyis kyi mdzad pa bzang / de la sras rin cen rgyal mtshan dang / nam mkha' rin cen gnyis las/ gcen gyis yab kyi chen po'i las ka rnams blangs/
spyan ras gzigs kyi sprul par grags/ 'di'i sras snga tshar gu'i gung chos grags dpal bzang

gis si tu chang gu'i las ka blangs/ sras phyi tshar zla ba rgyal mtshan/ 'khon ston bsod nams pa'i yum rnams 'khrungs/ gcung 'jam dbyangs pa rje btsun sa paN gyi dus su 'khor
du skyes pa dran/ shes bya'i gnas la blo gros kyi 'jug pa mchog tu yangs shing / kwa ding gu shri'i las ka bzung / yab dang gcen gyi bka' bzhin rab byung gi bslab pa phul/
sras lcam sring gsum 'khrungs/gu'i gung chos grags pa'i sras che ba bdag chen rnam rgyal grags bzang gis ta'i si tu'i las ka dang / gcung dkon cog legs pas shri'i zi'i
dre hos kyi las ka bzung ste srid kyi 'byor ba shin tu che/ khyad par gcen gyi lo chen byang chub rtse mo sogs dam pa du ma'i gsung gi bdud rtsi myang / rgya gar rdo rje
gdan gyi mkhan po shA ri pu tra dang / bo dong phyogs las rnam rgyal ba la zab rgyas kyi chos mang du gsan/ khyad par dpal dus kyi 'khor lo la mkhas pa'i phul du phyin
pas/ mkhas pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan dang / mi nyag chos grags bzang po sogs kyis/ chos rgyal 'di nyid kyi zhabs la gtugs nas/ dus 'khor gyi rgyud 'grel gsan/ rtses thang
pa sangs rgyas lhun grub kyis rigs ldan 'di nyid kyi drung du dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud 'grel mthar phyin par gsan nas/ slar dbus su paN chen byams pa gling pa'i drung du
rig gnas kyi thugs sbyong mdzad pa'i skabs/ bdag chen 'di nyid kyis legs par bshad pa'i dus 'khor gyi gsung gleng byung bas thugs ha las te/ nyid kyi gsung 'di ltar na nged
kyis sngar brtsams pa rnams la yang bcos byed dgos par 'dug gsungs skad/ mdor na dbus gtsang mtha' dag tu zur gnas rnams/ rigs ldan padma dkar po slar byon pa yin zhes
gleng zhing / gzhan yang theg pa che chung gi gsung rab mtha' dag la mkhyen spyan yangs pas/ skabs shig dus bzhi cig car ba dang rim gyis pa'i skor la bdag chen nyid kyis
na bza' ber gyi phu dung

brdzes te thal 'gyur 'phen pa sogs mkhas pa rnams spa bkong bar mdzad/ dus kyi 'khor lo'i dgongs 'grel dang / 'jig rten mes po'i gtsug lag mi mthun pa'i nad kyi rtsa ba drungs
nas dbyung bar byed pa'i gso ba rig pa'i gzhung lugs kun gyi yang snying rje btsun g.yu thog pa chen po'i ring lugs gsal bar byed pa'i bstan bcos/ log smra tshar gcod
pa sgra rig pa'i bstan bcos kyi nying khu ka lA pa'i mdo rgyan/ bzo rig pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gzugs kyi phyag tshad/ bstan pa'i gnas tshad/ gsang ba sngags kyi lha'i
sgrub thabs kyi rim pa/ ma 'ongs mngon sum gsal bar ston pa gtsug lag rtsis kyi skor/ mkhas grub chos rje'i rtsod lan sogs legs par bshad pa'i rtsom pa'i rigs ji snyed
cig mchis shing / dus kyi 'khor lo'i blos slangs sogs sku gsung thugs kyi rten bzheng mang du mdzad/ mnal lam du slob dpon chen po zhal gzigs pa dang rje sa chen la thugs
dad shugs drag po 'khrungs pas sa chen dbu gtsug nas thim pa'i snang ba sogs rtogs pa'i yon tan kyang mtha' yas shing rig pa'i gnas mtha' dag la mkhyen pa'i spyan yangs
pas rgyal po paNDi ta zhes snyan pa'i rgyud kyis rgya gar mkhas pa'i khengs dregs kyi gzhu yongs su 'gugs shing / rin po che'i rgyan sogs mi chen gyi cha lugs dang ldan
bzhin du sa dge'i mtshan nyid kyi slob dpon mkhas pa rnams la gsung rab mtha' dag brgal brtag gis gtan la 'bebs pa'i bgro gleng mdzad pa sogs 'chad rtsod rtsom pas dus 'da'
bas spyir yang ngo mtshar che/ khyad par 'gro ba'i 'dren par rlom pa'i dregs ldan chos smra ba'i lce mdud pa brgya phrag gis bcings pa rnams kyi snang tshul la dpags na
rjes su yi rang ngo //de rjes nam mkha' tshe dbang rdo rje/ de'i sras nam mkha' rin cen bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ kun dga' legs pa gsum las 'bring po rab tu

byung / chung ba lho byang yongs la mnga' sgyur/ dpa' gtum gyi grags che/ mched gsum gyi rigs las nam mkha'i rgyal mtshan kun dga' rin cen/ bkra shis stobs rgyas dbang po'i
sde sogs 'khrungs pa las/ 'di nyid slob dpon chen po'i zab chos kyi bdag por bka' babs so// smras pa/'od gsal 'chi med lam las babs pa'i 'khon gyi brgyud pa rin po che//shar
phyogs gong ma'i rgyal mtshan rtser mchod chen po'i las ka 'dod rgu'i char//'dzam gling khyon kun mngon par snyil ba'i mu thi la yi kArNi ka/rin cen nyams 'gyur phra
tshoms kyis mdzes ya rabs mdun sa'i rgyan du spel//g.yung po'i lugs min rigs rus cho 'brang ldan//gong ma'i lung 'dzin srid kyis mngon mtho'i mkhar//rnam dkar zla shel dri
med zil mngar can//bde skyid kunda dga' ba'i grogs su 'dzag/ kha bas bskor ba'i ljongs chen po 'di nyid du dpal dwags po'i bka' brgyud kyi bstan pa nags klung stug po'i
dbus su dpag bsam yongs 'du'i ljon pa lta bu ni dpal phag mo gru pa rdo rje rgyal po zhes dbang po

tha mal pa rtsod dus kyi gdul bya'i snang ngor rim gyis sbyangs pa'i sar gnas kyi sems dpa'i tshul 'dzin cing / dbang po yang rab la dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas yin par zhal gyis
bzhes pa'i snyan grags lha yi rdza rnga sgrub rgyud rnam par rgyal ba'i khang bzang gi rtse mor brdungs pas me tog mda' can lha min gyi tshogs mtha' dag brnag nus las
'das te phun sum tshogs pa'i legs byas kyi bdud rtsir spyod pa la nyer 'tshe'i bsam pa ring du gtong ba'i byed po theg pa chen po'i glang chen sa la rab brtan gyi steng
du rnam par 'gying zhing / ye shes 'dren byed stong gis ji lta ji snyed kyi chos mtha' dag rjen par 'char ba kun stong chen phyag rgya gcig gi rgyas thebs pa'i rdo rje rtse
brgya pas bdag 'dzin ri bo'i bgrod pa ming gi lhag mar btang ba'i skyes mchog mchod sbyin brgya pa 'di nyid kyi bka' brgyud yin la/de yang chos srid kyi 'byor pa bla na
med pa'i sgo nas yar ldan du spel ba ni rje spyan snga rin po che dang / gong ma ta'i si tu sogs dpal ldan rlangs kyi gdung las rim par byon pa rnams yin pas/ rlangs kyi
po ti bse ru las/ lar skyes pa'i mis rang gi skye brgyud ma shes na nags khung gi spre'u dang 'dra/ mi rang gi cho 'brang ma shes na g.yu 'brug zol ma dang 'dra/ yab mes
kyi che ge'i yig tshang ma shes na/ mon phrug yal bor dang 'dra zhes dang / skyes pa'i mi la grags pa'i gtam dgos/ byas pa'i chos la grub pa'i mtha' dgos/ che ba'i mi la
mtho ba'i rtags dgos zhes gsungs pa ltar/ bod gsil bur ma song ba'i snga rabs kyi dus rje 'bangs mtha' dag rigs rus 'chol bar mi spyod pas khungs dang yig tshang la nan
tan du byed pa'i srol 'dug cing / deng sang ni 'di rigs kyi rgyu mtshan mang du smra ba/ sprel rgan rnams kyis mi bzung nas/ / mjug ma med ces bzhad gad byed/ / ces pa'i
tshul lta bur 'gro bar

gda' na'ang gong gi 'phros las 'di nyid cung zad brjod na/po ti bse ru las/ 'bangs kyi mi rabs la/ 'byung ba sna lnga'i snying po la/ sgo nga chen po gcig yongs pa/ phyi'i
sgong shun la lha brag dkar po chags/ nang gi sgong chu la dung mtsho dkar mer 'khyil/ bar gyi sgo nga'i dar cha la/ / rigs drug sems can kun tu grol/ / sgo nga 'phrum gyi
bco brgyad chags/ / sgo nga bco brgyad 'bring po de/ / dung sgong gcig tu yar nas byung // zhes bshad pa ltar/ dung gi sgo nga de la dbang po lnga dang yan lag rnams so
sor dod de mtshar sdug gi khye'u yid la smon pa lta bu zhig byung bas ming ye smon rgyal por btags/ de'i jo mo chu lcag rgyal mo la/ 'phrul sras dbang ldan 'khrungs/ des
dung bza' dngul mo blangs pa la/ kwo sras skyes gcig 'khrungs/ de'i sras mi rabs mched gsum las/ chung ba stag tshal 'al 'ol gyi jo mo 'tshams bza' khyad khyud la sras mgur
lha mched bzhi byung / chung ba'i sras yab lha sde drug gi chung ba 'o de gung rgyal gyi jo mo lha mo la/ lha tsha mched dgu byung / jo mo gnyan mo la gnyan tsha mched
dgu/ jo mo rmus mo la/ rmu tsha mched dgu/ jo mo klu bza' la klu tsha mched brgyad byung / kun bsgril bas sras sum cu rtsa lnga byung / de rnams kyi chung ba sne khrom
lag khra'i jo mo lha lcam la/ la kha rgyal po 'khrungs/ de'i jo mo lung kha hril mo la sras gsum gyi che ba mthing gi/ de'i jo mo lha lcam dkar mo la sras bod 'jongs la brang
gi rmu bza' mthing bsgril khab tu bzhes par rgya khri la zhang 'khrungs/ de la sras rgyal po che chung gsum/ brgyud brgyad yod pa las/ chung ba'i jo mo mthing mo la
sras gsum byung ba'i khri rje gnyan thang gi sras dpal lha/ de'i sras a mi mu zi khri do'i jo mo gnyan bza' sha mig la sras gsum dang / rmu bza' la sras gcig sren bza' la
sras gnyis te drug byung

la/ 'di dag las mched pa rus chen bco brgyad/ 'bras la dkar nag khra gsum sogs dang / bod mi'u gdung drug byung tshul shin tu mang zhing / stod kyi 'bras dkar mched dgu la/
/ bal po dang bal yo bal srid gsum/ / ma stong bal stong con stong drug / mar ba dang zhang chung pu rangs dgu/ / zhes sogs dbye ba shin tu mang zhing / bse khyung 'bras
kyi jo mo btsan bza' dge ldan ma'i sras/ 'bras khra bo/ de'i jo mo srun bza' khra mo la sras bzhi byung ba'i sa ches hor bza' 'bum mo khab tu bzhes pa la khyung ru dkar
po/ de'i sras 'bram re shel mig de'i sras ar rje gtsug gsum/ de la gnam lha mched brgyad kyi lnga pas sras su sprul pa'i ming mang ldom stag btsan/ de'i jo mo rong bza' khye
lcam la sras ma byung bas thugs ma bde bar lha yul du byon te rang gi gcen rnams la dris par/rang re lha sras mched brgyad kyi//khyed ni mi yi sras su sprul//bu dang
sras med thugs chad na//zla ba bcu gsum sgrub pa mdzod//yi dam sgoms la gsang sngags bgrongs//lo gsar zla ba bcu gsum la//lha ri gnyan po can du byon//bsangs dang mchod pa
gsol ba thob//lha tshangs sras mo 'grub ste 'ong //lha tshangs sras mo 'grub pa na//lha yi sras la mi yi brgyud//rigs brgyud khyad du 'phags pa 'ong //

mi rabs bdun cu rtsa gsum par//bla ma mi dpon rgyun mi chad//sems can kun gyi 'dren pa dang //dpa' bos rgyal khams 'dul ba dang //grags pa sa steng khebs pa 'ong //zhes gsungs
pa dang mthun par mi yul du byon te sgrub pa mdzad/ lo gsar gyi zla ba la lha ri'i rtser byon te mchod pa mdzad pas nam mkha' las 'ja' tshon sna lnga pa byung zhing bar
snang la rol mo'i sgra sogs cho 'phrul sna tshogs byung bas/ tshangs sras lha mo 'khor brgyad dang bcas pa byon par gzigs te/ chung ma mdzad par gsol ba bzhin 'khor rnams
'od du yal/ lha mos zhal gyis bzhes/ rdo rje rnam 'joms kyi khrus chus jo mo'i sku lus bkrus nas yul du byon/ yun ring du song kyang sras ma byung / skabs shig nam mkha'
nas sgra zhig la/ mang ldom stag btsan dmag la byon/ / rgya dmag bod du lhags dogs yod/ rgya dmag bod du lhags pa na/ / khyod min gang gis thub mi 'gyur/ / zhes byung
bas mang ldom gyis chibs ngang dkar g.yu gshog la chibs/ dngul dkar gyi dung khrab dang shel dkar gyi rmog de gyon/ 'od 'bar gyi mtshon btags nas/ nam mkha' la lha dmag
dang chu rgyud la klu dmag rnams 'grim du bcug ste byon pas/ rgya rnams bros te g.yul las rgyal/ skabs der sman btsun gyis lha yul nas khrid pa'i dung gi mdzo mo bros pa
mang ldom gyis bkag sman btsun gyis mdzo mo 'tshol du 'ongs pa gzigs nas/ mdzo mo mi 'gro ba'i phyag rgyas bcings te pha bong gur 'dra'i nang du byon/ sgo bsdams te zur gcig
nas gzigs pas/ sman btsun gyis mdzo mo la 'o ma bzhos pa'i phud kyis dkon cog dang / mang ldom gyi skyabs

lha la mchod pa phul/ lhag ma chu la blug nas/ rigs brgyud khyad 'phags 'byung ba'i smon lam btab pas mang ldom mnyes/ dus der nam mkha' nas/ sprul pa'i lha brgyud spel ran
pas// sang phod dus kyi da tsam na/ / rigs kyi sras bu 'khrung bar 'gyur/ / zer ba'i sgra byung ba dang / mang ldom gyis sman btsun gyi rtsar byon nas gzims/ tho rangs mi
dkar rta dkar du sprul nas/ mched bdun la gsung ba bzhin byas yod/ sras ji ltar 'khrungs zhus pa'i lan du/ mi brgyud lha rabs gsum du yong / / gcig gis bla ma'i brgyud
pa 'dzin/ / sems can kun gyi 'dren pa byed/ / gcig gis bod khams dpon du 'gyur/ / bod khams kun gyi rje byed cing / / gcig gis dpa' ba'i rigs su yong / / zhes gsung / de
nas zla ba bdun rdzogs dus/ nyams sad pa'i phyir du bdag gi sras ma lags zhes lha mo la gsungs pas/ sras 'khrungs khar sman btsun gyis sngar gzims sar byon/ mnal lam du gser
gyi mchod rten rin po ches spras pa la/ bang rim grangs med cing thog mtha' bar gsum la rim bzhin bla ma/ lha'i bu bu mo bsgrigs pa zhig pang du byung ba rmis/ sang sras
'khrungs pa lha ri'i rtser khyer te/ g.yam sgrom gyi nang du sras bzhag nas/ mang ldom gyi sras yin na mi brgyud lha las sra ba dang / min na bya dang gcan gzan gyis
za ba'i smon lam btab/ mi'i dri ma phog pa'i stabs kyis lha gnas su ma thon par yul du log der mang ldom la rgyu mtshan rnams bshad pas/ de ma thag yab yum gnyis kyis lha
ri'i rtser phyin pa na/ khye'u g.yu'i zur phud can spyi gtsug na rlang pa dkar po yod pa gcig la g.yu 'brug gis ngar chu blud/ seng ges nu zho bsnun/ rgod kyis gshog pas
bkab/ gcan gzan ri dwags kyis skor ba byed/ 'ja' tshon gyi gur phub 'dug pa gzigs pas/ yab dgyes te/ rlangs so rlangs so// lan gsum rlangs/ gsungs pas

rlangs kyi gdung brgyud ces ming de nas chags/ 'ga' zhig tu ga gla btags su snang ba ni yig mkhan gyis ma dag pa'i rgyun 'byams par nges so/ /de'i jo mo ldong bza' khri sgron
la sras dpa' bo/ de'i jo mo lcog ro bza' lha gnam gyi sras stong tho/ de'i sras che che/ de'i sras rgod lding / gcen po'i steng du rgod lding ba ltar 'phur bas ming de
ltar chags/ de'i sras stong dge/ de'i sras stong khri/ de'i sras phag tshang / de'i sras ldang ra/ de'i sras gtsug gnyen rdzong khong / de'i sras btsan pa 'dab shong / de'i
sras snang gnyan khong sleb/ de'i sras mang po che sgro kha/ de'i sras stag po che dar dpal/ 'dis ma pham g.yu mtsho'i 'gram du gser gyi shAkya mu ni bzhengs/ g.yu snang
ba 'od ldan yon du phul/ byu ru bkra shis 'od 'bar gyi mchod rdzas byas/ grub thob seng ge rab gnas su gdan drangs pa'i tshe/ sgang bza' lha mo la sras gcig 'khrungs
pa/ grub thob kyis mtsho ni bzang zhing sras 'di lha'i spyan gyis gzigs pa zhig byung bas/ mtsho bzang lha gzigs su thogs gsung / 'di nas bzung ste rlangs lha gzigs su grags/'di'i
sras a mi byang chub 'dre 'khol te/ dgung lo brgyad la o rgyan du byon pa dang / srin po btul nas phyir byon pa'i tshe yi dam gyi lha zhal gzigs pa dang / ge sar
gyis gling yul du lan gnyis gdan drangs pa'i phyi ma'i tshe/ pha bong gwa ba rta 'dra ba la chibs nas phyogs bzhir gdon chen po bzhi btul ba sogs rdzu 'phrul ni mtha' yas
shing / sngar byang chub rdo rje zer yang / phyis lha srin bran du 'khol bas 'dre 'khol du mtshan chags/ slob dpon chen po padmas kyang / byang dang chub ces bya ba yi/
/ mi bu khyad du 'phags pa 'ong / / de ni nga yi thugs kyi sras/ / zhes gsungs shing / byang chub 'dre 'khol nyid kyi gsung du yang / / da nas mi rabs bcu gsum na/

/ bod khams yongs kyi bdag po 'ong / / zhes lung bstan pa/ 'jam dbyangs gong ma rgyal po'i pho brang tshun gyi mchog dman gyi skye bo mtha' dag gi mig dang rna ba'i spyod yul
du gyur pa de ltar yin la/ 'di'i jo mo skal ldan ma la sras dpal gyi sangge/ gnyan thog a khrom/ stag tshab gsum las/ 'bring po gnyan thog a khrom gyi sras gnyan po nya
mog khri/ de'i sras rlangs ston bya zhu nag po/ de'i sras a seng / de'i sras a ser/ de'i sras skyabs bdun dpal dang brgyad/ btsan dang dgu zhes pa'i che ba yon chen rgyal
ba skyabs yin la/ de yang rlangs stod tho yi spyi dpon mdzad/ mgo rum seng ges rgya bcom/ rtse 'thon gyis drag po spun bzhi btul/ ldong sras kyis 'dan yul dbang du bsdus
pa sogs 'jig rten mi chos nas mngon par mtho ba shin tu mang zhing / dam pa'i lha chos kyi sgo nas/ byang chub 'dre 'khol ni gong du smos zin pa dang / de'i sras gsum
gyis dpag par dka' ba'i sprul sgyur mdzad pa dang / rlangs khams pa go chas rab tu byung ba'i sad mi mi bdun gyi bar mar grags/ rlangs dpal gyi sengges slob dpon chen po'i
thugs sras mdzad de grub pa brnyes/ ye shes rdo rjes nyi ma ltong la mnan/ ye shes sengges dpal thang du jag pa btul/ dpal gyi 'byung gnas kyis lha 'dre dam la btags/ dar
ma sengges dur khrod bsil ba tshal du byon/ dpal gyi rdo rjes nyi zer la chos gos bkal ba sogs grub pa brnyes pa'i mthu stobs dang rdzu 'phrul dpag par dka' ba sha stag
tu byon pa yin no// smras pa/'chi ba med pa'i lam las legs 'ongs lha rigs rlangs kyi pad dkar tshal//

mkhas grub ra yig gnyis pa'i tshogs 'du ngo mtshar 'phur lding rol gar can//gsang chen theg pa'i ze'u 'bru rab ldem dngos grub sbrang rtsi'i za ma tog/lo rgyus myangs na zhim
pa'i ro bcud skabs gsum bdag po'i bdud rtsi bzhin//mdo khams yul gyi zla ba'i ma ma las//lha gzigs gdung gi mngon mtho'i bsil zer can//gangs can legs bris lam du 'phags
pa'i tshe//skal bzang skye rgu'i sa smos 'dod pa 'jo//de yang yon chen rgyal ba skyabs la jo mo 'bro ldog bza' dang / de gu ma/ 'bri bza' ye shes mtsho dang gsum las/ dang
po'i sras rje spyan snga rin po che dpon sangs rgyas bskyabs/ dpon shes rab rgyal/ gnyis pa'i sras dpon mgon po rgyal mtshan/ gsum pa'i sras rgyal ba rin po che/ bcu
gnyis pa gter rgyal ba rin cen rdo rje rnams las/rje spyan snga rin po che ni yab mes dang bka' brgyud kyi chos kyis gtso mdzad/ rgyal ba'i gsung rab rgya mtsho lta bu la
thos bsam lhur blangs pas/ sgrub ris yongs kyi bstan pa'i bdag por gyur/ shar rgyal po'i lung gis mthong tshad bsad na thos tshad skrag pa'i las rngam po che gsog pa'i byed
po dor rta nag po yang rdzu 'phrul gyis 'dul bar mdzad pas/ kha ba ri pa rnams la gcig tu bka' drin che/

de rjes rgyal ba rin po che rab tu byung ba'i mtshan grags pa brtson 'grus te/ dbus su phebs nas rje spyan snga rin po ches byin gyis brlabs pas chos thams cad mnyam pa nyid
kyi rtogs pa 'khrungs/ mkhas grub kyi yon tan phul du byon zhing / nam mkha' las thog babs pa sku chos su gtums pas rgyal sras thog rdugs pa zhes nus mthu'i snyan pa che/
gdan sar phebs nas sing gha gling ti ra hu ti ya rtse rgyal po rnams kyis rnam thos kyi bu la 'gran par nus pa'i mkho dgu'i yo byad bsam gyis mi khyab pa phul zhing /
khyad par sog po rbad 'gyel du grags pa'i nor bu sogs nor sna'i rigs kyi mchod rdzas bod yul du gdan sa thel bzang bar grags pa yang 'di'i dus byung / spyan snga rin po che
yan chad du gong ma'i 'ja' sa sogs med 'dug na'ang / 'di nyid kyi dus hu la hur gtogs pa rnams gong ma'i lung gi 'ja' sa dang bcas ldan ma sgom brtson gyis spyi dpon byas
na'ang lugs dang 'brel bar ma byung bas/ dpon rdo rje dpal rkang bzhi'i dpon byed kyin yod pa rgyal ba rin po ches tshur bkug ste khri dpon du bskos/ gong sar lan gsum
byon/ pho brang sgang / tshong 'dus brag kha/ sne'u gdong / sna mo/ ha la sgang / thang po che gling smad/ 'phyos gzhis ka/ mon mkhar bkra shis gdong / rgyal thang / lcags
rtse gri khu/ mchod rten gling / chad dkar te gzhis ka bcu gnyis brtsigs/ mnga' thang shin tu mtho zhing / dpon rang yang mgo la sgom zhwa dang / lus la chos gos rnam
gsum gyon/ btsun tshugs ma dor bas lugs gnyis thad nas kun gyis mtho bzos che/ 'khor rnams kyang 'chun che ba'i stabs kyis drag zhan mtha' dag gis dpon gyis gzigs sar bag
yangs kyi spyod pa byed mi nus skad/ chos rje bsod grags pas/ bcu gnyis rin po che'i dus gong ma'i 'ja' sa byung ba dang / tshes bzhi pa'i dus dpon rdo rje rin cen gyis
khri dpon byas

par smra ba sogs ni yig tshang khungs thub rnams ma gzigs par tshod 'jog tu bris pa'i skyon kho na ste/ lo rgyus rnams ma nges bzhin du 'bri dgos pa mo rtsis pa bzhin gyis
lung bstan byung ba yin na thugs bden par mchis so//'gro mgon rin po che'i sprul pa bcu gnyis rin po che rdo rje ni lung rtogs kyi yon tan mtha' yas shing / gdan sar phebs
nas pu rangs lo chung gi thugs dam dgra nag la gsol ba btab pas lho rgyud kyi 'khrug pa zhi ba dang mngon par mkhyen pa thogs pa med pa sogs rnam thar ya mtshan can mang
zhing / 'di'i dus khri dpon rdo rje dpal grongs nas khong gi gcung gzhon nu rgyal mtshan khri dpon gyi go sar bskos kyang / mgo la smyug zhwa/ lus la hor gos/ rkang pa
la hor lham gyon/ mtshan phyed kyi ring glu len zhing bro brdung / nyin phyed kyi bar nyal ba sogs bag med kyi spyod pa kho nas dus 'da' bas phag mo gru pa'i sde tshugs la
shin tu gnod pa byung / khong 'das rjes lho brag gshong sde mkhan po rin rgyal gong sar btang ste 'ja' sa zhus/ de rjes yar 'brog pa byang gzhon khri dpon du bskos na'ang
sngon ma'i mig ltos kyis bag med kyi spyod pa kho na'i dbang du song //dpon mgon po rgyal la sras rin cen shes rab/ grags pa ye shes/ grags pa rin cen/ rin cen skyabs
dang bzhi las/ grags pa ye shes ni sa skyar 'gro mgon 'phags pa'i drung du 'byon dus mdo sdud pa'i tshod tsam gyi phyag dpe zhogs re la bzung bas mkhyen rab kyis grags pa
che/ gdan sar bzhugs ring 'gro phan gyi sgo mchog tu yangs/ khri dpon byang gzhon gyi rjes su gzhon nu yon tan gyis khri dpon lo drug byas na'ang / chang nag kho na don
du gnyer bas sde'i 'dzin tshugs ma byung /gcung grags pa rin cen thos bsam sgom pa mthar phyin zhing gdan sar

bzhugs thog ti shri grags 'od dang / rgyal po the mur bog gnyis kyi 'ja' sa stag mgo phul/ khri dpon zur du ma bskos par bla dpon sbrags nas mdzad/ do sngon/ rgyal thang /
smon mkhar/ sa 'thon/ byi chung / za ra tho thang / lding gsum/ g.yu sring / mon mkhar sogs gzhon rgyal 'od du dben sha/ dpon chen legs pa dpal/ slob dpon a tsa ra/ dpon
chen a blon/ sa skya pa sogs la shor ba rnams phyag rdzas kyis bslu bar mdzad pas/ phag gru khri bskor la bka' drin shin tu che zhing / de'i don gyi si tu rin po che'i bka'
chems su/ sne'u gdong gi thab mgo 'dzin pa'i gzhis ka ming can 'di rnams zhi bar gshegs pas/ phyag rdzas kyis bslus pa'i gzhis kyang yin cing / sku drin che ba'i don gyis
da lta nyi shu gnyis mchod 'di rang re nang so dang bza' pa mi sde dang bcas pas bdag rkyen byed pa'i don de yin zhes gsung /dpon rin cen skyabs la jo mo zhang lcam ma
dang khra smon 'bum skyid gnyis las/ dang po'i sras rgyal mtshan dpal bzang / grags pa rgyal mtshan/ grags pa bzang po dang gsum/ 'bum skyid kyi sras gong ma ta'i si tu
byang chub rgyal mtshan/ grags pa shes rab/ bsod nams bzang po ste yum mi gcig pa'i sku mched drug las/ grags pa rgyal mtshan thos bsam sgom pa mang du mdzad cing / khyad
par mgon po'i bka' babs byung zhing gdan sa yun ring du mdzad/ 'di'i dus slob dpon rgyal mtshan bzang pos gong ma'i drung du phyin te lung dang lag rtags sbrel nas khri
dpon byas na'ang / bag yangs kyi dbang du song nas lugs gnyis kyi 'dzin bkod cher ma byung zhing / de'i rjes su rgyal mtshan skyabs kyis khri dpon gyi go sar bsdad kyang
'khos ka chung bas kun gyis brnyas pa byas te/ phag mo gru'i sde srid kyi 'dzin tshugs nyag phra ba byung /

de rjes ta'i si tu khri dpon gyi go sar phebs pa yin la/ 'di nyid ni/ thang yig las/ yar klungs mthil nas rnam smin bskyed rgyal 'byung / / phag gis sa rlog dbus khams sa hor
za/ / btsan rdzong brgya dang rtsa brgyad phyogs su 'byung / / zhes pa'i lung bstan thog tu babs pa ste/ 'jig rten thams cad kyi byed po gser mngal can gyis gnam ka ba
med pa'i sgo phye nas/ rin po che sna bdun sngon du 'gro ba can gyi gdong lnga'i dbang po'i gad rgyangs zad mi shes par sgrogs pa'i khri chen por snying stobs dpa' rtags
kyi lus stobs yongs su rdzogs pa'i sa srung dbang po'i snar rigs pa dang mi rigs pa'i sde bzhi'i spyod tshul la rmongs pa'i dra ba mtha' dag gcod pa'i shes rab kyi spu gri
rnon po rang byan du 'khor yang ngo tsha dang khrel gzhung sogs ya rabs dam pa'i spyod tshul gyi 'dzam bu chu bo'i gser gyi rgyan bzang pos mdzes par spud pas skye rgu
mtha' dag gi ral pa'i cod pan gyi rtse mor 'gying pa la skye bas thob pa'i skal ba mchog gi legs byas kyi zhags pa ring po stong spyi phud kyi rgyal khams su khrims kyi
thig drang por 'debs pa'i sa la spyod pa'i mtho ris kyi rgyal po ta'i si tu byang chub rgyal mtshan dge byed ces pa chu pho stag gi lo la sku bltams/ dgung lo gsum la 'bri
klog mkhyen pa dang / drug la chos skyong bya rog gdong can gyi rjes gnang gsan pas shin tu 'go ba byung / dgung lo bdun pa la spyan snga chos bzhi pa'i drung du dge bsnyen
gyi sdom pa mnos/ mtshan byang chub rgyal mtshan du btags/ dgu pa la mkhan chen tshul dar ba dang / slob dpon pu rangs pa la rab tu byung / bde mgon gyi bsnyen pa mdzad
pas dngos grub kyi mtshan ma khyad par can brnyes/ dgung lo bcu bzhi lon pa'i nag pa zla ba'i tshes bcu bdun la sa skyar 'byon pa'i grabs mdzad/ zla ba bzhi pa'i zla
stod la sne'u gdong nas thon te glur bzhugs pa'i dgongs 'khor rnams kyis chang

mang du blangs te bag med kyi spyod pa byed par brtsams pas/ bdag chen rin po cher 'bul rgyu'i rta la chibs te ma bzhugs par byon pas gzhan rnams kyang phyi la yong dgos pa
byung zhing / skabs 'gar gung gi dro 'phyis pas ma gsol ba sogs rab tu byung ba'i bla mar khas 'che ba 'ga' zhig las 'di nyid bslab pa la gus shing / gong dkar bas mi khal
la gnod pa byas par ngos kyis byon te bcwa hu bstan nas nga'i 'go khag khyed rnams la yod do zhes sogs kyi na phra mo nas gsung sgam po byon pas 'jigs te gtong len dang
bzod gsol byas/ gan pa phur lcang gong gi rgyal pos bar chad brtsam pa sgom bzlas mdzad pas ma tshugs/ de nas rim gyis sa skyar phebs te/ dpon chen 'od zer seng ges ban
rtsa byas nas bdag chen rin po cher phag gru'i dpon po 'di slob gnyer byung na rab/ ma byung na bzhi thog pa'i drung 'khor las tshan zhig zhus 'dug pa ltar dam gnyer la
bskos nas/ bdag chen pa thugs gtum pas gsol gzims dam gnyer sogs la bka' bkyon 'phral 'phral yong ba zhig 'dug pas/ dgongs pa zhus te rang bzhin las tshan med par bzhugs/
sbrul lo'i dpyid chos la chu mig tu phebs skabs zhabs phyir mtshan nyid kyi bla ma 'jam dpal dang / sngags kyi bla ma kun dbang sogs dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi rim pa dang
/ dpon chen dbang phyug dpal/ sang ye dpon po/ ba de lung pa'i dpon po/ stag lung dpon po rnams kyi sdebs khar/ si tu la phag gru dpon por 'bod cing / dpon po rnams kyi
nang nas mthong bzos che bar mdzad/ chag chag la khar/ bdag chen rin po che chibs bshol skabs si tu'i chibs 'dzin pa sngon la song nas med pas/ chibs 'drogs te rgyang ring
por khyer bas/ rgyal tsha rin dbang gis rta nas babs te rogs byas 'dug pa yar klungs pa'i zhen yin 'dug cing / bka' chems su/ nga rta

thog nas ma lhungs pa kho'i drin yin gsung / sa skyar phebs skabs drung 'khor rnams chang gi dga' ston byed par/ brang khang shar na si tu bad yod par bdag chen pa'i sku gzhogs
nas 'bod mkhan bstud mar gnang byung ba la byon pas/ gsol ras gser gyi theb rtse'i nang du gnang chas med par phyag rjen pas bzung chog pa'i dgyes pa'i bka' stsal zhabs
gom 'khyor ba tsam yod na'ang thugs rus mdzad de gsol/ bdag chen rin po che mngon mkhyen thogs med mnga' bas/ si tu la/ khyed la khri dpon yong g.yul rgyal slobs gsungs
pa sogs ma 'ongs pa mkhyen pa'i gsung mang du mdzad/ de'i rgyu mtshan gyis bka' chems su/ bla ma bdag chen pa'i drung du thugs la dpe med btags pa de nga'i bsod nams chen
po yod pa 'di mkhyen par 'dug bsam pa'i dag snang dang mos gus bsam gyis mi khyab pa yod gsung / ston chos thog bla ma mnyam med pa'i drung du brtag gnyis kyi gsan sbyong
mdzad skabs/ slob dpon nam blo dang ma 'cham pa'i tshig rtsod kyi gtam bla mas gsan pas/ khyed tsho rlung gis bdas pa'i bye ri yin/ phag gru dpon po srid pas bskos pa'i
gangs ri yin gsungs skad/ de nas rta lo'i lo gsar la rin cen sgang du dpon chen rin cen sengge'i rtsar byon pas 'brum pas bsnyung de drag pa dang / 'jad du zla ba gsum
bzhi skor bzhugs/ de nas dbus su 'byon khar bdag chen rin po che'i drung du phyag 'bul la byon pas/ bla ma mkhas btsun pa dang / si tu gnyis phyag sbrel nas mkhas btsun
pas si tu ba'i mgo gnyer dang / si tus mkhas btsun pa'i zhabs tog tu 'gyur ba byed dgos pa'i gsung nan che ba byon/ de nas dbus su byon te mi ring bar gong ma rgyal pos
stag mgo nor bu gsum pa dang bcas khri dpo na gyi las ka gnang / khyi lo zla ba brgyad pa'i nang tshun du rgyal mtshan skyabs kyis khri dpon byas na'ang /

lugs gnyis kyi byed pa mthu dman zhing khyad par khong rang gis las ka len par gong ma'i gser zhal lan gsum mthongaba'i rgyal dpal sgrol ma skyid 'phrog 'dod pa'i ched du bsad
cing / si tu la tshig ngan bskur ba sogs kyis/ si tus bla chen kun blo gong ma'i gam nas sa skyar bsnyen rdzogs la byon pa'i sdebs kar si tu rin cen grags/ dpal ldan
ju dben hun dpon gyi dam kha khrims ra dang bcas 'byor 'dug pa'i dus su gtug gsher byas/ rgyal mtshan skyabs las ka las phab/ khyi lo zla ba dgu pa'i tshes dgu'i nyin bka'
shog bcwa hu rnams bsgrags/ bcu bzhi la sne'u gdong rtsis blangs/ gzhon nu 'od gnyer par bskos kyang phyi nang gi zhib tshags tshul dang mthun pa ma byung yang gnyer rtsis
len pa las gzhan pa'i rtsa ra ma mdzad/ 'brug lo la a tu la yar klungs su byon/ yun ring bzhugs/ nyin gcig a tu las/ si tu rta rar khrid nas rta bres kyi kha shing gog
la khad cig 'dug pa de bstan nas/ khri dpon blo zhib dgos pa yin/ 'di la sa phag gsum bzhag na 'grig pas/ rta la snad yar mi yong ba yin/ rta rab la dngul bre ri/ dngul
bre do gser srang brgyad yin gsung ba sogs 'jig rten mi chos la dgos pa'i bslab bya che phra du ma mdzad/ de nas sbrul lo si tu'i rab tu byung ba'i mkhan po tshul dar ba'i
dbon po 'phyong rgyas pa hor gzhon nu bzang po gnyer du bskos/ de rjes gzhis ka rnams kyi gso phran dang / yul gru so sor skye shing 'dzugs pa/ gsham chu la zam mo che
'dzugs pa/ sne'u gdong rtse'i pho brang rgya bskyed de rnam par rgyal ba'i khang bzang sa la 'phos pa lta bu mdzad/ de nas mi ring bar g.ya' bzang pa dang kha mchu mang
du byung zhing / g.ya' bzang pa 'di chos phyogs nas phag gru'i slob brgyud dang / 'jig rten nas hu la hur gtogs pa'i phag gru'i 'og tu yong dgos rgyu yin na'ang / las kyi
shugs kyis bdas pa na/

blo chen log pa'i lam la 'gro/ / mu stegs byed kyi ston pa mchog / dbang phyug smyon pa'i brtul zhugs 'dzin/ / zhes pa'i dpe ltar g.ya' bzang pas phag mo gru pa'i steng du
dmag gis tshur 'gebs lan 'ga' byas shing / tshal pa rgyab phugs su yod pa dang / dpon chen rnams kyang yo bas kha mchu yang g.ya' bzang pa rgyal ba 'ga' re byung na'ang /
kha mchu'i rtsa ba ma chod pas g.ya' phag bar thang du g.yul 'khrugs pas phag gru pham ste/ ston pa gzhon 'od kyis 'go byas mi gces bcu gsum tsam bsad / si tu dang mnyam
du gzhon nu bzang pos 'go byas mi bco lnga tsam ma gtogs phal cher bros/ de nas dpon chen dbang phyug dpal ba'i drung du g.ya' phag gtugs gsher byas pas phag gru bden pa
che ba tsam byung yang / dpon kun rdor gyis gyog byas par brten g.ya' bzang pa rgyal/ de nas mi ring bar dpon chen dbang brtson gyis dog lum par si tu ston mo la bos thog
lab bslus kyi rnam par stag mgo gtod dgos pa'i tsha 'jam ci yang byas shing / zhag bcu dgu tsam gyi ring gung thang du btson la 'jug pa sogs byas kyang / shes rab ldan
pa mgo bskor yang / / bya ba'i cha la rmongs mi 'gyur/ / srog chags grog ma mig med kyang / / mig ldan gzhan las lhag par mgyogs/ / zhes pa ltar mkhyen rab dang snying stobs
phul du byung bas/ dpon chen gyis glags ma rnyed par phyir phebs/ de nas si tu dar ma rgyal mtshan/ mnga' ris phyin gyi 'jags byed pa dang / bod chol kha gsum gyi phye
gsal byed par byon dus/ 'dam dang tshong 'dus 'gur mo gnyis su gtug gsher byed mi thub kyang / mnga' ris 'khor nas yar klungs su se chen rgyal po'i 'ja' swa li ji bcwa
hu sogs yig ris rnams bstan pas si tu dar rgyal ba ha las/ g.ya' phag gi kha mchu'i bcad mtshams legs pa byas na'ang / g.ya' bzang tshul 'bum 'od

kyis/ e gnyal gyi dmag rnams bskul te rdog po rgyud du 'khrugs pas phag gru rgyal te/ ma dga' dgra dgas 'go byas mi nyi shu tsam bsad kyang / g.ya' bzang pas 'bras mo'i nang
du gzhon nu bzang po dpon g.yog gi steng du bkab par/ si tu dpon g.yog gis 'go dmangs 'byor te/ g.ya' bzang pa'i dmag rnams phyir bros/ g.ya' bzang dgon pa dang gzhis ka
rnams rtsis blangs/de nas sa skyar bla ma kun spangs pa dang / dpon chen rgyal bzang ba gnyis kyis si tu gsod/ sne'u gdong rtsis len pa'i gros ngan bshams pa rim gyis mched
na'ang / sngar nas sa phag gnyis 'brel zab cing / khyad par si tu rang bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal ba'i drung 'khor yin pa'i stabs kyis/ dpon chen la dgra dpang
mchongs byed pa'i rtsis yod skabs/ dpon chen rgyal bzang pa dbus phyogs su byon te rim gyis yar klungs su phebs/ sang g.ya' phag gnyis gtug gsher byed rgyu'i nyin/ si tu
bas gzhon nu bzang pos 'gos byas blon po rnams la/ sang nged dang g.ya' bzang pa gnyis khri dpon gyi mdun du gtug gsher byed rgyu yin pas/ ma nges pa'i dpon chen gyis nged
bzung ba bzhin byung na nged kyi lpags pa dmar bshus byed kyin 'dug zer ba byung yang / sne'u gdong ma gtong sogs kyi bslab ston rnams mdzad/ sang dpon chen gyis si tu
bzung kyang thel rtse me la bsregs pas yi ge len rgyu ma byung / de nas dpon chen gyis sne'u gdong du bskor g.yang byas par blon po rnams kyis zhal ngo las sde srid gal che
zer nas ma gtad/ de nas dpon chen gyis si tu la ko sha brgya dang sum cu rtsa lnga tsam brgyab/ zhwa rnga ma can gcig dbu la bskon pa sogs btson chas kyi rnam pas yar
khrid skyi nag bar du tshal pa'i dmag gis bskyal bas kha ngan gtong ba dang

'ded drag byas/ chen po re zhig gud gyur kyang / / de la gdung ba skye mi dgos/ / zla ba re zhig gzas zin kyang / / de ma thag tu grol bar 'gyur// zhes pa ltar/ nyug chos rdzong
du zla ba phyed gnyis dang / ko sbrel du zla gcig bzhugs/ de nas bo dong du dpang lag gi thog dpon chen dbang brtson 'ja' sa dang bcas mthong smon du sleb pa dang /
dpon chen rgyal bzang gis si tu la dam sbrags ma byas par si tu dbus su byon/ sne'u gdong du gzhon nu bzang pos 'go byas blon po rnams la kha mchu 'di'i dbye gsal ma byung
bar chos byed pa skad mi zer ba'i khas len bskor/ de nas dpon chen dbang brtson gyis khri dmag rnams bsdus te dog lung par byung ba dang / si tus kyang rdzong rnams kyi
'dzin cha dang dpung gi bsdu gsog mdzad/ byang gi la khar khrom po lha btsun dpon g.yog brgya skor dang / dpon chen gyi dmag rnams thug pa lha btsun pa can lag dpangs mtho
bar byung ba'i gtam snyan pa sleb/ sang gzhon nu bzang pos dmag dpon byas te/ phag gru khri bskor gyi dmag rnams bteg lhum steng du dro la sleb/ der rta rnams sgugs kha
slangs/ bab col du spyod pa ma yin par dpa' bo dmag la chas pa stag ltar mchong ba la med mi rung gi mi bzhi'i nang gi thug dkar bas lha gsol/ g.yul rgyal bas lto bsgyur/
dus tshod rtsis dang bstun nas dpung rnams 'grims/ dpon chen gyis khri dmag mon mkhar mda' na ru bsgrigs pa'i steng du bkab nas 'khrugs pas sa skya pa'i dbus gtsang gi
khri dmag mtha' dag spub/ phag gru pa'i jus rnam par rgyal ba'i ru mtshon srid rtse'i bar du bsgreng nas/ dgra mgo ru dar dang bcas pho brang chen po sne'u gdong rtser
lag rtags su bskur bas kun gsal sgeg mo rlung gi rgyal mtshan gyi gos gyon pa ltar rnam par bkra ba'i dar gyi lhab lhub dang grags snyan rdza rnga'i sgra chen pos nam mkha'i
nor bu yang skrag nas gling bzhi

bskor ba'i zol gyis rgyu bar byas so//sngar dpon chen rgyal bzang gis si tu bzung ba'i skabs pho brang chen por 'khra phur tshugs shing / nye lam dbang brtson gyis khri skor
bcu gsum gyi dpung bshams pa btul ba sogs gzhan sde rnam par 'joms pa'i dgra thabs kyis sde srid phag mo gru pa'i bstan jus tshugs pa'i rtsa ba lta bu hor gzhon nu bzang
po yin pas/ bka' chems su/ sne'u gdong dgra lag tu ma shor ba byung bas nga'i srog thon/ de la brten nas sde 'di zug chags byung bas kho drin che ba yod pa'i don de yin
zhing / da dung tshun bcad du nga la sngas gtod pa 'di yin pas shi gson gang byung yang nang nas bsdur dgos/ da lta'ang gzhon nu rgyal mtshan gyis 'go byas spun skya ser
kun la blo thub dang / nang mi 'chel ba'i don de yin gsungs la/ de nas si tu rang yang dpung thog tu phebs/ gra phyi 'phyong rgyas sogs lho rgyud kyi sa cha rdzong gzhis
phal cher blangs/ 'thab rtsod snga phyir byung yang gzhan dag rnams rmeg med par bcom/ de nas dpon chen dbang brtson gyis dmag bsags par bla ma dam pas bka' phebs dang /
de rjes kha mchu bsdum mkhan mang du byung yang / dpon chen gzhan gyis bskyod stabs su song bas ma 'grig pa'i zir bun gyi ngang la si tus gong dkar blangs/ de la dpon chen
gyi dpung bcug par bsad bzung tshul lcebs pa sogs mang du byung nas si tu ba rgyal te/ kha rag phyin gtsang la yar gtogs lha 'brug rnams rta rmig 'og nas blangs/ dben
pa dang mjal te gong ma'i drung du khyed rang 'gro'am mi gtong ba gang ris 'thad gsungs pa bzhin dbang phyug dang shes rab rdo rje gnyis btang ba nyes med du 'khor te khri
bskor la dgos pa'i dngul gyi dam kha dang bcwa hu sogs 'grub/de nas 'bri gung sgom pa kun rdor gyis snga phyir byed spyod ma mkhas pa la

brten/ phag gru dang 'bri gung pa 'gal te sde 'khrug lan mang du byung zhing / khyad par 'bri gung pa/ nam grags pa/ g.ya' bzang pa gsum gyis gros bshams nas/ phag gru'i steng
du bkab par gzhon nu bzang pos 'go byas yar stod kyi dmag rogs 'bras mo bsrung ba la bzhag si tu rang gis gtsos dpung chen byang khar bton nas 'bri gung par jus nyes
btang bas/ g.ya' bzang pa yang phyir bros/ tshal pa dang / nam grags pa gnyis kyi khron pa ri dang g.yu rtse brag la rdzong rtsig pa sogs kyi byed par brten/ phag gru'i dmag
rnams gsang mdar yongs thog g.ya' bzang pa 'bum phrag 'od kyis gnyal dmag rnams khrid nas lhun po rtser sleb pa'i 'phrod byung ba dang phyir log ste 'khrugs pas 'bum
phrag 'od kyis 'go byas dgu brgya tsam lhun po rtse'i nang la bcur/ de rjes gnyal dmag yongs pa rnams kyang mang du bsad cing go mtshon rnams thob/ 'bum grags 'od dpon g.yog
rnams kyis 'bab kha blangs/ gnyal shel mkhar sogs gzhis ka rnams su rdzong dpon btang zhing zug pa btsugs/de nas skabs shig chos rje bla ma dam pas bar mdzad nas/ si
tu dang dpon chen rgyal bzang pa gong dkar du mjal 'phrad mdzad/ dpon chen gyis si tu la bzod gsol byas te mthun skabs/ nam grags kyis shangs mthong smon la brgyab pas/ dpon
chen gyi rogs su phag gru'i dmag rnams chen pos 'go byas phyin pa shab chu'i lho khar 'khrugs te/ nam pa'i dpung rnams bcom/ de nas phag gru'i dmag rnams sa skyar 'gro
bar thag bcad kyang / dpon chen gzhan gyis mgo bskor gyi dbang du song ste dmag rnams phyir slog de nas dpon chen sa skyar byon pas bla ma ti shri'i sras po gnyis kyis
btson du bcug pas/ si tus dpung chen gtsang du btegs/ zhi drag gi thabs du ma'i sgo nas dpon

chen btson nas bton/ gtsang gi sa cha phal cher chab 'og tu bcug ste/ phyir 'byon pa'i lam zhor du gzhis ka rin spungs rtsig pa'i zhal bkod mdzad/de yang dus skabs 'di dag
tu sa skya pa zhal ngo mang bas bla brang go bzhir gyes nas nang mi mthun pa sogs kyis bstan jus mtha' dag phag gru pa'i 'og tu shor ba ni/ sa nang grums nas phag gis sa
rlog 'jig / yar klungs nang nas phyag rdor sprul pa 'byung/ / zhes pa'i lung bstan gyi don dang mthun par/ gong ma ta'i si tu 'di nyid ni gsang chen rdo rje theg pa'i bka'i
bsdu ba po rje btsun phyag na rdo rje'i gsang ba gsum gyi rmad du byung ba'i zlos gar las/ chos kyi rgyal po mes dbon gsum gyi mdzad pa'i snang brnyan dri mas cung zad
sbags pa bsal ba'i slad du dbus gtsang ru bzhi'i rgyal khams la stobs kyis mnga' sgyur bar gnam gyi lung gis spyi bo nas dbang bskur bar gor ma chag de nas gong ma rgyal
pos/ da ra kha che sogs gser yig pa mngags te ta'i si tu'i ming dang dam kha gnang /de nas 'bri gung pas phag gru'i steng du dmag tshan cher bsags par brten/ si tus gong
dkar gyi dmag rnams btang ste brag dkar phab/ de skabs sa skyar bla ma kun spangs pa bkrongs pa sogs nang 'khrug byung bas/ kha mchu lab par si tu gtsang du byon/ dpon chen
rgyal bzang 'bod par gtang ba khong lha rtser bka' gros la byon thog dpon chen dbang brtson dang mkhan po nam mkha' ye shes kyis dug btang yang zer/ a rag mang bas lan
kyang zer/ gang ltar dpon chen grongs/ de nas si tus sa skyas gtsos pa'i che gnyan rnams kyi bcwa tshe blangs mjug bsdoms su sa skyar byon/ bcwa tshe'i nang dang 'gal ba
byung na rtsa ra gtong ba'i khrims bsgrags/ lha khang chen mor rin cen 'od kyis 'go byas brgya skor zhig zug bzhag sa skya'i lo rgyus na 'di

skabs rdzong chung pa gzungs kyi dpal bas si tu la mngon spyod kyi las mdzad pas mtshan ma khyad par can byung skad/ de nas si tu dbus su byon rjes lha rtse pa dang byang pa
'khrugs/ de la bcwa tshe dang mthun pa'i rtsa ra gtong bar chen pos gtsos pa'i dmag brdzangs pa snyi tshar sleb dus lha rtse nas dpon chen dbang brtson gyi dpung gis sa
skya lha khang chen mor bskor ba thos pas dpung rnams snyi tshar nas sa skyar phyin te 'khrugs pas mang du bsad / dpon chen bzung / bzhi brgya skor la khrims lugs byas/
de nas ti shri kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon bsod nams blo gros/ g.ya' bzang khri dpon/ tshal pa khri dpon sogs kyis gong sar/ si tus sa skya dmag gis bcom/ khri dpon
gzhan rnams la mthar 'ded byas sogs kyi zhu log rim par phul bar brten/ gong ma thugs tshom pa sel ba'i ched du/ drung chen shes rab bkra shis kyis seng ge dkar mo'i pags
pa sder bzhi ma nyams pas gtsos pa'i 'bul ba dang bcas gong ma'i sku gzhogs su btang bas/ gdung rabs nas gdung rabs su phan pa'i 'ja' sa dang lung bzang po 'grub/ de ltar
'bri tshal g.ya' bzang sa skya'i dpon chen sogs stobs sbyor dregs pas myos pa'i rgol ba'i klan ka can rnams la/ ce spyang dus min du nga ro'i skad 'byin par/ gdong lnga'i
dbang po dgra zlar mi sems pa'i ngang tshul bzhin mdzad kyang / tshur 'gebs kyi byed pa dug sbrul sgong 'khyer gyi snang tshul la brten nas gzhan sde'i mnga' thang thams
cad dpung shed kyis bcad nas nub phyogs chu lha'i mthar thug gi bar du bka' rtags kyi phyag rgya btsan pos gser gyi gnya' shing lta bur lci ba'i rgyal khrims kyi 'og tu
bcug ste/ nyi 'og gi rgyal phran mtha' dag gis yul srol dang mthun pa'i nor gyi dpya 'bul ba sogs mdor na bsil ldan gangs kyi ra ba dar dkar gyi yol bas bres pa'i khongs
su 'khod pa'i skye rgu mtha' dag mi

bde ba'i rtsa rkyen gyi byed po kun nga rgyal ba'i gdong pa dmad nas gting sel gtsang bar tshar bcad/ gong dkar/ brag dkar/ sne'u/ 'ol kha stag rtse/ bsam 'grub rtse/ lhun
grub rtse/ rin spungs sogs dbus gtsang 'dzin ma'i lte ba'i sa mdud rnams la rdzong chen bcu gsum brtsigs/ pho brang chen po sne gdong rtser rgyal sgo phyi nang gsum du byas
pa'i nang ma la nag chang gi khrims bsdams shing / si tu nyid chang dang phyi dro'i kha zas spong ba sogs rab byung gi tshul la gnas pas lha sde dang mi sde kun gyi spyi
bo'i cod pan du nor bu dbang gi rgyal po ltar bsten/de yang sngar dpal ldan sa skya pas bod tsam du ma zad bod chen po'i rgyal khams la mnga' sgyur na'ang / gdung brgyud
zhal ngo rnams thugs 'dod kyi 'then phyogs so sor song zhing / dpon chen rnams kyang tig mi chags par spo len mang ba gong ma'i khrims kyang hor gyi shan shor ba'i hang
zom sogs la brten/ thang lhod dang mtho dma' ci rigs dang / khyad par hor khrims la mi bsad na srog tshab tu srog gtong bas mtshon pa'i khrims rnams sdig pa'i las shas
che bar brten/ bod chos rgyal gong ma'i lugs srol bzang po dge ba bcus gzhi bzung ba 'di nyid/ ta'i si tus gtso bor mdzad par bzhed de/ tshul de nyid sgrub par byed pa la
khas zhan rnams yal bar dor zhing / dregs po rengs su bcug pa ma yin pa'i bden rdzun thang mar brdal nas/ dkar nag shan phyed pa'i khrims kyis rgyal khams rgan mo gser khur
lta bur bde ba'i ched du/ dpa' bo stag gi zhal lce/ sdar ma wa'i zhal lce/ sne mo las 'dzin gyi zhal lce/ zhu bzhes bden rdzun gyi zhal lce/ bzung bkyigs khrims ra'i
zhal lce/ nag can khrag bcor gyi zhal lce/ dran 'dzin chad las kyi zhal lce/ hor 'dra za rkang gi zhal lce/ bsad pa stong gi zhal lce/ rmas pa khrag gi zhal lce/

smyon ham mna' dag gi zhal lce/ brkus pa 'jal gyi zhal lce/ nye 'brel 'bral bzlums kyi zhal lce/ byi byas byi rin gyi zhal lce/ nam bar tshur gyi zhal lce ste bco lnga'i sgo
nas gtan la phab/ de yang mi bsrun log par 'khu ba'i dgra sde tshar bcad nas/ jus don bzhed thog tu 'khyol ba'i thabs su drag po dpung gi sbyor ba bshams tshul/ tshur 'gebs
la btsan po'i rdzong la 'khra 'phur byed tshul/ sne mor mngags sleb rnams kyis rnam dkar gyi las la spyod cing nye 'gyang spangs pa'i gzhung don gtso bor byed tshul/
mi bsad la lan 'jal gyi gnyis phung sdig las byed du mi 'jug par stong sprod len sogs phra zhib mdzangs pa'i blos khrims kyi 'jam dar yug gcig tu brkyangs pa'i 'dzum gyis
rdzogs ldan gsar pa'i mgron ring nas 'gugs par mdzad do// smras pa/'jigs bral sra brtan g.yul ngor dpa' ba'i ru mtshon rtse la dgra sde'i srog dbugs blangs pa na//gser
ldan rus dkar khyab pa'i mdangs kyis zla gzhon skrag ste byang gling ngos kyi mkha' la bros//khrag gi rba rlabs 'phyur ba'i 'od dmar gzi yis rgod ma kha de rgya mtsho'i 'gram
du yibs//rnam par rgyal ba'i rdza rnga ldir bas sum rtsen bdag po 'dud par gros pa'i ca co gleng //e ma rtsod pa'i dus 'dir su wa rNa'i//'khor lo nam mkhar 'phags pa'i
rgyal thabs kyis//grags snyan du kU la yi ba dan dkar//srid pa'i rtse mor khyab ces lha rnams sgrog/

gong ma'i lung gis gtsug na zla ba'i mchog/thob pas stobs ldan 'gro skyabs gser can 'ga'//dpa' mdzangs seng ge'i sder mos bsad pa na//pad dkar mig cig gnyis pa sa 'dir snang
//de nas dwags po bka' brgyud kyi phyogs su mdo phyogs kyi bshad gra'i srol med pa gsar du btod pa'i ched du chos grwa chen po rtses thang btab/ phar tshad sogs bka' po
ti du ma la rigs lam nas drangs pa'i bshad nyan btsugs/ de dang thel gyi sgom grwa gnyis ka la phun sum tshogs pa'i mthun rkyen sbyor ba/ bde bar gshegs pa'i sku brnyan
du ma dang / gser gyi bka' 'gyur ro cog bzhengs pa/ ra sa 'phrul snang dang bsam yas kyis mtshon pa'i gnas chen khyad 'phags rnams la mchod 'bul sogs thar pa dang thams cad
mkhyen pa'i lam bla na med pa bsgrubs pa'i tshogs gnyis kyi chu gter chen po dbyar mtsho ltar gyur pa'i mthus dkar nag gi las kyi 'bras bu chos thams cad rjen par 'char
ba'i tshad ma'i srang la gzhal bas/ nag po'i 'bras bus cha tsam du yang ma gyur pas/ dge legs chu zla'i 'od dkar grangs med pa spros pas mngon par mtho ba dang nges par
legs pa'i gang bu yongs su smin pas nor 'dzin gyi bu mo mngal khur gyis lci bar mdzad/'di nyid gshegs rjes 'jam dbyangs gu shri chen po ni dpon bsod nams bzang po'i jo mo
nyi ru ma dang mang nyam gnyis las snga ma la nyid dang bdag po shAka rin pa gnyis/ phyi ma la dpon rin rdor 'khrungs pa las/ 'jam dbyangs pa bla ma klu lung grags pa la
klog yig bslabs/ chos bzhi grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi drung du dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa mnos/ slob dpon

gzhon brtson la rab tu byung ba'i mtshan shAkya rgyal mtshan du gsol/ gdan sar brtag gnyis dang / rtses thang du bka' po ti bzhi la bshad pa mdzad pas mkhas pa'i grags pa thob/
bu ston rin po che'i drung du rdo rje theg pa'i rgyud bshad dbang lung mang du gsan pas/ mgon po gdong gi ri man gyis yar klungs kyi zhing re'i khar dkyil 'khor rigs
mi 'dra ba re bzhengs kyang kheb par yod ces bu ston chos rjes zhal pho gsungs/ chos rje bla ma dam pa'i drung du bsnyen par rdzogs te lha sar chos 'khor dang / rtses thang
gi tshogs pa lo bcu gsum gyi bar du skyong bar mdzad/ mi ring bar pho brang sne'u gdong rtse'i khri thog tu phebs te hor gong ma rgyal pos/ ta'i si tu dang chang gu'i
lung / kwa din gu shri las ka dang dam kha gnang / bod chol kha gsum brgyud pa dang bcas pa shes su 'jug pa'i 'ja' sas spur rgyal bod gyi rgyal khams na mngon par mtho/
gtsang phyogs su log par 'khu ba'i kun dkris kyis brnag pa'i sems ldan 'ga' zhig gi steng du dpung gi sbyor ba bshams dus/ chos skyong bya rog gdong can gyi nus pas dmag
rnams gtsang po la thogs med du phyin/ phyir phebs nas dpal ldan bla ma dam pa gtso bor bzhugs pa'i dge 'dun khri phrag mang po la zhag bcu sbrel du gya nom pa'i bkur sti
mdzad nas chos 'khor btsugs/ mnga' 'bangs thams cad bde skyid kyi dpal la 'khod par mdzad/dpon rin cen rdo rje zin bkra shis skyid dang / do brag ma rin cen 'tsho gnyis
khab tu bzhes pa'i snga ma la rgyal sras grags pa rin cen dang / chos rje chos bzhi pa gnyis las/ chos bzhi pa chung ngu'i dus su mkhan chen seng ge rgyal mtshan gdan drangs
pas/ sman bla'i pho brang gi thugs ka nas 'od zer 'phros pa sku lus la thim pa gzigs pa'i lung bstan mdzad/ rgyal sras grags rin pa la brtag gnyis kyi lung zhus te thugs
sbyong dang / spyan snga grags

she ba la dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa mnos pa'i mtshan grags pa byang chub tu gsol/ 'jam dbyangs gu shri chen pos gdung brgyud spel ba'i bka' gnang yang ma bzhed par chos rje dpal
ldan bla ma'i drung du bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa bzhes/ de nas gdan sa chen po'i go sar bzhugs nas zab rgyas chos kyis skal bzang gi gdul bya smin par mdzad cing / gu
shri chen po'i rjes su pho brang sne'u gdong rtse'i khri thog tu byon nas bla dpon sbrags te rgyal srid chos bzhin du bskyangs/ snyigs dus kyi rgyal ba gnyis pa btsong kha
pa chen po yang 'di nyid kyi zhabs la gtugs nas mi 'phrog pa'i dad pa tshad med pa 'khrungs te/ mkhas dbang daNDi'i gzhung lugs nas drangs pa'i rtogs brjod dpag bsam lhun
por grags pa'i legs par bshad pa'i rtsom pa gnang / spyan snga rin po che yang rgyal ba btsong kha pa chen po'i rmad du byung ba'i mkhyen rab kyis gsung rab rgya mtsho
chen po'i pha rol tu byon pa gzigs nas bsngags pa rgya cher mdzad/'di nyid kyi gcung chos rje bsod nams grags pa dpon mo la 'khrungs/ mkhan chen gzhon dbang pa'i drung du
rab tu byung / rtses thang gi gdan sar phebs nas 'chad rtsod rtsom pa'i skyes bzang pos mkhas pa rnams kyi yid yongs su phrogs/ lha sar dge 'dun dpag tu med pa la chos
'khor bskor/ lo chen byang chub rtse mo'i drung du bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i sdom pa bzhes/ pho brang chen po'i khri thog tu phebs nas phan bde'i bsil zer mnga' 'bangs kunda'i
snying la brin par mdzad/sa skyong shAkya rin cen gyis zin rin cen 'dzom zhes pa grongs tshe las dag rnams kyi snang ngor sengge la chibs nas mkha' 'gros spyan drangs
pa mthong zhing / tshems la dung g.yas 'khyil byon pa'i rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i

rnam par sprul pa de nyid khab tu bzhes pa'i sras mi'i dbang po grags pa rgyal mtshan/ drung byang chub rdo rje/ spyan snga bsod nams bzang po/ spyan snga dpal ldan bzang po/
spyan snga bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ drung sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan rnams sku bltams pa las/mi'i dbang po grags pa rgyal mtshan ni/ 'jam dbyangs chen po'i sku'i skye ba
gsal bar dran zhing / mkhyen rab mchog tu yangs pas klog yig sogs ched gnyer du bslab sbyangs ma dgos par 'bad med du mkhyen/ mkhan po gzhon dbang pa'i drung du rab tu byung
/ spyan snga grags pa byang chub la chos khrid rnams rdzogs par gsan/ mtshan grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang por gsol/ chos grwa chen po rtses thang gi gdan sar phebs
nas rig pa'i dbang phyug chos kyi grags pa'i bstan bcos tshad ma rnam 'grel gsungs pas shin tu phra ba rtog ge'i rig pa la mngon par nga rgyal ba'i mkhas rlom sa srung
rnams kyi spobs pa phrogs/ de nas pho brang chen po'i sengge'i khri'i dga' tshal du zhabs zung sA la chen po'i ljon pa rnam par bkod pa'i rdzogs ldan gsar pa'i dri bsung
ma la ya'i rlung bzhon gyis bod chen por 'khod pa'i skye rgu kun gyi duH kha'i tsha gdung gi 'jigs pa ming gi lhag mar mdzad nas/ phan pa dang bde ba'i char chen po tha gru
kun tu phab/ bkra shis sgo mang gsum gyis thog drangs pa'i thugs dang sku'i rten/ bde bar gshegs pa'i bka' dri ma med pa bod du 'gyur ba'i glegs bam mtha' dag sa le sbram
gyi snying po las grub pa tshar gsum gyis thog drangs gsung rten mtha' yas shing / de dag kyang rgyal mkhar rtse'i sde dgon du bka' 'gyur shin tu mang ba char rtsis nas
bris pa snang ba lta bu ma yin par rgyu phun sum tshogs pa'i steng du/ bod kyi yi ge mtha' dag

gangs khrod pa rnams la bka' drin 'gran zla ma mchis pa thon mi sambho Tas mdzad pa'i sum rtags dang / de dag la brten nas bod kyi mkhas pa'i dbang po rnams kyi yi ge'i brda
dag gi bstan bcos mang du snang ba rnams la brten nas sdeb kyi sbyor lugs mtha' dag la zhib mor dpyad/ rgyud 'bum sogs su legs par sbyar ba lha'i skad kyi sngags mtha'
dag byA ka ra Na'i don khong du chud pa'i skad gnyis smra ba rnams kyis rang bzhin/ rkyen/ rnam 'gyur gsum la brten nas gtan la phabs pas/ bka' 'gyur de rnams gcig tu bstan
pa'i rtsa lag lta bur gyur/ gtsug tor dri ma med pa'i gzungs gser gyis bzhengs pa'i snying po can gyi rten 'bum ther grangs mang ba dang / 'bum ther dgung lo'i grangs
lo re bzhin bzhengs pa/ spyan snga rin po che bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyis chos 'byung mig 'byed 'od stong mdzad pa'i lo sa khyi yan la lo nyi shu rtsa gnyis star chags su
byung bar gsungs 'dug pas de nas kyang sa phag nas lcag phag gi bar lo bcu gsum gyi ring rgyun mi chad par mngon/ gzhan yang ris su ma chad pa'i grub pa'i mtha' mtha' dag
la bsnyen bkur dang / yongs 'dzin rnams la chos kyi gsan pa mdzad pa/ paN chen shAkya shrI'i rgyun 'dzin tshogs sde 'ga' zhig la bstan pa'i rtsa lag mkhan chen thams cad
mkhyen pa zhi ba 'tsho'i thugs dam bde gshegs bdun gyi smon lam 'bum phrag mang du bskul ba/ khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po btsong kha pa chen pos srid 'di'i legs byas rnam
par dkar ba'i nam mkha'i glang po yongs su 'khrigs pa las byung ba'i 'phral yun kun tu dge legs kyi 'jug pa rgyun mi chad pa'i gru char gyis/ ye shes mchog gi myu gu zad
mi shes pa'i zong du bskrun pa'i thabs mkhas kyi sgo 'phar brgya phrag phye ba'i kun mkhyen zas gtsang sras pos cho 'phrul bstan pa'i dus khyad par can chu shel dbang
po rta chen dga' ma'i khyim du rtse

dgar spyod pa'i zla bar/ bod yul gyi rdo rje gdan lha ldan sprul pa'i gtsug lag khang du smon lam gyi dus ston khyad par can 'dzugs pa mdzad pa'i mthun rkyen yang dag par bsgrubs/
ring mo nyid nas bsod nams kyi tshogs rlabs po che bsags pa'i rten 'brel gyis khri thog tu phebs pa nas bzung ste/ 'jig rten kun tu mu ge dang yams nad sogs med cing
mkho dgu'i yo byad la longs spyod pa'i 'dod rgu rmugs 'dzin gyi bang mdzod la rang dbang du spyod pa lta bur gyur/ de yang 'di'i yab sa skyong chen po shAkya rin cen
la tho gan thi mur gyis lung gnang nas pho brang chen por khri dpon du phebs shing / tho gan thi mur gyi dus gru tha la gru rgya nag gi yul gru chen po 'ga' zhig tu khral
len par btang bas/ de dang rgya'i mi dpon 'ga' zhig gros mthun te shing rta 'khor lo mang du byas pa'i 'og tu dmag dang / steng du rin po che dang gos dar gyi tshogs bzhag
ste khral skyel ba ltar byas nas pho brang gi nye logs su 'ongs te dmag gis bskor bas/ rgyal po gsang sgo zhig la bros/ gru tha la grus mang 'bangs thams cad chab 'og
tu bcug pa'i sras kyen 'un/ de'i sras yung lo ta ming rgyal po'i dus gser gyi dam kha dang / slar yang shel gyi dam kha/ dbang gi 'ja' sa gnang bas mtshan dbang grags pa
rgyal mtshan zhes snyan pa'i rdza rnga skabs gsum pa'i lam du brdungs pas 'jig rten gyi mes po tshangs pas gnam rim pa bcu gsum gyi mthongs nas rin po che'i bum pa dri bzang
gi chus gang bas spyi bo nas dbang bskur/ rdzong chen rnams kyi rdzong sdod so so la mi brgyud dang bcas par 'ja' sa'i shel dam gnang / mchog dman gyi skye rgu mtha'
dag gong ma chos rgyal chen po zhes gleng ngo / /nyang stod shar kha ba rgyal rtse rab brtan kun bzang 'phags pas gong ma 'di gnyis kyi gzims dpon gyi las ka bzung zhing
/ sde srid 'di nyid kyi

bka' drin las mnga' thang che bar yod kyang / cung zad byed ma mkhas pas gong ma'i thugs la phog ste/ nyang stod du dpung gi 'jug sgo lan gnyis tsam mdzad pas/ yar klungs pa
rnams dgra nyang stod shar kha ba zer ba'i skabs byung zhing / 'on kyang dran 'dzin tsam las rgyal mkhar rtse rtsis len pa sogs ma mdzad/ de tsam ma gtogs dbus gtsang mtha'
dag bde 'jags las/ dpung gi 'jug sgo sogs sdig pa'i las kyi sbyor ba la mi re bar chos ldan rgyal po'i khrims nyin byed dbang po shar ba na/ mi bsrun pa'i skye bo zhe
sdang gi 'dab ma rnam par rgyas pa'i ku mu ta'i tshal mtha' dag rang shugs kyis zum par gyur to/ /gong ma 'di'i dus dpa' 'dzangs rtul phod pa'i rgyal po'i bya ba la mkhas
pa'i blon po rin spungs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan rin spungs kyi rdzong dpon dang / sa skya'i lha khang chen mo'i dpon chen gyi khrir bskos/ 'phyong rgyas pa hor dpal 'byor
bzang por bsam 'grub rtse'i rdzong dpon dang dmag dpon gyi las ka gnang / gzhan yang sne'u pa nam mkha' bzang po/ brag dkar ba rin cen dpal rnams grags che/ rigs rus yon
tan mnga' thang sogs lugs gnyis kyi go rim dang mthun pa'i drung 'khor shin tu mang zhing / de dag kyang chen po'i las tshan gyi sgo dang bstun pa'i rgyan gos kyi rim
pa dang / khyad par gnam lo gsar du tshes pa'i dga' ston dus rin cen rgyan char grags pa'i bkod pas khyad par du 'phags pa'i rgyan sprod dang / rgyun mar yang rin po che'i
phra tshoms kyis rnam par mdzes pa'i kArNi ka rna ba'i rgyan du spud pa sogs mdzad la/ mdor na lugs gnyis kyi mdzad pa bzang po gzhan dag lta ci smos/ gnas skabs kyi spyod
lam yang ya rabs bzang po che btsun gyi ngang tshul las/ lung ma bstan gyi zhwa gos gyon pa/ sgrigs kun spyod kyi srang la bcur ba med

pa'i yid la shar tshad lag tu mi len pa'i mig ltos mchog tu bzang / chos rje bsod grags pas/ chos rgyal chen po 'di nyid kyi blon po'i khrod du brag dkar ba shes rab bkra shis
'dren pa ni/ sher bkras pas gong ma ta'i si tu'i skabs hor rgyal po'i drung du 'ja' sa zhu bar byon pa'i dus dgung lo bzhi bcu rtsa bdun gyi khar sleb cing / si tu rin
po che nas gong ma 'di'i ring la gdan rabs kyang 'ga' zhig song bas/ drung chen sher bkras pa 'ong ba'i don med cing / rin spungs nam mkha' rgyal po nam mkha' rgyal mtshan
gyi sras yin kyang / nam mkha' rgyal mtshan gyi sngon la 'dren pa sogs dmus long gcig pur rgyu ba lta bur kun dang mi mthun pa'i gtam mang ngo / / smras pa/phul byung
bsod nams shing rtas legs drangs pas//dbang phyug brgyad kyi yod tan 'bar ba'i gzis//sde gsum cig car gsal ba'i grags pa'i gzugs//rlung gi rgyal mtshan lta bur tshar du
dngar//tha gu'i lto can 'jug pa bcu pa'i sgyus//kun las rnam par rgyal la mtshar du ci//g.yo med drang po'i tshul gyis lhar bcas 'gro'i//gtsug na zhabs sen u dum wA ra 'dzum//gcung
sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan gyis rin spungs nas bdag mo zhig khab tu bzhes par grags pa 'byung gnas dang / kun dga' legs gnyis 'khrungs/

grags pa 'byung gnas sku na phra mo nas thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i rig pa'i gnas la mkhas par sbyangs/ khyad par rdo rje theg pa la thugs rab kyi rtsal shin tu che
bas/ mkhas pa'i dbang po 'gos lo ye bzang rtse ba'i zhal nas/ de rjes mi'i dbang po grags pa 'byung gnas pa thugs rab shin tu che zhing gsang sngags kyi mkhyen pa shin
tu rgyas par gyur kyang / gdan sa'i bzhugs khri rin po che shin tu gnyan par dgongs nas gdan sar ma bzhugs kyang / gnas chen du 'gro ba'i ri pa rnams la mgyogs khrid gsungs
zhes deb sngon du gsungs pa ltar yin la/ de yang chos rgyal chen po gshegs rjes/ 'di nyid sku na phra bas pho brang chen po'i khrir yab sras gnyis su bsko la bka' blon
rnams gros ma mthun par spyan snga rin po che bsod nams rgyal mtshan la zhus pas/ sras bsko bar bka' gnang ba bzhin mdzad kyang spyan snga gshegs rjes/ yab kyis khri thog
yong ba'i ched du gnang sgo ma legs par brten/ yar klungs su sde gzar langs te yab che sa dpon blon yar rgyab tu 'byon dgos byung / de nas gong ma dbus kyi gzhis bskor
la phebs skabs sne'u rdzong du mkhas grub chos rje dge legs dpal bzang dang / gsang ne'u thog gi chos rje rnam gnyis/ drung chen slob dpon sogs mjal bar phebs/ gong ma'i
sku gzhogs su bzhugs gral gyi thog gsung rab kyi 'bel gtam mdzad khar/ mkhas grub chos rje dang gsang phu'i chen po rnams so so nas bshad pa mdzad rgyu 'ong du re yang /
gong ma'i zhabs phyir 'gos lo tsA ba gzhon nu dpal ba yod pas khong gis rtses thang pa'i brtul zhugs kyi thog mar gzhung len pa mdzad skad/ de nas 'jam dbyangs gong ma rgyal
po kyen tha'i yis dbang gi 'ja' sa gnang ba nas bzung / dbang grags pa 'byung gnas su grags/ thel dang rtses thang gnyis su gdan sa zur du med na'ang / gsung chos 'gangs
che ba rnams rtse

nas gnang zhing / zur 'chad slon dpon rnams la bka'i 'khor los khyab pa dang / gser gyi bka' 'gyur bzheng ba sogs lugs zung gi mdzad pa mtha' dag gong ma na rim gyi srol bzang
po ma nyams par bzung / yar rgyab nas che sa rtses thang du gdan drangs/ zhal ngo nang mtshams kyi 'khon zhi nas thugs yid gcig tu 'dres/ byang phyogs kyi bso kha bsrung
bar 'u yug gling dkar gyi rdzong brtsigs/ rin spung nor bu bzang po/ 'phyong rgyas pa hor dkon cog rin cen ni chos rgyal chen po'i zhabs la gtugs kyang gong ma 'di'i
dus su khrims kyi kha lo sgyur ba'i blon po mdzad/gcung kun dga' legs pas gsung rab la sbyangs pa ma smad pa mdzad de rtses thang gi gdan sar phebs/ rin spungs nas bdag mo
khab tu bzhes par sras rin cen rdo rje dbang gi rgyal po 'khrungs/ 'jam dbyangs gong ma chen hang rgyal pos dbang gi 'ja' sa gnang / 'di nyid rtogs pa'i yon tan phul du
byung ba'i grub pa'i dbang phyug chen po zhig yin par 'dug na'ang gnas skabs su skye bo rnams kyi snang ngor mdzad sgo legs rgyu med tsam yod 'dug par dpags/ gtsang gi gzhis
bskor la phebs dus rin spungs nor bzang pas gus 'dud bla na med pa mdzad kyang gnang sgo'i khog la ma mgu skad/ de nas gong ma ka bzhi pa sku mched kyis gang zhus la
gsan pas/ yab yum nang mtshams su sel chen po zhugs te/ yar gong bya pa bsam sde pa sogs bdag mo phyogs dang / sne'u 'ol dga' rnams gong ma'i phyogs su chad nas dus mi bde
ba mang du byung / 'on kyang 'phyong rgyas pa rdo rje tshe brtan phan tshun gnyis ka'i phyogs su ma lhungs pas sde gzar bzlums shing / zhal ngo nang mtshams kyi legs spel
mdzad pas sde srid kyi zhabs tog tu 'gyur ba byung / de nas yum gshegs rjes rin spungs pa mtsho skyes rdo rjes mkhar thog bzung / de yang deb

ther sngon po las/ de rjes bdag po kun dga' legs pa dang / che sa sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan bka' bgros mdzad de/ shing pho khyi'i lo zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes bcu la chos kyi
rje rin po che dpal ngag gi dbang po dgung lo bcu drug bzhes pa zhig rin po che'i gdan seng ge'i khri la bzhugs su gsol zhes gsungs pa ltar/ bar skabs su thel gyi gdan
sa stongs na'ang / slar spyan snga ngag gi dbang po 'di nyid bzhugs pa yin la/'di'i yab/ la la dag tshes lnga rin po che grags pa 'byung gnas yin par 'chad/ 'ga' zhig tshes
lnga rin po che sku tshe'i stod smad mtha' dag tu rab tu byung ba yin pas/ ma yin par smra ba yang yod la/ 'di nyid kyis mdzad pa'i phur pa'i 'phrin las rgya mtsho'i
mdzad byang du/ jo sras kun bzang rol pa'i rdo rje zhes gsungs pa la dpags na yab yin nam snyam/ gang ltar shes ldan rnams kyis dpyad par bya'o/ / de yang spyan snga ngag
gi dbang po gzhon nu nas dpal ye bzang rtse ba sogs yongs 'dzin du ma bsten nas gsung rab la thos bsam bsgom pa mang du mdzad/ bstan pa la zhugs te yongs su rdzogs pa'i
dge slong gi sdom pa mnos te gdan sa chen po'i spyan sngar phebs/ bar skabs su gong ma'i gnang bkod la brten nang mtshams su mi mthun pa byung yang / slar rim pas 'jags skabs/
rin spungs don yod rdo rjes gtsang dpung rnams dbus su bcug ste gzhis ka sne'u pa'i lag nas rdzong gzhis 'ga' zhig blangs/ de nas spyan snga rin po che/ rin spungs
mtsho skyes pa dang don yod rdo rje gnyis/ 'phyong rgyas pa hor tshe dbang rnam rgyal dang / hor rin cen rgyal mchog sku mched kyis gtsos pa'i sne'u pa dpal 'byor rgyal po/
yar rgyab pa rin cen rgyal po/ byar pa bkra shis dar rgyas sogs blon po rnams kyis gros thog nas pho brang chen por spyir spyan drangs/ mi ring bar zhal ngo gong ma

rnams gshegs pas lha rigs rlangs kyi gdung 'dzin pa spyan snga nyid ma gtogs med par brten/ ji ltar grong khyer ser skya'i mi gtsang lud/ / de ni bu ram shing pa'i zhing la
phan/ / de bzhin byang chub sems dpa'i nyon mongs lud// de ni sangs rgyas chos rnams bskyed la phan/ / zhes pa'i don ltar/ bod kha ba can 'dir kun mkhyen bu ram shing pa'i
bstan pa rin po che dang / skye rgu rnams kyi phan bde ni gnam bskos kyi rgyal po phag mo gru pa'i sde srid la rag lus pas/ gong du smos pa'i blon po rnams kyis gong ma
spyan snga rin po cher nan gyis zhus te/ rdzong kha pa'i sras mo zhig bdag mor phul/ yab mes kyi lugs srol bzang po rnams dkar phyogs kyi zla tshes lta bur ches cher gsal
bar mdzad/ sras ngag dbang bkra shis grags pa sku bltams nas ring por ma lon par spyan snga zhi bar gshegs khar sras sku ha cang phra bas de la thugs chags pa'i tshul
gyis sku ngal ba chen por gyur skabs/ spyan snga chos kyi grags pas gdung brgyud rin po che nar ma son pa'i ring khong rang gis thel gyi spyan snga'i khur bzhes dang / thel
rtses thang gi chen po gros dbang pa blon po rnams dang bcas par gnang bkod bka' nan sogs kyis khyab pa'i sde srid kyi lar rgya mi 'phyug pa'i zhal len mdzad/ de yang
dpon tshab thel gtong byed par rin spungs mtsho skyes rdo rjes/ blon po gzhan rnams la gros med par 'ga' zhig gi 'dod pa ltar mdzad pas/ sde dpon gzhan rnams ma 'dod pa'i
dbang gis sde gzar langs/ 'on kyang 'phyong rgyas nas sde srid kyi lar rgya la dgongs te thugs khog che bar mdzad pas yo 'khyoms cher ma byung / de nas 'jam dbyangs gong
mas spyan snga rin po cher dbang gi 'ja' sa gnang yang spyan snga zhing brjes pas gnang sbyin rnams phyag mdzod du bzhag nas gser yig pa phyir log

de rjes rin spungs pa dang 'phyong rgyas pa gnyis kyis gtsos pa'i blon po rnams bka' bgros thog nas gdung brgyud rin po che ngag dbang bkra shis grags pa pho brang chen po'i
khri thog tu spyan drangs/ gzhon nu'i dus nyid nas rol rtsed sogs skye bo phal pa dag gis spyod yul las rnam par 'das pas 'jig rten gyi mes po rnams kyis kyang blos 'khyud
par dka' zhing / chos dang srid kyi yon tan ma lus cig car du shong ba'i za ma tog lto ba rab tu yangs pa/ chen po'i rnam par thar pa'i kha rgyan gyis mdzes pa'i gzi
brjid kyi rgyal po nyin mor byed pa la skyengs pa ster bas rigs stobs su ma zad/ blo stobs kyis kyang bod chen po'i rgyal khams su 'khod pa'i gong ma'i mdun na 'don blo can
shel gyi me long lta bu rnams kyang zil gyis gnon pa'i bka' khrims bzang pos bod 'bangs thams cad bde ba nas bde bar spyod pa'i bde skyid kyi glu dbyangs snyan pos dri
za'i rgyal po gan dharbha kha ba rir gnas sam snyam du skabs gsum pa rnams la 'phyang mo ster bar byed do/ /'on kyang 'di nyid kyi dus/ grags 'byung ming can sne yi gdong
po 'dzin/ / bdud sprul mi dgus phag tshang yos ltar rngod// ces pa'i lung bstan ltar/ rin spungs ngag dbang rnam rgyal gyis e gnyal gyi phyogs su dmag gi dpung khyer byed
pa sogs gong ma'i dgongs par phog pa mdzad par brten/ zhwa dmar ba bzhi pas/ phag mo gru pa'i sde srid 'di/ spyir rgyal khams yongs/ sgos sde dpon rnams/ yang sgos khyed
rin spungs pa la gces pas dgongs bsams mdzad dgos tshul gsungs kyang bzhed pa zhig ma byung / de yang lung bstan du grags 'byung zhes pa ni gong ma grags 'byung ba'i skabs
dus mi bde ba 'ga' zhig byung bas 'go zin pa la dgongs kyi/ dngos gzhi gong ma 'di'i dus so/ / de skabs 'jam dbyangs gong mas dbang gi mtshan dang 'ja'

sa gnang / zhabs drung gong ma chen po dpal ngag gi dbang phyug bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan phyogs thams cad las rnam par rgyal ba kwa din gu shri ho wang gi mtshan gyi
zlos gar srid pa gsum gyi me long gi ngos su gsal bar shar ro/ / mi ring bar rin spungs pas me tog mda' can gyi las dang tshangs pa mtshungs par spyod pa'i sdig sems kyis
