sde gzar bslangs pas/ lha ma yin lha'i mnga' thang la phrag dog gi bsam pas g.yul bkye ba na legs bris pa rnams kyi bsod nams kyi mthus lha min mtha' dag ming gi lhag mar
'gyur ba de bzhin du sde srid mtshan jus rgyal/ 'on kyang zhwa dmar chos grags pas bar mdzad nas lo gsum gyi chings bsdams na'ang / rin spungs pas slar sde gzar bslangs
te rgyal mkhar rtser bteg skabs/ 'phyong rgyas pa rin cen rgyal mchog gis gtsos gong ma'i dpung chen rnams nyang stod bar du byon/ dga' ldan pa dmag dpon bsod nams rgyal
pos skyid 'phan gyi dpung rnams khrid de shangs kyi bar du btegs pas ri la spyi bos brdung ba'i rnam thar 'dzin pa cher rlom gyi dregs ldan gzhis ka rin spungs pa 'bangs
gyen log gi rgyu mi zad pa bsags pa'i 'bras bu dus gcig tu smin pas ci bya gtol med du gyur na'ang / rgyal rtse dang pa snams pa'i sa cha bshor ba rnams phyir sprod pa
dang / gong sar dgongs bsangs/ rdzong dpon gyi las ka zhu ba/ phyin chad ma rungs pa'i sems 'dor ba sogs kyi dan kha las mtha' med du gtong ba ma mdzad/ de lta na'ang dus
kyi bskal pas 'gro ba'i bsod nams mthu dman zhing / nag po'i phyogs kyis yid bsgyur bas bdud kyi las 'grub pa'i 'bras bu'i shugs gang gis kyang dgag dka' bar brten/ rin
spungs pa dpon blon gyis sde gzar tshan che bar bslangs kyang / sde srid kyi mtshan jus la skyon ma byung / gong ma 'di nyid kyis bde bar gshegs pa'i gsung gi snying po gser
zhun ma'i

khu bas bris pa'i bka' 'gyur dang / stong 'khun mdzangs ma'i sor mo'i 'du byed las bskrun pa'i gan gos kha dog sna tshogs las grub pa'i sku brnyan bzheng ba phyogs lhung gi
bsam pas ris su mi gcog par/ ston pa bu ram shing pa'i rjes su zhugs pa'i grub pa'i mtha' thams cad la bsnyen bkur dang mgo 'dren/ jo shAka rnam gnyis dang byang chub chen
pos thog drangs pa'i gangs khrod kyi sku gsung thugs rten khyad 'phags rnams kun tu bzang po'i mchod pa'i sprin mngon par spro ba dang / rje btsun phyag na padma dbasod
nams rgya mtsho dang / dpal 'brug pa'i ring lugs pa padma dkar po rnams ti shrir bsten/ mdor na 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dbang phyug mtha' dag 'bad med du
'grub pa'i rgyu dge ba bcu la rdzogs par longs spyod pa dang ldan pa'i me tog gzhon nu gsar du dgod pa'i 'khri shing nam mkha'i mtha' klas par 'khyud pa'i khor yug dang
po bde bar gshegs pa'i snying po mchog gi go 'phang srid pa'i rtse mor bsnyeg pa'i them skas su 'dzugs par mdzad/'di nyid kyi dus rin spungs pa dang dpon blon nang mtshams
su sel che bar byung yang / phyi rgya'i blon chen gyi gral du rin spungs ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ sras don grub tshe brtan rdo rje rnam gnyis/ 'phyong rgyas pa hor rin cen
rgyal mchog sku mched/ sras hor bsod nams mgon po mched gsum/ de'i sras hor bsod nams dar rgyas rnams rim pa bzhin dang / brag dkar 'jam dpal tshe ring rgyal po/ yar rgyab
rin cen bkra shis/ dga' ldan pa bsod nams rgyal po/ bya nor bu bkra shis sogs blon po dang / drung 'khor 'gangs che ba shin tu mang / gong ma 'di nyid la rin spungs kyi
sras mo zhig khab tu bzhes par sras gong ma 'gro ba'i mgon po dang / spyan snga grags 'byung ba gnyis las/ gong ma 'gro ba'i mgon po gong dkar du phebs/ dpon sa

'phyong rtse'i drung khab tu bzhes pa'i sras zhabs drung ngag dbang grags pa sku bltams/ 'gro ba'i mgon po gshegs pa'i gdung rten rin po che'i phra tshoms kyis spras pa pho
brang gong ri dkar por bzhengs/ spyan snga grags 'byung ba thel gyi gdan sar phebs/ zhabs mi bde ba'i dbang gis zab bzhes thugs dam gyi rim pa gtso bor mdzad/ khyad par
gshed skor dang ma mgon bya rog gdong can la rtsal du thon pas sde pa 'ol kha ba phun tshogs rab brtan pas thel gyi mchod gzhis sogs la log sgrub mang du mdzad par mngon
spyod kyi las sbyor gnang bas/ dus de skabs der thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgya mtsho 'ol kha rtser bzhugs yod pa mtshan ltas 'gyur te rgyal du phebs/ mi ring bar sde
pa sku rbab la shor ba'i rkyen gyis grongs/ thel pa rnams lhungs pa'i tshe bar snang khams nas bya rog cig gis phyag bcad nas khyer song ba yin zer ba'i thel gyi mgon khang
na da lta lag pa zhig ston rgyu yod skad/zhabs drung ngag dbang grags pa gong dkar na bzhugs skabs/ rtser yum mi gcig pa'i sku mched yod par brten/ dpon sa 'phyong rtse
mas gnang bkod ma legs pa'i zir bun bslangs te/ rin spungs pa dang dga' ldan pa sogs zhabs drung ngag dbang grags pa'i zhabs tog tu rtser dpung gi sbyor ba bshams/ hor
bsod nams dar rgyas sogs blon po gzhan rnams dpung khyer gyi phyogs lhung mngon tshan can med na'ang / gong ma chen pos bkra shis rtse par nang blon bcol bar ma rangs pa'i
bar zhugs khog nas rtser dpung gis bskor ma dgos pa'i ngos/ gong ma 'on rgyal bzang du phebs bcug nas/ zhabs drung ngag dbang grags pa rtse'i khri thog tu gdan drangs/
'on kyang 'brug pa sprul sku padma dkar pos sde dpon rnams la rgyu mtshan gnang yang zer/ gang ltar 'gyangs med du gong ma phyir rtser phebs/ zhabs drung ngag dbang grags

pa gong dkar du bzhugs pa la yang bskor rgyag cha grul che ba byung skabs gong dkar 'di dbus gtsang gnyis kyis mdud 'dzom pa'i lte ba lta bur 'dug pas rang re'i mi ngo zhig
gis ma bzung na bod kyi bde skyid la gnod pas rdzong gtod mi dgos tshul gyi gong ma'i bka' shog gong dkar du gnang ba bskor mi rnams kyi lag tu brgyab pas dmag rnams gyes
te bde 'jags che ba byung /zhabs drung ngag dbang grags pa 'di nyid kyis lugs zung gi mdzad pa mtha' yas shing / lhag par dge 'brug gnyis la thugs mos che bas dam pa'i
chos kyi gsan pa mang du mdzad/ sger du thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgya mtsho dang mchod yon nyi zla zung gcig lta bur thugs snang dag pa byung bas gong dkar du 'jam dbyangs
gong ma'i pho brang nas rten 'bul gyi rgyun 'dzugs pa gnang / gong ma chen po'i sras zur pa sogs kyis sne'u gdong rtse'i khrir bzhugs shing / bdud mi spun dgus dbus
gtsang lan mang du dkrugs pa'i sri ngan langs te/ byi glang sde gzar gyi skabs 'pho 'gyur shin tu che ba byung / zhabs drung ngag dbang grags pa la sras bka' brgyud rnam
par rgyal ba dang / rnam rgyal grags pa gnyis 'khrungs par gcung yar rgyab nas bdag mo byon skabs rigs 'dzin chen po'i rgyal sras padma chos rgyal dang / lha rtse ba gnyis
kyis srung 'khor mdzad dus/ rgyal sras pas thun brab sogs tsham rngam ha cang che bas bdag mo 'dzangs te 'byon ma nus par bgegs skrod kyi mtshams cung zad bzhag pas rten
'brel 'phyugs nas ma 'gyangs par zhabs drung rnam rgyal grags pa sku gshegs/ gcen bka' brgyud rnam par rgyal ba lugs zung gi mkhyen sgo yangs shing khyad par phyag rgya
chen po sogs nges don gyi skor la thugs gzhol/ 'di nyid kyi sras mi pham bsod nams dbang phyug grags pa rnam rgyal dpal bzang da lta pho brang sne'u gdong rtser bzhugs
skabs so//

smras pa/rmad byung rlangs kyi gser skyogs kyis bcus lha rigs bdud rtsi'i zil dngar can//mtho ris yon tan bdun gyi mnga' 'byor yul dbus sman ljongs yol go'i nang //'phyur bur
gtam pa'i rin cen gdung brgyud chos srid bla na dngar ba'i ro//gangs can ljongs 'di'i skye rgu me zhal yongs kyi dga' ston e ma mtshar//skye bas thob pa'i rigs gzugs chu
nang zla'i//sde gsum gcig tu dkar ba'i bsil zer gyis//nam mkha'i ri bong can de pham mo zhes//chu 'dzin lang long 'khrigs pas sgrib snyam byed//gnam bskos rgyal srid sA
la'i sdong po la//las kas mngon mtho'i stobs ldan yal ga'i tshogs//srid 'byor lo ma'i phang phung g.yo bzhin du//legs byas 'bras bu'i 'dod 'jo dpyid du dar//de ltar gong
ma sde srid kyi bka' khrims kyi shing rta chen po'i kha lo pa rnams las/! rin spungs ni/ sngon bod rje sha khri btsan po'i dus ma sangs la

khar khye'u mtshan dang ldan pa zhig byung bar sger dpal legs 'od nas bzung / phyi sger/ nang sger/ grub thob gyi sger dang gsum las/ rim bzhin mi rabs nyer lnga pa na nang
sger ral pa 'dzin gyis gru gu'i yul nas gzings bdun gyis rin po che g.yu'i zong drangs/ khrag gi lus la mgo lnga pa 'brug gi skad 'byin pa zhig rig sngags kyis btul bas
nus mthu che bar grags shing / phyag na padma mi rje'i tshul bzung ba srong btsan sgam po'i nang blon mdzad/de nyid kyi brgyud las blo gros kyi rtsal ldan zla ba rgyal mtshan
gyis mnga' bdag khri srong lde'u btsan gyi chos blon du gyur pa nas bzung mi rabs nyi shu'i mthar/ sger shAkya 'bum gyi sras nam mkha' rgyal mtshan gyis gong ma sde
srid dbang grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi zhabs la gtugs/ gzhis ka rin spungs kyi rdzong dpon/ chu mig gi khri dpon/ dpal ldan sa skya'i lha khang che mo'i dpon chen du bskos/
de'i sras nam mkha' rgyal po na tshod phra mo nas lugs gnyis kyi mkhyen pa'i spyan mchog tu yangs/ de'i sras nor bu bzang pos gong ma'i zhabs la gtugs shing / yab mes dus
kyi rdzong sdod khri dpon rnams kyi 'ja' sa gnang / dpung gi sbyor bas rta g.yag gi rdzong dang / lcags thag mgo sbrel du grags pa'i rgyal phran mang po'i mnga' 'bangs
rnams blangs/ nyang smad bsam 'grub rtse'i rdzong dpon mdzad/ gter ston kun skyong gling pas/ bstan ma gsol zhing rje yi mgur lha mchod/ / mi rabs bcu gsum bar du mi rabs
brtan/ / zhes pa'i lung bstan bzang po mdzad/ de nas rong byams chen gyi chos sde btab/ dge 'dun rnams la dbyar dgun dpyid chos kyi phogs sogs mthun rkyen gya nom pa sbyar/
sku gsung thugs kyi rten mang du bzhengs par paN chen nags kyi rin cen gyis me tog gtor/ brag dmar chos sde snying pa'i 'dabs su spyil po brgya lhag tsam brtsigs te thos
bsam sgom pa tshul bzhin du

byed pa'i 'dus grwa btsugs/ mdor na ris med pa'i grub pa'i mtha' thams cad la bsnyen bkur bla na med pa mdzad pas mngon par mtho/ chos rje bsod grags pas/ chos rje ngor chen
pas rin spungs nor bzang pa la/ rje dge 'dun grub kyis dgon pa 'debs pa 'gog dgos tshul gsungs pa ni ngag rgyun ma dag pa'i 'chal gtam zhig bris par snang ste/ thams cad
mkhyen pa dge 'dun grub kyis bkra shis lhun po 'debs skabs/ bsam 'grub rtse'i rdzong dpon 'phyong rgyas pa hor dpal 'byor bzang po yin zhing / 'di nyid kyis rje dge 'dun
grub kyi sbyin bdag gi mthil mdzad par ming tsam gyi mkhas pa ma yin pa'i grags pa don dang mthun pa'i paN chen byams pa gling pa bsod nams rnam par rgyal bas mdzad pa'i
yar rgyab kyi gdung rabs na gsal bar gsungs so//rin spungs nor bzang pa'i sras u pa si ka kun tu bzang po/ don grub rdo rje/ mtsho skyes rdo rje/ shAkya rgyal mtshan dang
lnga las/ dpon chung ngu nas grongs/ kun bzang pas dbang grags pa 'byung gnas sku mched kyi zhabs la gtugs/ yab mes kyi 'ja' sa las ka gnang ste rin spungs kyi rdzong
dpon mdzad/ dpal ldan sa skya pa'i rang lugs pa kun mkhyen sangs rgyas 'phel dang go rams bsod nams seng ge dang mchod yon du 'brel te 'bras yul skyed mos tshal gyi bshad
grwa btsugs shing / rta nag thub bstan rnam rgyal gyi dgon pa 'debs pa'i mthun rkyen mdzad/ don grub rdo rjes gzhis ka bsam 'grub rtse'i rdzong dpon gyi las ka bzung / ma
sangs mtsho skyes rdo rjes yar klungs mkhar thog gi rdzong bzung zhing spyan snga dpal ngag gi dbang phyug gshegs rjes gdung brgyud sku na ches phra bas/ pho brang sne'u
gdong rtser dpon tshab kyi thel gtong mdzad/ shAkya rgyal mtshan gyis nyang khog gi rdzong gzhis su bzhugs nas

bdag po rgyal mkhar rtse pa gtser ba sogs dgra thabs kyi bya ba la mkhas par grags/kun bzang pa la sras rdo rje tshe brtan dang / don yod rdo rje gnyis las/ don yod rdo rjes
rdzong chen gnyis kyi las kas mtho ba dang bcas dbus phyogs nor 'dzin gyi char dpung gi 'jug sgos gzhis ka brag dkar dang chu shul lhun po rtse sogs snel pa'i lag nas blangs/
mi ring bar 'phyong rgyas pa blon po gzhan rnams dang gros khog bstun pa'i spyan snga ngag gi dbang phyug pho brang sne'u gdong rtse'i khrir mnga' gsol ba'i byed po
mdzad/ la stod dang lho rgyud phyogs su dmag lan kha yar mdzad pa rnams rgyal zhing / de rjes spyan snga gong ma sku gshegs/ gdung brgyud rin po che nar ma son pa'i bar
du bag yangs pa dang / khyad par lta grub kyi kun slong drag po snying la gzir ba'i 'gro ba'i 'dren par rlom pa me tog mda' can gyi zhags pas bcings pa 'ga' zhig gis yid
rnam par bskyod pa la brten nas skyid shod phyogs su dpung 'jug byas par gdan sa chen po dga' ldan rnam par rgyal ba'i gling nas mkhas shing grub pa'i dbang phyug kun mkhyen
smon lam dpal bas mgon po phyag drug pa'i gtor chen gyi las sbyor mdzad par brten/ dmag lan gnyis rkyen gzhan gyi dbang gis phyir bzlog dgos pa byung / slar kun mkhyen
smon lam dpal ba sku gshegs pa'i gtam byung rjes dmag gi 'jug sgo byas pa dang / dga' ldan pa nam mkha' rgyal po ngo bltas pa sogs kyis sde gzar chabs su brgyugs te gzhis
ka sne'u rtsis len pa sogs mdzad/ 'on kyang gong ma chen po sne'u gdong rtse'i khri thog tu gdan 'dren par blon po gzhan rnams kyi grogs su 'gyur ba'i mdzad pas ngo tsha
khrel yod kyi gos dang ldan/ zhwa dmar chos kyi grags pa dang mchod yon bka' bgros nas yangs pa can gyi gtsug lag khang sde dang bcas

pa 'dzugs pa'i mthun rkyen mdzad/ rje drung chos grags rgya mtsho'i bzhed pa ltar lha ldan nye 'dabs su dgon pa btab na'ang / las 'bras kyi shugs 'di gang gis kyang dgag par
ma nus pas yun du ma gnas/ mtsho skyes rdo rje'i sras ngag dbang rnam rgyal gong ma spyan snga'i zhabs la gtugs nas rdzong dpon gyi las ka blangs/ rig gnas chung ba lnga
dang / sgyu rtsal drug cu rtsa bzhi sogs la blo gros kyi 'jug pa gsal bar shar/ e gnyal gyi phyogs su dmag gi mdzad sgo sogs la brten/ gong ma chen po'i thugs la phog par
rje 'bangs go rim ma log pa'i dgongs bsangs khengs dregs kyi dbang gis ma mdzad par brten/ dbus phyogs kyi sne'u sogs rdzong gzhis rnams shor te mnga' thang cung zad nyams/
'on kyang gtsang phyogs su seng ge rtse pa dang / la stod lho sogs 'og tu bcug byams chen gyis gtsos pa'i gtsang rong gi chos sde rnams la 'tsho rkyen sogs dge rgyun
bzang po sbyar/ rin spungs nyid du pho brang chen po'i mig ltos kyis gsang ba sngags kyi dus rim gyi srol btsugs/de nyid la sras gsum las/ che ba chung ngu nas grongs/
de 'og don grub tshe brtan rdo rjes sngar yab mes kyi dus ma lon pa'i pa snams lhun grub rtse'i rdzong mnga' 'bangs dang bcas pa rang dbang du byas/ rje drung mi bskyod rdo
rje'i gsung bzhin gsung rab gling gi dgon pa btab/ bkra shis dpal bzang bla mar bsten nas theg pa'i rtse mo nyams su blangs/ gcung ngag dbang 'jigs grags mkhyen rab kyi
klong rnam par yangs pas rig pa'i gnas che ba lnga dang chung ba lnga ste bcu phrag gcig la slob dpon mkhas pa bsten nas/ rgyal po paNDi ta'i rnam thar bzung / hor gos
bzang po'i rgyu las grub pa'i rigs ldan yol bar grags pa'i bkod pas khyad par du 'phags pa de nyid bzhengs/ rje kun dga' grol mchog pa rab gnas su spyan drangs/ daNDi'i dgongs
rgyan 'jigs

med sengge'i rgyud kyi nga ros thog drangs pa'i tshig sbyor phun sum tshogs pa'i bstan bcos kyi rtsom pa mang du mdzad/ lugs gnyis la rnam dpyod kyi sgo 'phar mchog tu yangs/
'on kyang phag tshang yos ltar dkrug pa'i lung bstan thog tu bab pa'i mtshan rtags kyis zhing gshag pas 'bangs gyen log byas skabs sras padma dkar po bkrongs pa'i gtam
byung ba/ rin cen spungs par dme 'khrug dar ba 'byung / / zhes pa'i dus su mngon/ sku tshe'i mjug tu mnga' thang phal cher shor/ sras zla ba bzang po'i brgyud deng sang
yang snang ngo // //! gong ma'i blon po hor gzhon nu bzang po ni/ za hor gyi rgyal rigs te/ grong khyer shing thabs can na rgyal po shing rta bcu pa zhes bya ba byung ba'i
sras chos rgyal mya ngan med ces bya ba bden tshig gi mthus mchod rten bye ba bzhengs pa/ de'i sras rgyal po dza zhes pa smon lam gyi mthus rdo rje sems dpa'i glegs bam
gyi char pho brang gi steng du babs pas mdo sde za ma tog rlung gis khyer te pho brang yom bu gla sgang gi steng du babs pa lha tho tho ri snyan shal gyi gnyan po gsang
bar btags la/ de'i sras za hor rgyal po indra bhU ti sngags la mos pas/ po ti gnyis phyag na rdo rje'i byin rlabs kyis rnyed kyang brda ma 'phrod pas grub thob ku ku rA dza
spyan drangs te smin par mdzad/ de la sras mo go ma de wa dang / sras sha kra gnyis kyis rig pa 'dzin pa'i sa grub cing / de'i sras rgyal po gtsug lag 'dzin bya ba slob
dpon chen po'i zab mo'i chos dang lung gis dbugs dbyung ba/ de la sras dharma rA dza/ mkhan chen zhi ba 'tsho/ lha lcam man dha ra ba gsum las/ bar pa gnas lnga rig pa'i
pha rol tu byon zhing / gangs can bstan pa'i rtsa lag mdzad/ phyi ma ye shes mkha' 'gro kun gyi gtso mor gyur/ dang pos rgyal srid bskyangs pa'i sras dharma pA la/ shAkya
de wa/ ma hA de wa gsum byung la/ de yang gangs can gyi ljongs

su mnga' bdag khri srong lde'u btsan gyis dpal bsam yas kyi gtsug lag khang bzhengs pa'i srung mar/ slob dpon chen pos klu zur phud lnga pa bka' bsgos pas/ nged kyis mi 'ongs/
za hor gyi yul na dmu'i rigs la klu'i tsha bo rgyal po hu zhes bya ba nor rgya khab tsam gyi rjes la bya rgod po'i nyin lam bco brgyad 'gro ba zhig yod pas de bsko bar
zhus pas/ rnam sras seng sngon can rta bdag brgyad dang bcas pa bkug nas gzugs brnyan bris pa'i ru dar la bstims nas/ khams kyi g.yer ma thang du dmag sgar btab/ slob dpon
chen pos ting nge 'dzin gyis pe dkar bkug nas lan cig bod du 'ongs kyang ha cang gdug rtsub che bar byung zhing / slar mkhan slob chos gsum gyis za hor du pho nya mngags
nas/ rgyal po dharma pA la/ g.yu'i thub pa rang byon/ zhal brnyan bse 'bag chibs shel gyi sengge dang bcas te sna drangs pas pe kar yang rin po ches spras pa'i shing
bya la zhon nas lha mi rnams bod du byon/ slob dpon chen pos spyi bor rdo rje bzhag ste dam tshig bsgrags/ deng sang yang rgyal po nges par brlams na spyi gtsug tu rdo rje'i
rjes yong / rnam sras sprin gseb ma'i lo rgyus dang pe dkar ar gtad kyi lo rgyus gnyis 'di dang gung 'grig par mngon/ dharma pA las mnga' bdag khri srong lde btsan gyi
bla ma mdzad/ dpal chu bo rir theg pa mchog gi rnal 'byor zab mo'i grub pa'i rtags khyad par can brnyes/ des pho yong bza' bya ba mkha' 'gro'i rigs can zhig khab tu bzhes
pa'i sras dpal gyi rdo rje dang rin cen rdo rje gnyis las/ gcung rgya gar du byon/ thos bsam sgom pa mang du mdzad/ si ta'i grong khyer du sku lus ma spangs par mkha'
spyod du gshegs/ dpal gyi rdo rjes pa tshab kyi rigs kyi jo mo zhig blangs par sras rdo rje grags pa/ rin cen grags pa/ chos kyi grags pa gsum las/ gcung ni rab tu byung
/ gcen gyis sgrub pa mdzad pas yi

dam gyi lha mang po zhal gzigs/ zhing skyes kyi DA kI zhig phyag rgyar bsten pas sras zla ba grags pa/ de'i sras rig pa seng ge/ de la sras shAkya blo gros/ yon tan blo gros/
grags pa ye shes gsum gyis g.yon ru sa'i lte ba yar klungs su phebs/ gcen gyi g.yon ru khra 'brug dang khad nye ba'i g.yu srid smon mkhar du bzhugs/ 'bring ba gnam lde
'od srungs kyi bla ma mdzad nas mkhar thog btab/ chung bas lha sman jo mos sa skyong ba'i phyogs su lha khang btab nas bzhugs/ 'ga' zhig bye sa lha khang yin zer/ yon tan
blo grosakyi sras rdo rje gsal ba dang rdo rje rin cen gnyis/ 'di'i dus rgya dang shar ga bya dang rngog khu dang dpus dkar sogs rus chen gyi 'bangs mang du byung / gcen
gyi sras ye shes rdo rje/ des g.yu ru nam mkha' ri khu mo skyid khab tu bzhes pa la sras mo zhig las ma 'khrungs par mkhar thog dang bcag gnas rgya la byin pas pho brang
rgya'i mkhar thog tu ming chags/ rin cen rdo rje mnga' bdag dpal 'khor btsan gyis gdan drangs/ phu lung 'di ngan lam rgya mtsho dang gtsang pa mi bdun du grags pa'i rigs
sngags pas kyang ma thul tshul zhus nas/ gser gyi phyags shing khru do pa zhig phul/ bla mchod du bkur bas phu lung gi lha 'dre rnams btul/ der dgon pa stegs kha mo btab/
jo mo mchil mo zhig khab tu bzhes par sras rdo rje grags pa dang rdo rje 'bar ba gnyis 'khrungs/ yab sras gsum gyis hor pa sar byon/ sgang kha spel zhes bya ba'i pho brang
zhig btab/ rgya gar gyi srol bzhin sras che ba khang pa phyi mar phog pas sras khang phyi par grags/ rdo rje 'bar klu sdings su phog pas sras lcang ldur bar grags/ mched
gnyis kyis g.yu srid kun dga' bar sa dpyad legs par mkhyen nas phyag phab/ yab bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i mtshan rdo rje rgyal por gsol/ rdo rje 'bar ba la sras hor da dar
ba zhes bya ba sbas pa'i rnal 'byor

nus mthu'i mnga' bdag chen po zhig byung bas/ hor se chen rgyal pos gsan nas gser yig pa mngags te spyan drangs kyang / thabs mkhas kyi mdzad pas btul te ma phebs/ de'i sras
hor bkra shis 'bum dang mkhan chen tshul dar ba gnyis las/ mkhan chen pa dpal ldan rlangs kyi gdung las/ spyan snga bcu gnyis rin po cher so sor thar pa'i sdom pa mnos/
bka' brgyud rin po che'i zab chos mang du gsan zhing / spyan snga grags pa shes rab dang / ta'i si tu byang chub rgyal mtshan gnyis kyi dbu skra'i phud bzhes te bla ma mdzad/hor
bkra shis 'bum la sras gzhon nu bzang po dang bkra shis bsam grub/ gnyis kas gong ma si tu'i zhabs la gtugs/ khyad par gcen gyi gsol ja ba nas bzung bka' blon gyi
bar las tshan rim par mdzad/ dpon chen rgyal bzang pas si tu btson du bzung ba'i skabs/ dmag gis bsdigs pa'i bskor g.yang mang du byas kyang sne'u gdong rtser 'khra phur
bzung zhing / dpon chen dbang brtson gyis khri bskor bcu gsum gyi dmag yar klungs su bteg pa dus kyi me lce'i 'phreng ba la phye ma leb mchongs pa'i ngang tshul bzhin bcom
pas/ stobs 'byor gyi dregs pas myos pa'i sa skya'i dpon chen kyang spa bkong bar mdzad pa sogs kyis sde srid phag mo gru pa'i bstan jus tshugs pa'i rtsa ba lta bur byung
bas/ si tus/ gzhon nus snying bgyis/ gzhan rnams yan lag gi tshul bgyis zhes dang / gzhan yang ya gi gtsang sa skya nas smad 'jang zhabs lho mon dang bcas pa mnga' 'og
tu 'du ba gzhon nu bzang po'i drin yin gsungs/ gcung bkras bsam pa'i sras gzhon nu rgyal mtshan/ kun dga' dpal bzang / nam mkha' rin cen/ dbang phyug rin cen dang bzhi
byung ba rnams kyis spyan snga rin po che dang gong ma si tu'i zhabs la gtugs/ rgyal srid skyong ba'i blon po'i bya ba rnams gong sa'i dgongs pa dang bstun par

mdzad do//kun dga' dpal bzang gi sras dpal 'byor bzang po/ bsod nams dpal ldan/ sangs rgyas skyabs/ dkon cog rin cen bzhi 'khrungs/ dpal 'byor bzang pos tshes bzhi gsar ma
ba'i zhabs la gtugs/ nyang smad bsam 'grub rtse'i rdzong dpon dang / phyis su dmag dpon la bskos pas dgra sha drod ma yal bar blangs pas srin po yang byin sha 'dar zhes dpa'
rtags byung / thams cad mkhyen pa dge 'dun grub dang mchod yon du 'brel bas/ rgyal ba gnyis pa btsong kha pa'i ring lugs la mos pa thob/ bsam rtse na kun mkhyen bu'i
phyag bris dang phyag rtags 'byar ba'i bka' 'gyur bzhugs pa phying bar stag rtser gdan drangs/ gcung gsum gyi sa skyong grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi zhabs la gtugs/ khyad par
nang so dkon cog rin cen gong ma'i lugs gnyis kyi mdzad pa mtha' dag spel ba'i nang blon mdzad/ bod kyi blon po rig pa can rgyud mar 'byung ba'i rten 'brel gyi ri bo'i
'dabs rol tu phying bar stag rtse'i btsan rdzongs lha'i grong khyer mi yul du 'phos pa lta bur yid du 'ong ba brtsigs/ de'i skabs sras nyag phra bar byung bas/ gdan sa chen
po dga' ldan rnam par rgyal ba'i gling nas chos rje zhwa lu pa legs pa rgyal mtshan gdan drangs/ gshed dmar gyi sgo nas rigs bskrun pa'i cho ga mdzad pas hor rdo rje tshe
brtan 'khrungs/ skabs shig lha mo 'od zer can ma'i las tshogs la brten nas/ rgya khab rtser brgyus dgra phyogs su bstan pas dmag dpung chen por mthong ba dang / rdzong
la chu med par dbyangs 'char gyi sgo nas lu ma bton pa sogs bka' drin che bas dga' ldan dos skyel du grags pa zhal ngo rim par mdzad/hor rdo rje tshe brtan dbang grags
pa 'byung gnas sku mched kyi zhabs la gtugs nas bka' khrims sgyur ba'i blon po mdzad/ phying bar stag rtse'i ri

glang po che lta bu'i ngos su ri bo bde chen gyi gtsug lag khang rten dang brten par bcas pa bzhengs/ thon mi sa mbho Ta'i gdung las gnas lnga rig pa'i paNDi ta chen po byams
pa gling pa bsod nams rnam par rgyal ba mi pham dga' ba'i bshes gnyen spyan drangs nas rab tu gnas pa mdzad/ 'phags pa'i yul gyi mkhas grub rnams kyi gsung gangs can gyi
ljongs 'dir 'gyur ba'i glegs bam rnams kyi steng du/ rgyal ba btsong kha pa chen po'i gsung 'bum po ti bcu drug bsnan pa'i pusta ka mkha' mda' mig gi grangs ldan bzhugs
shing / bstan 'gyur snga ma rnams la med pa'i skad gnyis smra ba'i dbang po zha lu lo chen gyis bsgyur ba'i mngon pa'i 'grel pa gnam lcags thog gzer yang yod do/ /mched
rnams kyi sras/ tshe dbang rnam rgyal dang rin cen rgyal mchog gnyis las gcen ni rig pa'i gnas bco brgyad dang sgyu rtsal drug cu rtsa bzhi la mkhas par byung zhing / hor
rin cen rgyal mchog ni srid zhi'i yon tan nor bu'i 'phreng ba mgrin pa'i do shal du spud cing / dpa' mdzangs rtul phod sogs lugs gnyis kyi bla na mtho ba'i gong ma chen
pos thugs shin tu 'jog pa'a'i blon po rnams kyi gtso bo lta bur gyur/ gong ma'i bka' shog hung rgya ma'i nang du/ dbus gtsang gi chings kyi skor la gnas tshul dri bar btang
'dug pa/ 'di tshor che chung ji 'dra zhig byed kyang khyod rang la 'dri ba las 'os med pas sgo gang zab kyi thag de kha nas chod gsung ba sogs rgyal po las blon po gtso
ba'i gtam phyag len du mdzad/ srong btsan gzhis kar zhwa dmar chos kyi grags pa spyan drangs/ yangs pa can gyi chos sder mchod gzhis sogs kyi mthun rkyen gong sar zhu
ba gnang / bde skyid gling du spyan snga bka' brgyud bris 'bur dang / bka' 'bum yongs rdzogs gser gyis 'dri ba gnang / jo mo la bsam yas rgyal po'i gnod pa byung bar/ gsol
kha bshol nas ar la gtad

pas chos skyong gi tshur btud de/ dngos grub ster bar gsungs pa bzhin nyi ma gcig la rdzong bcu gsum blangs/ dbus gtsang gi chings bdag mdzad pas/ gram pa shar/ stod lung rmad
sogs smyu gu mchu rin la bzhes/de'i sras bsod nams mgon po/ tshe dbang bkra shis/ rin cen tshe brtan rnams las/ gcen gong ma'i thugs la btags pas dmag dpon gyi las ka
bzung / skyid shod dpal 'byor lhun po thab skyong la gnang / 'bring po 'jigs pa med pa dpa' bo'i dbang phyug ste/ rgyal po rA ma Na ltar dgra thabs la mkhas pas yan lag
rnam bzhi'i khyu mchog yin la/ chung ba yang rnam dpyod zla ba gsar pa'i ngos su gtsug lag ri dwags kyi gzugs brnyan 'char ba zhig go/ mched rnams la bya bkra shis dar rgyas
kyi sras mo don yod sgrol ma jo mor bzhes par sras hor bsod nams dar rgyas dang / don grub rdo rje gnyis las/ gcen lugs gnyis kyi gtsug lag mtha' dag la mkhyen pa'i spyan
dang ldan zhing / khyad par bka' brgyud karma kaM tshang gi ring lugs pa don dang mthun pa'i mkhas pa'i dbang po dpal khang lo tsA ba'i drung du thun mong ba'i rig pa'i
gnas mtha' dag la phul du byung ba'i sbyangs pa mdzad/ thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgya mtsho gdan drangs te dam pa'i chos kyi bgo skal stsal/ gcung 'khor ba'i phun
tshog mtha' dag chu shing gi snying po ltar gzigs te/ sdom gsum rim gyis mnos pa'i grub pa'i dbang phyug chen por gyur/hor bsod pa'i jo mor dga' ldan pa sa skyong bkra shis
rab brtan gyi lcam sring tshe dbang rgyal mo blangs par sras bsod nams stobs kyi rgyal po/ tshe dbang bsod nams bstan 'dzin/ karma ngag dbang grags pa gsum gyi che ba
phun sum tshogs pa'i gzi brjid kyis nam mkha'i nor bu la skyengs pa ster bar nus la/ g.yul ngor chas pa'i drag shul gyis thob rgya lha rtse'i rdzong mnga'

zhabs dang bcas pa chab 'og tu btsud/ dus gsum mkhyen pa mtsho skyes rdo rje'i ring lugs pa slob dpon bai ro tsa na'i thugs sprul gter ston shes rab 'od zer ti shrir bsten
nas/ sa 'dzin dpal gyi ri la theg mchog sgrub pa'i 'dus sde btab/ sher phyin sum brgya pa/ shel brag gi thang yig sems nyid ngal gso rnams par du bzhengs/ 'brug nas sprul
pa'i sku kun mkhyen ngag dbang nor bu sogs dam pa du ma la phu dud mdzad/ dkar phyogs rdzogs pa gnyis pa'i tshes la dpa' bo mkha' 'gro'i dga' ston spros bcas dang spros
med kyi zlos gar le'u brgyad pa'i cho ga bsgrigs bzhin btsugs/ gdan sa chen po ri bo dga' ldan gyi shar pa chos rje nam mkha' rgyal mtshan zhes rig pa'i gnas lnga la ma rmongs
pa'i mkhas pa de spyan drangs nas ri bo bde chen ser khyim pa lta bur song ba slar gtsang dgon mdzad/ 'bring pos rgyal ba'i bstan pa spyi dang / khyad par chos kyi
rgyal po btsong kha pa chen po'i bstan pa la rmad du byung ba'i bkur sti dang phud dud mdzad/ chung ba gtsug lag rtsis kyi gzhung lugs la mkhyen pa'i spyan yangs so// mched
rnams la jo mo 'od gsal lha'i gdung brgyud mi dbang byams pa rab brtan gyi sras mo don grub blangs par sras ngag gi dbang phyug mched gnyis dang lcam gsum 'khrungs/ dang
po ni/ lhums su zhugs pa'i skabs mtshan ma khyad par can mang du byung zhing / lugs gnyis la mkhyen pa'i spyan yangs/ 'chi med grub pa'i ring lugs pa chos rgyal khri srong
lde'u btsan gyi yon tan gyi sprul pa byang pa bdag chen ti shrir bsten/ khyad par gsang chen rdo rje theg pa la rtsal du thon pas rim gnyis kyi rnal 'byor zab mo la
thugs dam gyi mthil du mdzad/ yi dam dang chos srung gi gnang ba thob pas lha srin bran du 'khol nus pa'i mthu stobs dbang phyug gi snyan pa che zhing /

stag rtse la zhugs kyi gnod pa byung skabs/ sngags chas kyi na bza' skor rnams ma tshig cing / zhal dkar ma chag pa sogs byin rlabs dang thugs rje'i ngo mtshar bla lhag tu
che/ me'i gnod pa 'di yang / rig pa 'dzin pa'i dbang phyug 'di nyid za hor rgyal po gtsug lag 'dzin gyi skye ba'i mtha' ma yin pas las kyi rnam par smin pa'i mtha' brtul/
padma 'od kyi gzhal yas su thegs khar/ drung 'khor 'ga' zhig la slob dpon chen po'i rnam thar zhal thang gra tshar khrod nas gang zin pa zhig khyer shog gsung ba ltar phyag
tu phul bas/ slob dpon rgyal srid spangs nas brtul zhugs kyi spyod pa mdzad pa'i thad der byung ba nas/ da bu chung gis kyang sde srid 'di zin pa zhig mi 'ong bar 'dug
gsung ba sogs ma 'ongs pa mngon sum du mkhyen pa'i bka' stsal to/ / gcung ni thun mong ba'i gtsug lag rnams la blo gros kyi pad dkar rnam par spro zhing / mchod sbyin brgya
pa'i dpung tshogs rtsub 'gyur gyi tshul du sleb pa lta bur shugs drag dmag gis sbyor ba la snying stobs kyi go cha btsan po gyon pa zhig ste/ mched gnyis sras dang bcas
pa rim par byon no// //! ta'i si tu'i blon po drung chen grags pa bzang po ni/ chos rgyal khri srong lde'u btsan gyi dus mkhan slob rnam gnyis kyi slob ma grub pa'i dbang
phyug nyang ting 'dzin bzang po'i gdung las rim par brgyud de/ btsan thang shar phyogs su nyang grags pa bzang po 'khrungs/ gong ma ta'i si tu'i zhabs la gtugs te 'ol
kha stag rtse'i rdzong dpon mdzad/ de'i sras btsan thang sgom grags dang sgom she gnyis kyis yar klungs mgo nag gi sras mo bkra shis skyid mo jo mor blangs pa la sras drung
chen shes rab bkra shis/ kun grags pa/ kun dbang pa gsum las/ 'bring pos 'ol kha stag rtse'i rdzong dpon dang / chung bas rtses thang du slob gnyer mdzad/ shes rab bkra
shis gong ma'i zhabs

la gtugs/ sa skya pa bla ma kun dga' rgyal mtshan dang / tshal pa/ g.ya' bzang pa sogs kyis hor rgyal po la zhu log phul bas/ dgongs pa dag byed kyi rgyu mtshan 'bul bar sher
bkras pas lus srog la bltos pa med par hor rgyal po tho gan thi mur gyi drung du byon/ rgyu mtshan 'bul mkhas pas 'phral yun du phan pa'i 'ja' sa 'grub/ sde srid kyi zhabs
tog tu 'gyur ba byung bar dpags/ gzhis ka brag dkar khyod shes rab bkra shis mi brgyud dang bcas pas shes su chug gi bka' shog gnang /de'i sras drung rin cen dpal dang
/ dge slong gnyis las/ che ba la gong ma chos rgyal chen pos rdzong dpon gyi las ka gnang / rgyal ba btsong kha pa chen po'i sbyin bdag gi mthil len mdzad nas/ ri bo dga'
ldan gyi dgon pa 'debs pa'i mthun rkyen snga phyir bsgrubs/ de la 'phyong rgyas nas jo mo sangs rgyas ma blangs par sras rin cen lhun po/ lhun grub pa/ grags pa rgyal
mtshan/ dngos grub/ kun dga' 'dzom pa rnams las/ che ba gong ma chen pos rdzong dpon du bsko bzhag gnang / ri bo dga' ldan gyi rtsa ba'i sbyin bdag mdzad/ de 'og gong ma'i
gsol dpon gyi las ka bzung / de 'og rab tu byung ste gsung rab la sbyangs nas se ra theg chen gling gi gdan sa mdzad/ de 'og chos sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan gyi gsol dpon
dang / de 'og gong ma kun dga' legs pas rdzong dpon gyi las ka gnang / mched rnams la gzhis ka rin spungs nas sras mo lha mo chos skyong jo mor blangs pa la/ nang so dkon
cog pa dang sri chod rgyal po gnyis las/ che bas rab tu byung / chung ba la tshes gnyis rin po ches rdzong dpon gyi las ka gnang / gnas rnying kun dga' bde legs dang /
chos rje smon lam dpal ba sogs mkhas pa rnams la dam pa'i chos kyi gsan pa mang du mdzad/ de la rgya ma pa'i sras mo bu khrid khab tu bzhes pa la/ nang so

'jam dpal tshe ring / bdud 'dul rgyal po/ ma zhig pa/ bsod nams rgyal po/ lcam gnyis dang drug las/ 'jam dpal ba'i jo mor yar rgyab nas tshe ring dpal 'dzom blangs par/ sras
tshe brtan rdo rjes rdzong dpon gyi las ka bzung / chab srid bskyangs so//! gzhis ka snel pa ni/ chen po rin cen bzang pos gong ma si tu'i zhabs la gtugs/ sa skyar dmag
la 'byon skabs/ si tus phag gru'i khri dmag rnams kyis chen po la phyag 'tshal dgos pa sogs gsungs nas dpon tshab tu bskos/ dus der dpon chen bzung ba sogs jus kyi 'gro
khyab che ba byung / sa skya pa dang hor rgyal po mchod yon du 'brel ba'i dus kyi nor sna khyad 'phags rnams dbus su drangs/ dpon chen rnams kyis gtsos pa'i gzhan sde rnams
la khrims ra nyi ma bcu gsum bsgyur cing bya khra ma'i steng du mi lnga brgya tsam khrims la sbyar ba'i drag shul gyis 'bod grogs kyang 'dar/ skam po grong du sger gzhis
kyi mkhar las mdzad/ bya sar sger gru btsugs/ yon bdag blo bde'i sras mo bde skyid/ khams mo/ dpon mo dpal ldan 'bum gsum jo mor blangs pa las/ dang po la rgyal ba rin
cen/ drung nam mkha' bzang po/ gnyis pa la dpon shag pa/ gsum pa la dpal ldan chos skyong dang / bsod nams bzang po 'khrungs/dpal ldan chos skyong gis nyang smad bsam 'grub
rtse'i rdzong dpon thog cig mdzad/ drung chen dpon grags pas gong ma'i zhabs la gtugs/ spyan snga grags pa byang chub dang / rdzong byi rgyal mtshan bzang po dpon blon
bka' bgros thog sne'u'i rdzong dpon du bskos/ gong dkar nas sgom log chos rgyal gcung po rtses thang dge bsnyen dang / pa sde mkhan pos gtsos pa'i dmag gi sbyor ba bshams
pa mtsho sna gdong du slebs skabs/ dpon grags pa rang gis

dmag dpon mdzad nas 'khrugs pas rgyal te/ pa sde mkhan pos gtsos pa'i mi drug cu tsam lnga pa'i lam du btang / de rjes stong pa 'jam dpal gyi thog tu dpung bteg gnya' gnan
du gzhis ka smon mkhar brtsigs/ lha ldan sprul pa'i gtsug lag khang gi gyo thog rdo gcal gsar rjes khyams ra dang / bar bskor gyi thog 'bubs/ ldeb bris/ gong ma si tu'i dgongs
rdzogs su/ chos rdzong / bkra shis sgang / brag nag dbus gling sogs skyid shod stod smad kyi sngags grwa rnams su dkyil 'khor sgrub mchod btsugs/ byams pa chos 'khor
gyi drung du dge 'dun bzhi sdes byams pas dam bcas pa'i gzungs smon lam dang bcas pa'i rgyun/ dung mtshor sngar dung mtsho ras pas ngan slong la skyo tshul btsugs pa bar
skabs su chad pa gser bre'i nas khal lnga bcu lnga bcus lo ltar du gsos/ chen po rin bzang pa yab yum/ rgyal ba rin chen sku mched kyi sgrib sbyong la/ jo bo rnam gnyis
drung du sman bla 'don pa'i rgyun/ gsang ne'u thog sogs dge 'dun gyi sde rnams su mthun rkyen sbyor ba sogs rnam dkar gyi las gcig tu de che/drung chen nam mkha' bzang po
gong ma'i lung gis sne'u'i rdzong dpon du byon/ rgyal ba btsong kha pa yab sras la rtsa ba'i bla mar mdzad/ khyad par dpal ldan 'bras spungs kyi chos sde chen po 'debs
pa'i mthun rkyen phul du byung ba dang / rta chen gyi zla ba'i cho 'phrul gyi dus khyad par can la 'gro ba'i bsod nams ma smad par bskrun pa'i thabs dam pa lha sa smon lam
chen mo 'dzugs pa'i mthil len mdzad/ 'di nyid kyis lcam rin cen sgrol ma jo mor blangs bar/ drung chen nam mkha' dpal 'byor 'khrungs/ gong ma grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis
rdzong dpon gyi las ka gnang / gser gyi bka' 'gyur bzheng ba dang / 'phrul snang gtsug lag khang rten dang brten par bcas pa'i zhabs tog

dpal ldan 'bras spungs kyi chos sde chen po'i mjug chags rnams mdzad/ dpon grags pas tshal pa dpon mo jo mor blangs pa'i sras/ drung chen grags pa dpal bzang gis gong ma grags
'byung ba'i zhabs la gtugs/ stag sna'i dmag res byes gnyer dang / khrims las/ gsol dpon sogs las tshan rim par mdzad/ rgyal mkhar rtse'i sras mo skal bzang ma jo mor
blangs kyang / bar skabs su re dogs ci rigs la brten rab tu byung / slar hor chas su bsgyur nas gong sas du dben shri'i las ka gnang / byang sbra thag 'then tshad kyi dpon
du bskos/ rin spungs pa la mdzo rir jus nyes chen po btang bas dpa' grags che/ de'i sras drung chen dpal 'byor rgyal po/ dbang grags 'byung ba sku mched kyis rdzong dpon
gyi las ka gnang/ bstan pa spyi dang khyad par rgyal ba btsong kha pa'i bstan pa la phul du byung ba'i bsti stang mdzad/ mnga' thang yang shin tu mtho bas/ 'bri grung rdo
tham man/ kha rag rdo bug pa can yan/ yar klungs khra 'brug tshun zhes lam yig mdzad skad/ 'di nyid kyi sras/ ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal po/ ngag dbang bsod nams lhun
po/ ngag dbang bsod nams rnam rgyal gsum las/ dang po chung ngu la grongs/ phyi ma gnyis kyi dus rin spung don yod rdo rjes dpung gi sbyor bas mnga' thang rnams shor ro//
//rgyal mkhar rtse pa ni/ sngon 'dod khams stod du dgra rgod ldang btsan bya ba/ stag lpags brgya'i thul pa gyon pa/ dred la sbar 'dzin byed pa/ khrom ge sar rgyal po'i
mag pa byas pa'i bu tsha brgyud/ yon bdag 'bum nyeg bya ba'i sras slob dpon nam mkha' byang chub bya ba gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa'i sgo nas grub pa brnyes pa zhig gi sras
slob dpon nam mkha' lhun grub/ de'i sras slon dpon nam mkha' bzang po/ de la sras brtson 'grus rdo rje/

grags pa brtson 'grus/ gzhon nu 'phags gsum las/ che bas snar thang du rab tu byung / chung bas ti ri grags 'od pa'i yig dpon mdzad/ bar pa la sras rgyal mtshan yig ris mang
du mkhyen/ 'di nyid kyis brtsams pa'i bka' pota yang snang / 'di chos rje karma pa dang thugs 'brel che bas/ mtshur phu'i byang chub chen po bzheng bar byon skabs/ bzo
rgyus ldangs na kho bos mdun gyi nags ri 'di tsam blor shong zhus pas/ sprul sku nags ri par grags/ 'dis ma gcig lha sman jo mor blangs par sras dpal ldan bzang po/ dpal
ldan rin cen/ ma zangs dar po gsum 'khrungs/ nyang stod 'dul chung chu nub kyi nang tshan/ lhan yul sngon mo lung rings su byon pa'i lam khar lcags pa'i gdung brgyud 'phags
pa rgyal la dang mjal te ming zhus pas/ gcen gnyis la 'phags pa dpal bzang dang / 'phags pa rin cen du btags/'phags pa dpal bzang gis dpal ldan sa skya pa'i las tshan
bzung / gtam yig rtsis gsum/ mda' kha dpa' rtsal dang ldan pa'i shar dung lho dung 'dul ba'i rgan por sa skya nas bskon cha dang bcwa tshe gnang / de nas bzhi thog nye gnas
kyi go sa bzung / pa shi da ra kha che shar phyogs gong ma'i drung du brdzangs pas/ 'dri mtshams gangs dkar po tshun shes su bcug pa'i 'ja' sa gnang / gong ma si tu'i
drung du byon par/ slob dpon nam rgyal/ sher bzang / pa shi dkon cog rnams kyis rin spungs su bsgar nas/ grwa tshong 'dus su bskyal te ngam gcur byas pa las grol te yar byon
skabs/ hor rgyal pos nang chen gyi 'ja' sa gnang / rtse chen dang phag ri rnam rgyal gyi rdzong brtsigs/ rgyal rtse/ sna bo rdzong gnyis nyi ma gcig la 'gram btings/
khyung rtse sogs rdzong mang du brtsigs/ rtse chen gtsug lag khang btab/bdag chen 'phags pa dpal la sras mang du yod kyang / jo mo ma

gcig dpal ma la nang chen kun dga' 'phags 'khrungs/ de la sras dpon mo mgon po sogs sras lcam sring mang du 'khrungs pa las/ bdag chen rab brtan kun bzang 'phags 'di nyid pho
brang sne'u gdong rtser gong ma grags pa rgyal mtshan pa'i drung du byon/ gong mas sne'u gdong dga' ldan rtse'i rten gsum rnams kyi nang nas dpon rab brtan dang ji ltar
'dod pa zhig khyer gsungs pas/ thub dbang rdo rje gdan chung ma zhig zhus pas/ thugs nyams che ba'i grags pa byung / deng sang yang rgyal rtse'i li ma lha khang du bzhugs
yod 'dug cing / gtsang du byon nas grogs po brgya rtsar rin spungs nam mkha' rgyal po'i dpung rnams spub ste mtshan jus legs pa byung / mkhas grub rin po che dang mchod
yon du 'brel nas/ dpal 'khor bde chen gyi gtsug lag khang sde dang bcas pa btab/ sngags grwa pa rnams kyis dkyil 'khor mang po'i zhal 'byed dang / mdo grwa pa rnams kyis
dbyar chos thog bka' pota rnams la rab 'byams grwa bskor gyi rgyun srol btsugs/ sku 'bum bkra shis sgo mang dang gos sku chen mo/ bka' 'gyur rgyun 'jags su bzheng ba sogs
dbus gtsang gi sde dpon zhig la rnam dkar gyi mdzad pa 'di nyid che bar mngon/ 'di'i sras rab brtan bkra shis 'phags/ de'i sras don grub 'phags nas bzung ste bdag po phun
sum pa yan chad du mnga' thang rgyun gnas shing / bar skabs su dus mi bde ba 'ga' zhig byung yang / gong ma sde srid nas rgyab gnyer mdzad pas skyon du ma gyur to// //!
sde pa 'ol kha ba ni/ drung chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan la sde srid gong ma grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis rdzong dpon gyi las ka gnang / chos rje bzang skyong pas nyi ma
gling gi dgon pa 'debs pa'i sbyin bdag gi mthil mdzad/ rin po che'i khu bas bris pa'i bde bar gshegs pa'i bka'i glegs bu kha bas bskor

ba'i ljongs su 'gyur ro cog bzheng ba sogs sku tshe'i stod la rgyal srid chos bzhin du bskyangs shing / rjes su rigs kyi sras nar son pa dang / chos rje rgyal tshab pa'i drung
du bstan pa'i rtsa ba so sor thar pa'i sdom pa mnos/ 'ol kha dge sbyong chen por skye bo rnams gleng / de rjes nor bzang pa dang / rgya mtsho ba mched kyis srid bskyangs
shing sde pa rgya mtsho ba la gong ma chen pos dmag dpon gyi las ka gnang bas/ gzhan sde 'joms pa la snying stobs kyi rtsal dang ldan skad/de nas mkhan chen pas mchod
khang dang / rje btsun mi pham mgon po'i sku'i snang brnyan bzheng ba sogs gong ma'i rgyun bzang po bzung / de rjes don yod rnam rgyal rdo rjes/ mkhas shing grub pa'i dbang
phyug rje btsun nor bzang rgya mtsho zhes dang po'i sangs rgyas dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i gzhung lugs sngon chad gangs can pa rnams kyis ma rtogs pa dang log par rtogs
pa'i the tshom gyi dra ba mtha' dag drung nas 'byin pa'i shing rte chen po pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa dge 'dun rgya mtsho rnams la gus mchod lhur len zhing / khyad par
gsang ba mkha' 'gro'i sbas pa'i bsti gnas chos 'khor rgyal gyi 'dus sde rten dang brten par bcas pa la 'tsho ba'i yo byad bzang po gong 'phel du sbyar ba sogs dge ba'i las
kyi shugs zad pa med pa'i ral gris mu mtha' med pa'i 'khor ba nags klung stug po'i mtha' dbral te/ sras phun tshogs rab brtan gshegs par brten/ zhal ngo'i brgyud ring
bar ma byung yang / phyis su 'od gsal lha las babs pa'i sa skyong ba dang khyon gcig par gyur to// //! yar rgyab pa ni/ chos kyi rgyal po srong btsan sgam po'i blon po thon
mi sambho Ta zhes bya ba 'jam dbyangs kyi rnam par sprul pa/ sngar bod du yi ge'i srol med pa la/ rgya yig lnga bcu tham pa bod yig sum cur gtan la 'bebs pa'i

shing rta chen po de nyid kyi gdung brgyud yin la/ kha cig bho Ta zhes smra ba ni mi rigs par saM bha drar 'dod pa mchis na'ang sambho Ta zhes gangs ris bskor ba'i ljongs 'dir
legs par sbyar ba lha'i skad smra ba la 'gran pa'i zla thams cad dang bral ba zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba chen po zha lu ba chos skyong bzang pos mdzad pa'i brda sprod pa'i
bstan bcos za ma tog tu/ gangs can khrod pa'i bla ma mchog / sambho Ta zhes rab grags pa'i// zhes gsungs pas so/ / chos blon chen po 'di nyid kyi sras ma hA sa twa/ de'i
sras ye nag de'i sras nyi ma klong gsal/ de'i sras ber nag can/ de'i sras mon mo/ de'i sras gtso bo lha sras/ 'di rnams dgung lo brgya lhag tsam bzhugs pa sha stag byung
/ de'i sras bsod nams rgyal po/ de'i sras rgyal po dga'/ de'i sras rta mgrin rgyal mtshan/ de'i sras rdo rje bkra shis/ 'dis dpal ldan sa skyar ti shri kun blo'i zhabs
la gtugs/ de nyid kyi hor rgyal po'i drung du brdzangs pas/ du dben shri'i bya las chen po gnang /de'i sras dpon bzhi 'dzom/ gong ma grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis gzhis ka gong
dkar gyi rdzong dpon la bskos/ de'i sras rgyal ba shes rab/ de'i sras dpon chen gral lnga/ 'di nyid kyis sku tshe'i stod la gong ma grags pa 'byung gnas kyis yar rgyab
dpon chen dang gong dkar rdzong dpon gyi las ka gnang / 'on kyang sprul pa'i gang zag khyad par du 'phags pa yin pas/ sku tshe'i smad la rab tu byung ste gsang ba sngags
kyi chos sde gong dkar rdo rje gdan du grags pa'i ngo mtshar can de btab/ 'di nyid kyi dbon sras nas bzung ste/ sde pa rnam rgyal ba sku mched kyi bar du mnga' thang yar
rgyas su gnas so// //! bya pa khri dpon ni/ yul yar klungs kyi smad/ ma yul ljongs kyi 'dabs su bya'i rgyal po gshog bzang dang 'dab bzang gi rigs las mched pa

mang du byung bas bya pa zhes grags la/ yar klungs mthil du rnam smin bskyed pa yi/ / glo bur rgyal po bya mig mas kyis 'gebs/ / zhes pa'i lung bstan du gleng / yul der bya
chos kyi ka ba dang / gcung thod pa g.yu'i smin ma can mched gnyis las/ chung ba'i sras mkhan po yon tan mchog dang / bya sha ka gnyis 'khrungs pas/ gcen gyis 'bring sde
la rab tu byung / e nas klogs/ byar nas shar mda'/ dwags po nas grom mda'/ gnyal nas srin mo mig rnams bzung / bya sha ka la sras rdo rje legs pa dang rdo rje dbang phyug
gnyis byung ba gnyal phyogs su byon/ rgya mtsho grong mkhar btab/ gcung gi sras bla ma bya nag chen po rin cen 'od 'khrungs/ kha che paN chen dang mjal nas spyod rgyud
dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis zhus/ gzhan yang rgyal ba thog rdugs pa/ skyo 'od 'byung / 'jad rta mig pa sogs bla ma mang du bsten nas thos bsam sgom pa lhur bzhes mdzad/ khyad par
spu gri skor gsum sogs yi dam chos skyong la rtsal du thon pas yang rtse'i gtsug lag khang las kyang gnyan pa'i grags che/ 'di nyid kyis gtsug lag khang brtsigs dus stag
spre'u/ sho mong gsum bong tshod shing tu che ba'i cho 'phrul byung bas/ stag dang sho mong gnyis bsad pa'i sob kyang rtse'i mgon khang spyan gzigs khrod du yod skad/
spre'u de gsod thub na dbus gtsang spyi dang khyad par lho rgyud kyi mi bde ba'i rtsa ba zhi ba zhig 'ong rgyu yin kyang / 'gro ba'i las kyi mthus spre'u shor bas phyis su
sku rab tu byung / bla ma 'di la byar smad du tshal sgom chos la dga'/ lo rong rab dga' ba chen po/ dwags por ba tsho ras pa/ gtsang du 'u yug pa chen po ste chos kyi bu
bzhi/ gnyal du chos grwa grong mkhar/ er se po/ dwags su nags mo shod/ byar na rgya mtsho blug gang ste sde bzhi byung la/ rigs kyi sras bya jo sras/ de'i sras mnga' bdag
de la sras dge slong ba/ bya rin cen/ chos rgyal dpal

bzang gsum las/ dang po'i sras rin cen dpal/ dbang phyug rin cen/ rin cen bzang po/ dwags po ba bzhi byung / dwags gnyal lo ro rnams su gzhis ka mang du brtsigs/ bya rin cen
gyis e gnyal byar dwags lo ro rnams kyi sgo sdud mdzad nas hor dmag bzlog pas kun gyis dpon du bkur/'di'i sras kun dga' rin cen gyis sa skya'i dpon chen kun dga' bzang
po la gtugs/ bya chos rgyal dpal bzang pos 'gro mgon 'phags pa'i drung du byon/ shar pa kun bsod la slob dpon bcol nas rgyud gsum man ngag dang bcas pa sbyangs pa mdzad/
a mi bya nag gi dus la yang rtser mgon khang sogs yod pa'i steng du/ slar gtsug lag khang du grags pa'i mkhar las rgya bskyed/ rgya hor gyi nor sna mang po bsdus nas mdzod
nag tu rgyas btab/ rgyal ba'i bka' 'gyur gser las grub pa bzhengs/ chos srid kyis mtho ba'i 'go tshugs/ 'di'i sras kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen spyil pu ba/ mnga'
bdag chos seng 'od/ bya thub pa dpal rnams las/ dang pos dpon chen 'od zer seng ge la 'dam du rdzongs zhu bar byon/ rte'u ra'i gya gnyer kyang 'di'i ring la byung / mnga'
bdag chos seng 'od 'bri gung gi sku tsha yin par brten/ 'bri gung nas byar dwags kyi dpon du bskos/de'i sras mkhan chen tshul khrims bzang pos zangs mo che'i mkhan po mdzad/
slar yang rtser khri dpon gyi go sar byon/ de'i sras dkon cog bzang po/ de'i sras bkra shis dpal bzang gis rtses thang du slob gnyer mdzad/ bshad ston bzang po btang
/ gong ma sde srid grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis bya pa'i khri dpon la bskos/ de'i sras rgyal ba bkra shis/ shAkya dpal mgon/ thub pa rgyal mtshan rnams las/ dang pos sne'u
gdong rtser byon/ gong ma sde srid kyi drung 'khor mdzad/ bya pa khri dpon gyi go sar bskos/ sras bya bkra

shis dar rgyas/ padma rta mchog rgyal po/ bya tshe dbang rgyal po/ skal bzang chos kyi rgya mtsho/ bya nor bu rgya mtsho rnams 'khrungs/ gcung shAkya dpal mgon mkhan chen yon
tan dbang phyug la rab tu byung ste thos bsam sgom pa lhur blangs nas/ zangs mo cher mkhan thog tu bzhugs/skal bzang chos kyi rgya mtsho ni mdzad pa 'khrul med sogs bstan
bcos mang du mdzad cing / gsung rab la mkhas par grags/ bya bkra shis dar rgyas rtses thang nas dpon sa rdo rje rin cen dbang gi rgyal pos lho rgyud lung gi khri dpon
du bskos/ slar yang sne'u gdong rtse nas gong ma ngag gi dbang phyug gis bsko ja bzang po gya nom pa gnang / bya pa khri dpon gyi zhal ngo gcig la 'di nyid grags che zhing
/ chos rje karma pa rje drung chos grags rgya mtsho la mchog tu gus/ gser gyi bka' 'gyur gyis thog drangs sku gsung thugs kyi rten bzheng ba sogs rnam dkar gyi dge las
mang du mdzad/ 'di nyid kyis rdo rje gos dkar mo jo mor blangs pa'i sras/ bya nor bu bkra shis dang / grags pa rgyal mtshan mched gnyis 'khrungs shing / de yang rdo rje
gling pa'i lung bstan du/ gnyal lung pa rgyal po gcig gis 'bangs su sdud/ spyan ras gzigs kyi sprul pa'i sku zhig rgyal por 'byon zhes pa'i lung bstan du 'ga' zhig gleng
bar mched gnyis kyi nang nas 'brug pa sprul pa'i sku 'jam dbyangs chos grags pas sku tshe'i stod la yab yum gyi bka' nan bzhin rgyal srid bskyangs pa'i sras bstan 'dzin nor
bu dang / mtsho skyes rdo rje/ de'i sras gong ma chen po mi pham tshe'i dbang po dang / dmag dpon stag rdo rje/ de gnyis kyi sras karma tshe dbang grags pa dang / gangs
dkar rnam rgyal byung ngo // //! dga' ldan pa dmag dpon bsod nams rgyal po ni/ skyid shod yar phyogs gling zhes par/ mi chung don rgyal du grags pa des chos rgyal srong
btsan sgam po

blon po mgar gyi rigs las/ tre hos dga' bde bzang po zhes tshal pa khri dpon gyi go sar yod par de la gtugs/ dus 'gyur gyi dbang gis sde srid phag mo gru pa'i rdzong dpon gzhis
ka snel pa'i phyag g.yog mdzad/ nyang bran dga' ldan gyi mi dpon du bskos pas dga' ldan pa'i ming thogs/ de la sras bsod nams rgyal po/ dbang dar/ rnam sras gsum gyi
che ba snel pa dpal 'byor rgyal po'i thugs la btags pas/ dbyi nag bsod rgyal du grags shing / byang phyi chos lung dang yang dgon nang sor gtogs pa phud rjes/ klan ka gnyis
kas gtsos/ lo sbrel sna gdong phyin gyi 'ja' sa gnang / 'bring pos snams bon grong gi bdag po mdzad/ chung ba 'brong ri sngon rdzong du yod thog rin spungs pa'i dpung
gis bskor ba'i rgyogs nad la brten rdzong gtad nas tshal du mkhar las mdzad nas bzhugs/ dbyi nag bsod rgyal ba mched kyi sras nang so nam mkha' rgyal pos bar skabs chu shol
lhun po rtse bzung / 'on kyang snel pa nang zlos dus rin spungs pa'i dpung snye thang du 'byor thog chu shol gtad/nam mkha' rgyal po'i sras tshe brtan rgyal po dang /
bsod nams gnyis las/ che ba rab tu byung / chung ba la snel pa sku mched kyi dgongs par mi bde ba mang du byung bar brten/ rin spungs don yod rdo rjes dpung skyid shod du
bcug skabs/ rin sprungs par ngo gtad pa'i dmag gi sne bsu mdzad pas sne'u dang po ta la sogs rin spungs pa'i phyag tu 'byor ba'i lag rtags su rnying khung gi steng snye
mda' chu so kha yan gyi 'ja' sa gnang / de nas mi ring bar sde srid gong ma chen po'i dpung gzhung po rar phebs skabs/ yar rgyab rin cen bkra shis kyis 'tshams sbyar nas/
dga' shag gnyis kyis gong ma'i zhabs phyir 'brangs/ shag pa la skyor mo klung dang skyid shod g.yas ru'i ru dpon/

dga' ldan par bde chen du gtogs pa'i chu lho byang rnams dang / yar rgyab par sne'u'i rdzong dpon gyi las ka gnang / gong ma'i zhabs tog tu 'gyur bas bod yul gyi rdo rje gdan
'phrul snang gis gtsos skyid shod lung pa'i khrims bdag tu lung bud/ gtan khra shel tham gyis chod/'di nyid kyi sras ra nu lha bsrung gis gong ma chen po chu shol du bzhugs
skabs/ rin spungs pa'i dmag gis khang bcar bar ra nu lha bsrung gis gtsos pas kha spub che bar btang bas/ gong sa nas dmag dpon bsod nams rgyal po'i ming gnang / byi
ri stag rtse'i mi brgyud rdzogs rjes dga' ldan pa dang khyon sgril bar sras lcam sring drug 'khrungs pas gnyis chung ngu la grongs/ lcam tshe dbang rgyal mo 'phyong rgyas
hor bsod pa'i jo mo dang / lcam dung dkar sde srid kyi bdag mor bzhes/ de 'og nang so don grub rgyal pos gong sa nas rdzong dpon gyi las ka zhus/ mi ring bar sde srid
zhal ngo nang du sel zhugs skabs dga' ldan pa'i dbang gis skyor mo klung rdzong dmar 'bebs su btang / stod lung dang 'phan yul gyi rdzong mnga' zhabs phal cher blangs/ gong
sa nas chu shol mkhan chen por bka' bkyon gnang ba'i dpung gi rkangs mdzad nas chu shol 'bebs pa dang / gong dkar nas zhabs drung ngag dbang grags pa rtse'i khrir phebs
pa'i zhabs 'degs mdzad/gcung sde pa bkra shis rab brtan pas/ gong sar yar rgyab nas zhabs 'dren zhus skabs skyid shod kyi dpung rnams lho khar bton pa sogs sde srid kyi
zhabs tog tu 'gyur bar brten/ gzhis ka brag dkar gyi rdzong dpon gnang / skyid smad rnam rgyal sgang gi sgrub mchod gling mkhar du/ sne gdong yar rgyab sogs lho rgyud kyi
dpung rnams 'byor pa'i steng du/ sde pa bkra shis pa nyid kyis 'go mdzad nas mchongs pa dang / stod lung mtsho sna gdong du yar gong chu snyug

gnyal byar lor gsum/ lho brag dwags kong du rgyal bzang gi dpung zhib sgril byung ba bzlog thub pa sogs dgra thog tu mngon par lci ba'i dpa' grags kyis srin po'i rgyal po lang
ka mgrin bcu la skyengs pa ster nus/ dga' ldan dngul gdung rin po cher sgo rgyan/ 'phrul snang gtsug lag khang gi gser thog bzo ba/ rin cen sgang du rig pa'i dbang phyug
chos kyi grags pa'i ring lugs kyi bshad grwa 'dzugs pa sogs rnam dkar gyi mdzad pa'i zla snang gis legs byas puNDa ri ka'i tshal ches cher rgyas par mdzad cing / rigs
rus yon tan du mas mngon par mtho ba'i lha'i btsun pa bsod nams dpal bzang dang / mkhas pa'i dbang po shar pa chos rje nam mkha' rgyal mtshan sogs ti shrir bsten nas bkur
sti bla lhag tu mdzad/ thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i rig pa'i gnas mtha' dag la rnam dpyod kyi rtsa la rmad du byung ba'i yon tan dundu bhi'i sgra dbyangs skabs
gsum bdag po'i gnas su bsgrags so//'di nyid kyi sras sde pa g.yul rgyal nor bu lugs gnyis kyis mngon par mtho zhing sras bsod nams rnam rgyal/ yid bzhin nor bu chos rje gsum
las/ gcen gnyis kyis rtse nas gong ma'i lcam jo mor bsus pa'i sras mgon po rab brtan/ rdo rje rnam rgyal/ chos rje mtsho skyes rdo rje rnams byung ngo // smras pa/sde
bzhi'i dpal 'byor yongs 'du rlangs kyi ljon//gnam bskos rgyal srid yal 'dab stug po las//bsod nam dpung gis spyod pa'i mi bdag 'bras//mnga' 'bangs dga' ba'i 'dod rgu char
du phab//rigs rus bzang po'i nor 'dzin dbus//

stobs 'byor gser gyi 'dzin mas bskor//ya rabs rnam thar lhun po'i rtser//rgyal phran nye dbang tshogs kyi 'dus//chos srid blang dor gnas kun la//ma 'dres gzigs pa'i spyan stong
ldan//sde srid mchod sbyin brgya pa gang //srid 'dir mtho ba'i khri la 'gying //de ltar gong ma ta'i si tu nas bzung ste/ bod gnyan zhan gyi go rim sil bur ma gyur gyi
bar/ srid kyis mngon par mtho ba phal cher ni sde srid gong ma'i thugs la btags shing / lung dang las ka gnang ba shas che na'ang / sa skyong lha rgya ri ba ni/ gong sa
nas lung dang 'ja' sa ched du ma blangs par/ nyi 'og gi rgyal por gyur pa zhig ste/ de yang bod chos rgyal gyi gdung brgyud dri ma med pa gnam lde 'od srungs kyi sras mnga'
bdag dpal 'khor btsan gyi brgyud tsha ba khri bkra shis brtsegs pa'i sras gsum gyi 'od lde las rim par byung ba/ 'od skyid 'bar gyi sras gtsang tsha spun drug las brgyud
de/ gdan sa thel gyi mdar bcad po tsha ba rong pa zhes mi dpon zhig dpal phag mo gru pa rdo rje rgyal po'i dus byung zhing / de nas rim par brgyud nang so mda' smad
pas/ e stod chu tshan kha zhabs su ri la rtswa rgya bo skyes pa zhig na gzhis ka brtsigs pas rgya ri zhes ming du chags/de nas lha chos kyi bshes gnyen sogs zhal ngo rim
par byung ba las/ lha dgra las rnam rgyal gyis ri rdzong du bzhugs/ thams can mkhyen pa dge

'dun rgya mtsho dang mchod yon du 'brel/ rgya ri lcog mkhar du lo gar gtor chen gyi phyag srol btsugs/ lha dgra las pas e chen ri sgo phyogs su phebs pas/ yul du bkra shis
pa'i dge mtshan mang du byung bas/ yul mi rnams kyis nas phud khal re phul/ bla'i dpon du gyur te/ ri sge bkra shis chos rdzong du pho brang gi lte ba mdzad/ de nas lha 'jig
rten dbang phyug khri thog tu phebs rjes/ lha byams pa rab brtan dang / lha yul 'khor dbang phyug sku mched gnyis byung / 'di'i dus su sprul sku bde chen gling pas/ e
yi nang du khrag mtsho lan gsum khol/ / rgyal po byams pa'i ming can bya ba 'byung / / rgyal po de yi bstan pa rgyas pa la zhes sogs kyi don dang mthun par mnga' thang gong
du 'phel/ khyad par lha yul 'khor bas lang ka'i grong khyer sa la 'phos pa lta bu'i btsan rdzong 'ol kha stag rtse mnga' 'bangs dang bcas pa rang dbang du mdzad/de nas
lha bsod nams rab brtan sku mched gsum las/ bsod nams rab brtan khri thog tu phebs/ chad dkar rdzong gi nye 'dabs su dge 'dun gyi sde 'dzugs pa sogs rgyal srid chos bzhin
du bskyangs/ de rjes/ lha dga' ldan dpal 'bar gyis khrir phebs nas rgyal ba'i bstan pa spyi dang / khyad par chos kyi rgyal po btsong kha pa chen po'i bstan pa la sri
zhu bla lhag tu mdzad/ rog pa rtsar mi bsrun pa'i skye bo rang nyams gyi blo'i spyod yul can rnams ming gi lhag mar bcom pas mgo lag khrag gi ral pas sbags pa blangs pa sogs
'jigs pa med pa'i snying stobs kyis rnam par rgyal ba'i dbu rmog btsan po gyon/ de rjes khri thog tu blo bzang mthu stobs chos rgyal byon nas snying rje chen po'i gzhan
dbang gis sde 'khrug snyol ba gtso bor mdzad/ 'on kyang las ngan gyi rba klong drag pos bdas pa'i skye bo 'phar 'gro'i rigs can na kra'i mgrin par

'jug 'dod kyis tshur rgol gyi sde gzar 'ga' zhig byung ba rnams bka' khrims sgyur ba'i byed po bsod nams rab brtan sogs kyis zhi drag gi sbyor ba du mas bzlog par byas/ khri
chen 'di nyid ni rnam dkar dge ba'i las la mchog tu brtson zhing / khyad par gsang sngags zab mo'i rnal 'byor lhur mdzad do/ / de rjes lha ngag gi dbang phyug dga' ldan
rab tu brtan pa mi 'gyur rnam par rgyal ba khri thog tu byon te/ phun sum tshogs pa'i mnga' thang 'gog pa med pa'i snang ba rab tu rgyas so/ / smras pa/mchod sbyin brgya
yis 'chi med dbang po'i sar//skabs gsum rigs kyi bdag por dbang sgyur na//nor 'dzin chos bzhin skyong ba'i legs byas kyis//stong gsum kun kyang rang gir byas kyis dogs//e
ma khyod kyi sde bzhi'i nor//bsod nams gser gyi 'khor lo yis//drangs pa'i 'dzad med gan mdzod 'di//re ba skong ba'i dpag bsam dbang //de yang gnam bskos kyi rgyal po 'jam
dbyangs gong ma se chen gan gyi lung gis kha ba'i rdul mang yongs su brtsegs pa'i bod dang bod chen po'i rgyal khams mtha' dag dpal ldan sa skya pa la phul te/ gnam la
nyi zla zung gcig sa la mchod yon rnam gnyis zhes grags shing / de nas zla ba'i 'phreng ba bcu

phrag bdun gyi phyogs su nye ba na/ gang gis kyang gzhom gzhig nus pa'i go skabs phra mo tsam yang ring du spangs pa'i bsod nams kyi dpung pa can/ sa'i tshangs pa ta'i si tu
byang chub rgyal mtshan gyis gzhan dring mi 'jog pa'i dpa' mdzangs rtul phod pa'i rnam dpyod kyi bod yangs pa'i sa kun la dbang sgyur ba nas bzung / dus yun ring po'i bar
du dpal phag mo gru pa'i sde srid kyi bka' khrims gdugs dkar po gcig gis 'og tu khyab tshul sngon du brjod ma thag pa de lta na'ang / zhabs drung gong ma chen po zhing
khams gzhan du 'pho ba'i tshul bstan pa'i mjug tu/ phag gru'i mtshan don mi rgyug pa dang / glo bur gyi rgyal po zhig 'byung ba sogs dus 'grig pas/ 'phreng mgo gter ston
shes rab 'od zer gyi thugs rje chen po padma'i dbang phyug gi lung bstan du/ sgra snyan 'dra ba'i gnas sgo ru: 'jig rten dbang phyug sprul pa nyid: ar tha'i ming mdzin byung
gyur na: lho byang glo bur rgyal po byed: sgrub pa snying po'i bstan pa 'dzugs: mi lo lnga bcur bde la 'god: skye ba'i rten 'brel ma 'grig na: yul de rang 'pho gud pa
dang : mtha' ma rlung gis 'khyer du nye: zhes sde pa 'phreng mgo ba'i mi ngo zhig gis glo bur gyi rgyal po byed pa'i lung bstan dang / gnang rtse nas kyi gsang ba'i lung
bstan du/ gtsang phyogs rgyal po padma'i ming can 'byung : sku tshe mthar phyin bdud dbang ma gyur na: zhes pa lhad bcug pa min na rin spungs pa'i sras padma dkar pos bod
spyi'i rgyal po byed par bshad pa sogs ni rten 'brel 'phyugs pas thog tu ma phebs la/ padma'i rgyal tshab mnga' ris paN chen dang rigs 'dzin legs ldan pa'i bla ma bka'
brgyud yongs 'dus kyi lung bstan du/'dzam gling shar lho'i phyogs mtshams su:bdud mo rno myur nag mo la: bu dgu skyes nas 'dzam gling 'joms:khyad par bod yul gangs can 'dir:ma
'ongs bzhi bcur

nye dus su:bdud sprul dgu dang de blon dgu:btsan mo phyi nang las byed dgu:bang 'phrin dbu gtso dmag dpon dgu:dgu dgu brgyad cu rtsa gcig gis:'gro kun kha lo thur du 'khrid:ces
pa'i dus rtags thog tu khel te/ rin spungs pa'i blon po zhig gis bsam 'grub rtse'i rdzong dpon gyi thog snar thang pa/ nor khyung pa/ brgya tsho ba sogs lho byang gi
dpon rigs mang po dang 'brel btags byas pa'i sde pa rong par 'bangs gyen log gis/ sde gzar lan snga phyi kha yar du byung ba'i mthar je 'phel du song ste/ gtsang stod rgyal
po'i lung gis dbus gtsang mtha' dag rim gyis chab 'og tu bcug pa'i mnga' thang gi dpal phun sum tshogs pa dag ji ltar nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor seng ge mo'i bu'i mgrin par
chud pa ltar/ mnga' 'bangs mtha' dag cig car du rang gir 'dzin pa'i byed po ni/ rtsod dus kyi 'khor los sgyur ba bstan 'dzin chos kyi rgyal po ste/ 'di nyid ni/ gter ston
dri med lhun po'i lung bstan las/ spyir yang mtha' dmag lan bdun mtha' ma la: badzra pA Ni'i sprul pa'i rgyal po zhig: bod khams dar cig bde la sbyor ba 'byung : zhes gsang
ba'i bdag po phyag na rdo rje mi'i srid pa'i zlos gar can yin par lung gis zin pas/ byang sems 'phags pa snying rje dang smon lam gyi dbang gis 'gro ba'i don du bsams
bzhin chos ldan rgyal por skye ba bzung bas phan bde'i 'od brgya phyogs bcur 'gyed pa ste/ gang zhig tha mal gyi skye bo rang nyams kyis spyod pa'i snang tshul gyi mun
pa mtha' dag rgyang du bsrings pa ni gor ma chag la/de yang byang phyogs hor sog gi rgyal khams na sde chen po grangs med pa yod pa'i ya gyal/ o rod tsho ba bzhir grags pa'i
nang tshan/ ho shod kyi dpon po ha na'i la jo mo a ha'i ha thun blangs par sras lnga byung ba'i gsum pa

rgyal po 'di nyid chu pho rta'i lo la 'khrungs/ mtshan tho rol pa'i hur btags so/ / dgung lo bcu gsum lon pa'i tshe/ mgo dkar gyi dmag khri phrag tsam gyi steng du/ dmag rnams
kyi sna drangs te mchongs pas pha rol gyi dpung tshogs mtha' dag 'jig brten phyi ma'i ltad mo dus gcig tu myong bar byas pa'i grags pas/ srin po'i rgyal po lang ka mgrin
bcu mi'i yul du rgyu ba'i 'gran zla gnyis pa byas so/ / de skabs yul phyogs de dag mtha' 'khob las kyang ches mtha' 'khob tu gyur pa kla klo'i rgyal khams lta bur gnas
pa las/ sog po'i yul gru gzhan dag tu/ thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgya mtsho dang / gser gyi rgyal po mchod yon zung gcig la brten nas dam pa'i chos dar zhes pa'i chos
kyi ming tsam thos 'dzin gyi rgyan du gyur pas yid dga' spro dang bcas te phyogs der phyag btsal bas dpral ba skrangs pa tsam du gyur cing / bstan pa'i dbu brnyes pa ni/
lha tho ri gnyan shal la gnyan po gsang ba byung ba bzhin no/ / me rta dgung lo nyer lngar slebs pa'i tshe/ yum grongs pa'i rkyen gyis mkho dgu'i 'byor pa mtha' dag mchog
dman gyis skye bo rnams la sbyin par btang zhing / de yang tshe 'di'i snyan grags dang / rnam smin lan la re ba tsam ma yin par/ slob dpon zla grags kyis/ sbyin pa sbyin
bya len po gtong pos gtong zhes gsungs pa ltar/ 'khor gsum bden stong gi rtsis zin pa'i 'phags chen dam pa'i rnam thar ro/ / byang 'phags rnams ni gzhan don du 'gyur
tshe dmyal ba'i me 'obs kyang mtho ris kyi dga' ba'i tshal bzhin du 'jug par mdzad pa ni chos nyid de/ de skabs khar kha dang o rod phan tshun du g.yul rlabs po che bshams
pa'i 'khrug long gis/ srog gcod pa'i sdig pa'i las rngam po ches/ ngan song mu mtha' med pa'i nags klung stug por bskyur ba'i sbyor ba la brtson pa dag la dmigs pa med
pa'i snying rje chen po'i gzhan dbang

du gyur te/ khar kha o rod phan tshun du 'grul tsam yang byed mi nus pa'i skabs/ bdag gzhan brje ba'i snying stobs kyi go cha btsan po gyon te/ khar kha'i khrod du tsham tshom
med par byon nas/ gzhung dka' tshegs chung ngus bzlums par mdzad pa dge legs pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa lta bu'i rnam thar ro/ / stong 'khor chos rje dang khar kha'i rgyal
blon rnams yi rangs te/ da'i gu shri zhes cho lo byin/ slar rang yul du byon/ rje bsod nams rgya mtsho la o rod cig gis mdo sde gser 'od dam pa la phyag nas zhus pa'i
tshe/ gsung rab kyi ming dri ba gnang bar/ al tan ge ril zer zhus pas/ da nas mi lo nyi shu na khyod kyi yul du chos 'di dar bar 'gyur ro zhes lung bstan pa ltar/ gser 'od
dam pa sogs chos mang du sgyur ba'i sbyin bdag mdzad pa sogs bstan pa'i srol btod pa ni/ chos skyong ba'i rgyal po srong btsan sgam po gnyis pa sa 'dir 'ongs so zhes lha
rnams gleng ngo //sngar sog po tsho chen drug la gzhung dang chings yod pa rnams cha dkar rgyal pos bshig pa'i dus 'khrug la brten/ bros po 'ga' zhig khar kha'i khrod
du 'ongs par/ dpon po nang phan tshun rtsod pa'i rkyen gyis/ khar kha chog thu rang yul nas spyugs te mtsho khar 'ongs pa/ sdig can gyi yul du rin po che'i char bab pa'i
gtam rgyud ltar/ re zhig mnga' thang che bar byung bas/ nag po'i gdon gyis yid rnam par brlams pas/ bstan pa spyi dang khyad par rgyal ba btsong kha pa'i bstan pa la log
par 'khu ba'i bsam sbyor ngan pa nyams su bstar ba la brten/ rgyal po 'di nyid kyis bstan pa 'ba' zhig thugs su bcug pa'i/ rang yul nas dmag gi dpung tshogs dang chabs gcig
par bteg pa/ me glang zla ba dang por mtsho khar 'byor te/ stobs ldan gyi rgyal po rA ma Nas lang ka'i bdag po lnga pa'i lam du btang ba bzhin chog thu'i dmag

khri phrag bzhi dang bcas pa ming gi lhag mar btang / shar phyogs rgya mtsho'i mtha' tshun mnga' 'og tu bsdus te chos srid gnyis ldan gyi sgo nas mnga' 'bangs rnams bde bar
bskyangs/ rim gyis nyi ma dbus kyi rgyal khams su byon/ bsod nams kyi tshogs rgya cher spel ba'i dga' ston bsgrubs/ bod yul gyi rdo rje gdan ra sa 'phrul snang gi gtsug
lag khang du/ rgyal phran kun gyi cod pan du bgrod byed zung nye bar 'god pa'i ngal sor mdzad pa'i chos kyi rgyal po chen po'i mtshan dang las ka sogs mngon par blangs te/
phyir lam gdan sa chen po dga' ldan rnam par rgyal ba'i gling du phebs/ de dgongs nyer bdun yin na'ang / srod kyi dus rde'u phra mo tsam yang mthong ba'i mun pa shin tu
dkar ba byung bas/ bstan srid mtha' dag dkar 'jam du 'gyur ba'i rten 'brel 'grig de skabs bod dang bod chen po mtha' dag mnga' 'og tu chug pa'i mtshan ltas legs pa'ang 'ga'
zhig byung 'dug glang lo'i dgun thog mtsho kar phyir byon/ de yang bar khams su be ri don yod kyis/ kun mkhyen bu ram shing pa'i rjes su zhugs pa mtha' dag la nye bar
'tshe zhing / bon kho na spel ba la brten/ sa yos hor zla lnga pa'i nang du be ri'i thog tu dpung tshogs rnams bteg mnga' 'bangs phal cher blangs/ lcags 'brug zla ba bcu
gcig pa'i nyer lnga la/ be ri dpon po sogs mtha' btsan por bros pa rnams kyang / gang gis bsod nams kyi lcags kyu rnon pos/ khab len rdo ba dang lcags phye'i snang tshul
ltar khrims kyi do ra chen por yongs su bcug mi bde ba'i rtsa rkyen mtha' dag gnas nas dbyung / sa dge/ kar 'brug stag lung pa sogs kyi bla dpon khrims dong du tshud pa
rnams bton te rang gnas su bskyal/ 'jang rgyal po tshun chad kyi skye rgu rnams kyis nor gyi dpya khral phul zhing gus 'dud lhur blangs/ de nas dbus gtsang gi phyogs su dpung
gi

tshogs bshams par mngon du phyogs pa ni/ mnga' ris sku mched kyi gter lung du/khyad par gdug pa sbrul gyi lo shar dus:gnam rtags 'od dkar skya rengs yang yang shar:gza' skar
'khrug cing byang du hor sog g.yo:'ol kha'i phyogs su rkyen byas 'khrug:dbus gtsang sde 'khrug 'gro rnams nyam thag 'gyur:sa g.yos nad rims lo gsum lo nyes 'byung :lo dgu'i
bar du dbus gtsang dbu rur 'tshogs:khrag gi char pa lo bdun bar du 'bab:ces dang / yol mo sprul sku'i gter gsar du/yos kyi lo la ngal so byed:'brug gi lo la 'brug ltar
lding :sbrul la sbrul shun bzhin du 'thor: de phyir yos bu'i lo la long :zhes pa'i dus rtags dang mtshungs par dpung tshogs bye ba phrag brgya'i g.yul bshams te/ lho phyogs
gshin rje'i mthar thug pa tshun dbang du bsdus/ chu rta zla ba gnyis pa'i nyer lnga la/ bod shing sgo can yongs kyi rgyal blon rnams kyang nga rgyal gyi gdong pa smad
de gus 'dud lhur len gyi sbyor ba la nye bar zhugs/ chu shel gyi dbang po nag pas nya ba/ dus 'khor ba'i lo'i thog ma'i dus tshes nas bod chol ka gsum gyi rgyal por gyur
te/ bka' khrims kyi gdugs dkar po srid rtse'i bar du 'khor/ ris bral gyi grub pa'i mtha' rnams la gus 'dud lhur len gyi lhag pa'i bsam pa mnga' na'ang / kar srid rnams
kyi byed spyod ma mkhas par brten/ shar phyogs kong po'i yul tshun dpung shed kyi spyad/ gter ston 'ja' tshon pas rang gter du slob dpon chen po'i sprul par bstan yod ces
ngos bzung / rgya gar gyi rgyal po kho shing / bal yul yam bu'i rgyal po/ mnga' ris rgyal po sogs mtha'i rgyal po mang pos kyang / yul lugs kyi skyes mang du phul/ de yar
ratna'i bstan pa spyi lung du/'bri yi rwa co phag gi mjug ma can:gung gi tshang 'cha' sa yis zas za zhing :zhes pa'i 'og tu/dbus gtsang thams cad sku yi mnga' 'og

'du:de lta'i bstan pa mi lo drug cu 'byung :zhes pa 'bri gung pa dang phag gru'i bstan pa g.yag tsam las rwa co dang mjug ma lus pa'i tshod tsam gyi dus rtags dang gnas tshad
bstan no/ / de yang rgyal ba btsong kha pa chen po'i thugs rje'i bdud rtsi gang gi gsang ba gsum gyi za ma tog tu bltams pas chos srid mtha' dag gser gyi 'khor los sgyur
ba'i rgyal po'i dpal la 'gran pa 'di bzhin no/ / smras pa/dbyangs gsal sdeb kyis sra bar bcings pa'i lcags ri'i khor yug dbus na mngon mtho glegs bu'i rin cen rdul mang
brtsegs pa'i ba gam na//'gal ba'i khur mang gya gyu'i tshul spangs legs bshad khams kyi dwangs ma kun bsdus tshar du dngar ba'i deb ther ri dwags mig can ma//nyams 'gyur
'jo sgeg gar gyi rnam rol bcad lhug spel ma'i dbyangs bdun lhur len tshig don ma 'dres zur mig dbang gzhu ltar 'khyug cing //mngon brjod u dum wA ra'i 'phreng mdzes gtam
rgyud mgo skyes g.yon 'phyang ma 'di blo ldan brgya byin dag las gzhan gyi spyod yul min//ka raNDa ltar ya rabs mchog gi spyod tshul snod du ca co'i ngag spangs khungs
ldan lo rgyus dbus 'gyur ta la'i glegs bam ji bzhin rab gsal pa ri dzrA yi pusta ka//kha dog tshig don ma 'dres lang tsho rnam par bkra ba'i cha shas

yongs rdzogs snyan tshig bsil zer mdangs kyi tha gru kun khyab sgra 'dzin bdud rtsis pha rol shes ldan dga' ston che//ga dza lha bu'i dregs pa'i blun po legs bshad skyes las
ja chang btung ba 'ba' zhig don du gnyer phyir da lta'i dus kyi snang tshul 'di la ba glang spyod las gzhan mi brin//nga zhes stobs nor snyems pas 'gying yang shes ldan
rig pa'i nya gar gzhal tshe lci dang yang ba'i mtha' bral na ra'i dbus na g.yung por mthong bas ma dmad 'gro ba shin tu dkon//tsa ko ra yi lus 'degs blo yis shes bya'i mkha'
la bgrod tshe zha bo ji bzhin mthu dang bral yang ra gan gser gyi zol can 'ga' zhig gis//tsha zer la sogs grang dro'i 'jigs pa khyad bsad bsgrubs rnams gtan bde za bar
byed pa gor ma chag mod la lar 'di snang rnam dpyod tshul dang bral//dza Ta'i cod pan chos rgyal med dbon 'khon rigs rlangs sogs grags snyan 'a 'ud srid pa'i rtse mo kun
tu sha shi'i 'od 'dzin blo gsal tshogs rnams kyis//wa ler sgrog 'dod sems kyis bskul bas bsngags brjod rgyud mang glu blangs ya mtshan dpal gyis skabs gsum pa rnams sa
la blta phyir rgyu skar zol gyis lhags//ha cang sa chen skyong ba'i chos ldan rgyal po a shwattha yi ljon pa'i dbang po dar ba'i mchog/ha ri tsan dan dpung pa skyes kyi
dbus mtho a ga ru yi rgyal phran kun gyis zla bral ba//ha ri ka yi mgrin dbyangs khrims gnyis nga ros a mra'i yongs

'du mnga' 'bangs yongs kyi 'dab ma 'dzum//ha har bzhad pa'i phul byung dga' ston bzang pos a mri ta yi snying po'i zil dngar bla na med//srid zhi'i khams kyi lha lam yangs
pa'i ngos//rgyal dbang ye shes sgyu ma'i 'od dkar can//bsil ldan chu snod so sor shar ba las//bka' khrims dge ba'i bcu drug cha shas rdzogs//gang can kun gsal mdzes ma'i
bzhin ras la//thub bstan nam mkha'i sgron me'i spyan gyi dkyus//lung rtogs khyog pa'i snang mdzod lcags kyu yis//phan bde'i 'od dkar gzhon nu ring nas 'gugs//srong btsan
dge bcu'i legs lam zla tshes can//log spyod ra ri'i dri ma phyung ba'i 'od//grags snyan ral par spud tshe mgrin sngon can//sa bla'i ljongs su song zhes lha rnams gleng //yid
srubs kyis brlams sdig lta'i sems 'chang rigs//legs byas snang ba 'gog tshe khri srong lhas//thabs mkhas 'phrul gyis spel bas dge legs 'od//spur rgyal yangs pa'i sa la
kun tu 'bar//ral pa'i zur phud bla brer bres pa'i mkhar//thun mtshams lang tsho'i sde yis legs 'khyud pas//bdud sde'i rgyal mtshan nags kyi me khyer dag/

gangs ldan ra ba'i ngos las phyi rol brgal//ma rig stug por 'phyan byed dgra sde'i lhar//mngon par 'khon pa'i bdud rtsi bod yul zong //'thungs pas chos srid bdag po sa skya
pa//stobs ldan sgra gcan gnyis pa sa 'dir snang //rin cen bdun gyi 'dod rgur mnga' sgyur ba'i//sa dbang rgyal po'i go sar gnam gyi mthongs//sgo 'phar yangs pa'i spo nas
bum bzang gis//spyi bor dbang bskur sde srid phag mo gru//e ma sngon byon sa spyod lha rnams kyis//bod 'bangs 'dab brgya bzhad pa'i phan bde'i 'od//spros tshe nyin byed bdag
gis ci bya zhes//gnod sbyin phyogs kyi 'khrig pa'i khyim du bros//khrims gnyis srab kyis ma gcun rengs pa'i gnyar//drang thig 'dzam bu gser gyi 'khor lo yis//mnan tshe
ngan spyod skye bo'i bag yangs kun//bkres skom gdung bas mnar lus ji bzhin snyam//brnag nus las 'das pha rol rgol ba'i g.yul//rnam par bcom pa'i mgo 'phreng khrag gis brlan//lan
gcig min par gsher ba'i dmar 'od kyi//rgod ma kha de rgya mtsho'i mtha' ru yibs//

gser mngal stobs la rmugs 'dzin 'byor pa'i mdzod//gcig tu bsdus 'dra'i srid kun dge phyogs su//bsgyur bas rnam smin dkar po'i thigs pa 'bum//'dzag byed dam pa'i spyod tshul
rmad du byung //mthon po'i mnga' thang phun tshogs dpal 'byor kun//bkod pas khyad 'phags rnam dpyod dbyar rnga'i sgras//che ba'i rnam thar bzang po'i gtsug phud can//ya
rabs dga' ston rnam bkra'i gshog rlabs ngom//kye ma thos bsam bdud rtsi yal bor nas//ngan g.yo zang zing rnyogs pa'i bza' btung gis//lto ba khengs pa'i dregs ldan mthon po'i
khrir//'dzegs kyang tha ga pa dang khyad par ci//ya rabs tshal du rigs rus cho 'brang gi/yongs 'du'i ljon pa rgyas pa rmad byung yang //che ldan bya ba'i spyod tshul
mi shes na//gser skyogs snod du ngan skyugs blug dang mtshungs//mkhas dang grub pa'i skye bar khas 'che nas//'chad rtsod rtsom pa'i blo gros mthu dman na//gnod sbyin nor
la spyod pa tshe 'phos nas//dbul po'i khyim du skyes dang khyad par ci//mi 'dzad stobs 'byor gter la mnga' bsgyur yang //

'di phyi'i phun tshogs bsgrub pa'i rnam dpyod mig/longs tshe sa 'og gnas pa'i klu tshogs dang //srang la bteg tshe lci yang gang gis 'byed//khungs ldan lo rgyus mthong bar
rigs lam nas//'dren pa'i rnam 'byed shes rab mthu phra yang //dmus long gcig pur rgyu ba'i gom stabs bzhin//'gal 'du'i khur gyis lci ba'i glegs bam mang //lo rgyus gzhu la
drang po'i rgyud drangs nas//legs bshad 'dab ldan g.yo ba'i nyag phran can//mi shes rmongs pa'i snying la phog srid kyang //gzur gnas mkhas pas mthong tshe spro ba 'phel//mi
mjed zhing gi gangs ri'i spo la sde bzhi'i rtsal gsum yongs su rdzogs pa'i mtho ris rgyal po gdong lnga'i dbang //rim par byon la bsngags tshig swa sti'i sgra yi gdub
sil 'khrol bas ya rabs mdun sa'i kha rgyan spel legs 'di//shes bya'i rba klongs yid mtshor rol pa'i bande tshangs dbang sras mos bzhad pa'i 'dzum ldan legs bshad gter
mdzod kyis//mi bdag gsung gi ri bo man dha ra yis bskul ltar dpyad gsum dag pa'i 'chi med lus phra'i padmo bskrun//gangs can 'dzin ma'i dpyid kyi mngal khur las//blo gros
yal 'dab dar ba'i shes ldan rnams//ngo mtshar gtam gyi legs bshad skyes 'dod na//

deb ther dpyid kyi rgyal mo'i dbyangs 'di bsten//thub bstan kun gsal mdzes ma'i khor yug tu//rung mthun gos kyis thun mtshams zol bsten nas//nges gsang theg pa'i yang rtse
sngo skyes 'bras//yongs smin gang bu rgyas pa'i g.yur za ldem//de lta na yang nges pa lnga ldan gzugs//bshes gnyen dam pa'i A daRsha yi ngos//zlos gar bsgyur ba'i drin las
rig pa'i gnas//smra tshe dbyangs can dgyes pa'i 'dzum gyis bsu//lhag bsam rab dkar dri bral yid kyi mkhar//bstan bcos chu lha'i bu yi pusta kas//skye rgu'i nyon mongs 'du
ba 'khrugs pa'i nad//legs bshad chu klung dwangs pos drungs 'byin cing //'dzam bu'i lang tsho dar babs 'khri shing gis//nyer mtshon yangs pa'i nor 'dzin skyong ba kun//rtsub
'gyur dpal gyi rno ngar rab zhi nas//dge bcu'i khrims kyis rdzogs ldan 'bod par shog/phan bde'i gdugs dkar srid pa'i rtse mo'i bar//khor yug gcig tu khyab pa'i legs
pa'i lam//stobs bcu'i rtsal 'chang ring lugs snying po'i brgyud//'gro ba'i bsod nams zhing du 'bar gyur cig/ces gangs ris bskor ba'i ljongs su mchog gsum dam par gtan gyi
skyabs

su 'dzin cing / rnam 'dren zas gtsang sras po'i bstan pa rin po che la phud dud sogs bla na med par bkur ba'i sa la spyod pa'i mtho ris kyi rgyal blon rnams gtso bor brjod
pa'i deb ther rdzogs ldan gzhon nu'i dga' ston dpyid kyi rgyal mo'i glu dbyangs zhes bya ba 'di yang / stobs kyi dbang phyug bstan 'dzin chos kyi rgyal po'i bkas bskul bar
brten/ bka' chems bka' khol ma/ thugs rje chen po'i skor/ mkhas pa'i dbang po 'gos lo gzhon nu dpal dang / tshal pa'i deb ther sogs khungs thub kyi yig tshang rnams la
zhib mor dpyad/ mkhas rlom dregs ldan gyi khungs med blun tshig gi glegs bam rnams la dgag gzhag cung zad bgyis te/ snyigs dus kyi rgyal ba gnyis pa btsong kha pa'i bstan
la zhugs pas rgyu mtshan shes nas mi ldog pa'i dad pa thob kyang / 'thad ldan gyi grub pa'i mtha' rnams la chos spong gi sgrib pas ma sbags shing / bcu phrag gi rig pa'i
gnas la blo gros kyi 'jug pa cung zad shar ba'i za hor gyi rigs las lo rgyus smra ba'i btsun pa ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho/ ming gzhan tshangs sras bzhad pa'i rdo rje
'jigs med go cha thub bstan lang tsho gsar pa'i sdes/ 'gro ba'i bla ma shAkya seng ge drag po zhes pa lcags sprel lor bltams nas lo nyis stong drug brgya dang nyag ma
gsum 'das pa/ 'phags pa'i yul du sUraya zhes pa gangs can gyi ljongs 'dir nyi mar grags shing / mahA tsi na'i rgyal khams su dbang thang dang bstun pa'i skad gu'i wu'i/ phyogs
'dir chu mo lug tu brjod pa'i glu dbyangs kyi zla ba'i phyogs snga ma'i rgyal ba dang po'i tshes la/ sman ljongs sa'i lte ba dga' ldan pho brang me tog mngon par bkra
ba'i lding khang du sbyar ba'i yi ge pa ni ngag dbang dge legs so// // mangga laM//
